 <hr>
  <h3 align="center">Xhosa Bible: Psalms</h3> 
 <p><a name="an_1:1">1:1</a> Hayi, uyolo lomntu ongahambiyo ngecebo labangendawo,  Ongemiyo endleleni yaboni, Ongahlaliyo embuthweni yabagxeki!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:2">1:2</a> Yena unonelela umyalelo kaYehova; Ucamanga ngomyalelo wakhe imini nobusuku:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:3">1:3</a> Unjengomthi omiliselwe phezu kwemijelo yamanzi, Onika isiqhamo sawo ngexesha lawo, Ogqabi lawo lingabuniyo; Konke akwenzayo kophumelela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:4">1:4</a> Abanjalo abangendawo; Bona banjengomququ ophetshethwa ngumoya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:5">1:5</a> Ngenxa yoko abangendawo abanakuma emgwebeni, Naboni ebandleni lamalungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:6">1:6</a> Ngokuba uYehova uyayazi indlela yamalungisa; Ke yona indlela yabangendawo iya kudaka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:1">2:1</a> Yini na ukuba iintlanga zenze imbuthumbuthu, Izizwe zicamange into engeyakonto?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:2">2:2</a> Ookumkani behlabathi bazimisile, Izidwangube zabhunga NgoYehova nangoMthanjiswa wakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:3">2:3</a> Besithi, Masiziqhawule iimbophelelo zabo, Sizilahle izintya zabo kuthi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:4">2:4</a> Ohleli emazulwini uyahleka, INkosi iyabagculela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:5">2:5</a> Iya kwandula ithethe kubo ngomsindo wayo, Ibakhwankqise ngokuvutha kwayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:6">2:6</a> Ithi, Mna ke ndimmisile ukumkani wam Phezu kweZiyon, intaba yam engcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:7">2:7</a> Athi yena, Ndiya kuwuvakalisa ummiselo: UYehova uthe kum,  UnguNyana wam wena; Mna namhla ndikuzele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:8">2:8</a> Cela kum, ndikunike iintlanga zibe lilifa lakho, Iziphelo zehlabathi zibe zezakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:9">2:9</a> Uya kuzivikiva ngentonga yentsimbi, Uzihlekeze, zinge zizitya zodongwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:10">2:10</a> Ngoko ke, nina bokumkani, qiqani; Bagwebi basehlabathini,  yalekani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:11">2:11</a> Mkhonzeni uYehova nisoyika, Gcobani nithuthumela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:12">2:12</a> Mangeni uNyana, hleze aqumbe, nitshabalale endleleni,  Ngokuba ungahle uvuthe umsindo wakhe. Hayi, uyolo lwabo bonke abazimela ngaye!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:1">3:1</a> Umhobe kaDavide, ekubalekeni kwakhe kuAbhisalom unyana wakhe. Yehova, hayi, ukuba baninzi kwabandibandezelayo!  Baninzi abasukela phezulu kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:2">3:2</a> Baninzi abathi kumphefumlo wam, Akunalusindiso kuThixo.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:3">3:3</a> Ke wena, Yehova, uyingweletshetshe kum, Uluzuko lwam,  umphakamisi wentloko yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:4">3:4</a> Ndidanduluka kuYehova ngezwi lam, Andiphendule entabeni yakhe engcwele. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:5">3:5</a> Ndalala phantsi, ndalala ubuthongo; Ndavuka, ngokuba uYehova endixhasa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:6">3:6</a> Andizoyiki izigidi zabantu Abakhe uluhlu lokulwa ngeenxa zonke kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:7">3:7</a> Khawusuk ume, Yehova; ndisindise, Thixo wam; Ngokuba uzibetha zonke iintshaba zam emhlathini; Amazinyo abangendawo uyawaphula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:8">3:8</a> Usindiso lolukaYehova: Mayibe phezu kwabantu bakho intsikelelo yakho. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:1">4:1</a> Kumongameli wokubethelwa izinto ezineentambo. Umhobe kaDavide. Ekudandulukeni kwam ndiphendule, Thixo wobulungisa bam; Embandezelweni yam wandenzela indawo ebanzi; Ndibabale,  uwuve umthandazo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:2">4:2</a> Nina, nyana babantu, kunini na uzuko lwam niluhlazisa,  Ningxamele into engeyakonto, nithanda amanga? (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:3">4:3</a> Yazini ke ukuba uYehova uzibalulele owenceba; UYehova uyaphulaphula ndakudanduluka kuye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:4">4:4</a> Qumbani, ningoni; Thethani neentliziyo zenu ezinkukweni zenu, nithi cwaka. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:5">4:5</a> Bingelelani imibingelelo yobulungisa, Nikholose ngoYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:6">4:6</a> Baninzi abathi, Ngubani na owosibonisa okulungileyo?  Siphakamisele ukukhanya kobuso bakho, Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:7">4:7</a> Uyivuyisile intliziyo yam, Kunexesha lobuninzi bengqolowa yabo, newayini yabo entsha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:8">4:8</a> Ndiya kulala phantsi, ndilale ubuthongo kwangoku, ndixolile,  Ngokuba wena, Yehova, undihlalisa ndikholosile, noko ndindedwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:1">5:1</a> Kumongameli: ngogwali. Umhobe kaDavide. Wabekele indlebe amazwi am, Yehova, Kuqonde ukucamanga kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:2">5:2</a> Libazele indlebe izwi lokuzibika kwam, Kumkani wam, Thixo wam; Ngokuba ndithandaza kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:3">5:3</a> Yehova, uya kuliva izwi lam kwakusasa, Kwakusasa ndiya kuwusingisa kuwe umthandazo wam, ndibonisele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:4">5:4</a> Ngokuba wena akunguThixo onanze okungendawo,  Akanakuphambukela kuwe onobubi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:5">5:5</a> Abanakuma abaqhayisi phambi kwamehlo akho; Uyabathiya bonke abasebenzi bobutshinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:6">5:6</a> Uyabatshabalalisa abathetha amanga; Indoda enegazi nenkohliso ilisikizi kuYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:7">5:7</a> Ke mna, ndinokungena endlwini yakho ngenceba yakho eninzi,  Ndiqubude, ndibhekise etempileni yakho engcwele ngokukoyika.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:8">5:8</a> Yehova, ndikhaphe ngobulungisa bakho ngenxa yabandilaleleyo;  Yilungelelanise indlela yakho phambi kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:9">5:9</a> Ngokuba emlonyeni wabo akukho nto imiyo, Umbilini wabo ngumeyeliselo; Lingcwaba elivuliweyo umqala wabo; Bathetha okugudileyo ngolwimi lwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:10">5:10</a> Bathwalise ityala, Thixo; Makatshitshe amaqhinga abo;  Elukreqweni lwabo oluninzi batyhale, Ngokuba bakuphikisile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:11">5:11</a> Mabavuye bonke abazimela ngawe, Bamemelele ngonaphakade,  ubakhusele; Badlamke ngawe abalithandayo igama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:12">5:12</a> Ngokuba wena uyalisikelela ilungisa, Yehova,  Ulihlanganisele ngenkoliseko njengekhaka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:1">6:1</a> Kumongameli wokubethelwa izinto ezineentambo: ngelamadoda ilizwi. Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, musa ukundohlwaya unomsindo,  Ungandithethisi unobushushu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:2">6:2</a> Ndibabale, Yehova, ngokuba ndintshwenyile; Ndiphilise,  Yehova, ngokuba ekhwankqisiwe amathambo am.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:3">6:3</a> Umphefumlo wam ukhwankqiswe kakhulu; Ke wena, Yehova, koda kube nini na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:4">6:4</a> Buya, Yehova, uwuhlangule umphefumlo wam; Ndisindise ngenxa yenceba yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:5">6:5</a> Ngokuba ekufeni akusekho kukukhumbula; Kwelabafileyo ngubani na osenokubulela kuwe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:6">6:6</a> Ndidiniwe kukugcuma kwam; Ndiludadisa ubusuku bonke ukhuko lwam, Ndiwenza manzi umandlalo wam ngeenyembezi zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:7">6:7</a> Lonakele kukukhathazeka iliso lam; Laluphele ngenxa yababandezeli bam bonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:8">6:8</a> Sukani kum, nina nonke basebenzi bobutshinga; Ngokuba uYehova ulivile ilizwi lokulila kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:9">6:9</a> Ukuvile uYehova ukutarhuzisa kwam; UYehova umthandazo wam uyawamkela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:10">6:10</a> Ziya kudana, zikhwankqe kakhulu, zonke iintshaba zam; Ziya kubuyiswa zidanile ngephanyazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:1">7:1</a> Ishigayon kaDavide, awayivumayo kuYehova ngenxa yamazwi kaKushi, umBhenjamin. Yehova, Thixo wam, ndizimela ngawe;  Ndisindise kubo bonke abandisukelayo, undihlangule,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:2">7:2</a> Hleze bawuqwenge njengengonyama umphefumlo wam, Bawudlavule,  kungekho mhlanguli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:3">7:3</a> Yehova, Thixo wam, ukuba ndithe ndenza oku, Ukuba kukho ubugqwetha ezandleni zam,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:4">7:4</a> Ukuba ndimphethe kakubi obexolelene nam, Ndambhunyula ondibandezele kungekho sizathu:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:5">7:5</a> Maluwusukele utshaba umphefumlo wam, luwufumane,  Lubunyashele phantsi ubomi bam, Uzuko lwam lululalise eluthulini. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:6">7:6</a> Khawusuk ume, Yehova, unomsindo, Kuphakamele ukuphuphuma komsindo wabandibandezelayo; Uvuke, undikhawulele; wena umise umgwebo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:7">7:7</a> Ibandla lezizwe malikungqonge; Ubuyele phezulu phezu kwalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:8">7:8</a> UYehova uya kugweba phakathi kwezizwe. Lithethe ityala lam,  Yehova, ngobulungisa bam, nangokugqibelela kwam okukum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:9">7:9</a> Mabuphele ububi babangendawo, ulizimase ilungisa;  Ungumcikidi weentliziyo nezintso, Thixo wobulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:10">7:10</a> Ingweletshetshe yam inoThixo, Umsindisi wabantliziyo zithe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:11">7:11</a> UThixo ngumgwebi olilungisa; UnguThixo obhavuma yonke imihla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:12">7:12</a> Ukuba ongendawo uthe akabuya, ulilolile ikrele lakhe;  Usityedile isaphetha sakhe, wasilungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:13">7:13</a> Uzibhekise kuye izixhobo zokufa, Uzenze zanomlilo iintolo zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:14">7:14</a> Yabona, yena unenimba yobutshinga; Ukhawule ububi, wazala ubuxoki;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:15">7:15</a> Umbe umhadi, wawugomba; Weyela esihogweni awasisebenzayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:16">7:16</a> Ububi bakhe bobuyela entlokweni yakhe, Naselukakayini lwakhe kufike ukugonyamela kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:17">7:17</a> Ndiya kubulela kuYehova ngokobulungisa bakhe, Ndivume ngendumiso kwigama likaYehova ophezu konke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:1">8:1</a> Kumongameli: ngolwaseGati. Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, Nkosi yethu, Hayi, ubungangamsha begama lakho ehlabathini lonke! Wena uwambathise amazulu ngendili yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:2">8:2</a> Emlonyeni wabantwana nabanyayo useke amandla, Ngenxa yababandezeli bakho, Ukuze udambise utshaba nophindezelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:3">8:3</a> Xa ndilikhangelayo izulu lakho, umsebenzi weminwe yakho,  Inyanga neenkwenkwezi ozimisileyo:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:4">8:4</a> Uyintoni na umntu lo, le nto umkhumbulelayo? Unyana womntu,  le nto umvelelayo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:5">8:5</a> Umsilelise kancinane ebuThixweni, Wamthi jize ngobuqaqawuli nangobungangamela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:6">8:6</a> Umphathise ubukhosi phezu kwemisebenzi yezandla zakho, Zonke izinto uzibeke phantsi kweenyawo zakhe:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:7">8:7</a> Impahla emfutshane, neenkomo zonke ziphelele,  Kwaneenyamakazi zonke;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:8">8:8</a> Iintaka zezulu, neentlanzi zolwandle, Into ehamba ngeendlela zolwandle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:9">8:9</a> Yehova, Nkosi yethu, Hayi, ubungangamsha begama lakho ehlabathini lonke!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:1">9:1</a> Kumongameli: ngemute-labhen, Umhobe kaDavide. Ndiya kubulela kuYehova ngentliziyo yam yonke; Ndiya kuyibalisa yonke imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:2">9:2</a> Ndiya kuvuya ndidlamke ngawe; Ndiya kulibethela uhadi igama lakho, Wena usenyangweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:3">9:3</a> Ekubuyeni kweentshaba zam umva, Ziyawa, zibhubhe ebusweni bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:4">9:4</a> Ngokuba ulifezile ityala lam nebango lam: Uhleli etroneni ungumgwebi olilungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:5">9:5</a> Uzikhalimele iintlanga, wabatshabalalisa abangendawo; Igama lazo ulicimile ngonaphakade kanaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:6">9:6</a> Iintshaba zona zigqibele, yangamanxuwa kwaphela; Imizi uyinyothule, Yadaka inkumbulo yayo yona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:7">9:7</a> Ke yena uYehova uhleli ngonaphakade, Uyizinzisele ugwebo itrone yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:8">9:8</a> Uya kugweba yena kwelimiweyo ngobulungisa, Agwebe phakathi kwezizwe ngokuthe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:9">9:9</a> UYehova makabe yingxonde kotyunyuziweyo, Ingxonde ngamaxesha engxingongo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:10">9:10</a> Bakholose ngawe abalaziyo igama lakho; Ngokuba akubashiyanga abakuquqelayo wena, Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:11">9:11</a> Vumani ngendumiso kuYehova ohlala eZiyon; Xelani ezizweni izenzo zakhe ezincamisileyo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:12">9:12</a> Ukuba umphindezeli wamagazi ubakhumbule, Akakulibalanga ukukhala kwabalulamileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:13">9:13</a> Ndibabale, Yehova; Zibone iintsizi zam ezikhoyo ngabandithiyayo, Mphakamisi wam emasangweni okufa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:14">9:14</a> Ukuze ndibalise yonke indumiso yakho, Emasangweni entombi uZiyon, Ndigcobe ngosindiso lwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:15">9:15</a> Iintlanga zitshone esihogweni ezasenzayo, Emnatheni ezawugqumelayo kubanjiswe kwaolwazo unyawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:16">9:16</a> Uzazisile uYehova; wenza umgwebo, Emthiyela ngomsebenzi wezandla zakhe ongendawo. (Bethani uhadi ngofefe. Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:17">9:17</a> Baya kubuyela kwelabafileyo abangendawo, Kwaiintlanga zonke ezimlibalayo uThixo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:18">9:18</a> Ngokuba aliyi kuhlala lilityalwa ihlwempu, Ithemba leentsizana aliyi kudaka ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:19">9:19</a> Khawusuk ume, Yehova; malungangcwangushi uluntu,  Mazigwetywe iintlanga phambi kwakho,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:20">9:20</a> Zimisele ukoyika, Yehova, Zazi iintlanga ukuba ziluluntu kuphela. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:1">10:1</a> Yini na ukuba umele mgama, Yehova, Uzifihle ngamaxesha engxingongo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:2">10:2</a> Ngokukratsha kwabangendawo bayatsha abaziintsizana;  Babanjiswa ngamayelenqe abawacingileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:3">10:3</a> Ngokuba ongendawo uyaqhayisa ngeminqweno yomphefumlo wakhe.  Nolibawa wahlukene noYehova, wamgiba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:4">10:4</a> Ongendawo ngobuchi bakhe uthi, Akasayi kubuza. Yonke iminkqangiyelo yakhe ithi, Akukho Thixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:5">10:5</a> Ziqinile iindlela zakhe ngamaxesha onke; Ziphakamile izigwebo zakho, zikude kuye; Bonke ababandezeli bakhe uyabafuthela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:6">10:6</a> Uthi entliziyweni yakhe, Andisayi kushukunyiswa;  Izizukulwana ngezizukulwana, ndingongayi kuba sebubini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:7">10:7</a> Umlomo wakhe uzele kukushwabula nokukhohlisa nokuxinezela.  Ngaphantsi kolwimi lwakhe bububi nobutshinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:8">10:8</a> Uhlala emilaleleni yeengqili, Agwinte omsulwa entsithelweni; Amehlo akhe azonda oludwayi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:9">10:9</a> Ulalela entsithelweni njengengonyama eludadeni wayo;  Ulalela ukuba axwile emke nosizana; Uxwila emke nolusizana,  elutsala ngomnatha wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:10">10:10</a> Uyabuthuma, uyabunguzela, Bawele ezinzitsheni zakhe abaziindwayi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:11">10:11</a> Uthi entliziyweni yakhe, UThixo ulibele, Ubusithelisile ubuso bakhe, akabonanga nento.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:12">10:12</a> Khawusuk ume, Yehova, phakamisa isandla sakho, Thixo.  Musa ukubalibala abalulamileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:13">10:13</a> Kungenxa yani na ukuba ongendawo amgibe uThixo, Athi entliziyweni yakhe, Akuyi kubuza?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:14">10:14</a> Ubonile wena; ngokuba uyabubona ububi nenkathazo, ububeke esandleni sakho; Uzinikela kuwe oludwayi; Ungumncedi weenkedama wena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:15">10:15</a> Yaphula ingalo yongendawo; Onobubi, mbuze okungendawo kwakhe, kungasali nento.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:16">10:16</a> UYehova nguKumkani ngonaphakade kanaphakade; Zitshabalele iintlanga, azabakho ehlabathini lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:17">10:17</a> Umnqweno wabalulamileyo uwuvile, Yehova; Wazizimasa iintliziyo zabo, wayibaza indlebe yakho,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:18">10:18</a> Ukuba ugwebe ityala lenkedama noxinzelelweyo, Angabi sabangcangcazelisa umntu wasehlabathini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:1">11:1</a> Kumongameli. EkaDavide. Ndizimela ngoYehova; Ningathini na ukuthi kumphefumlo wam, Balekela entabeni yakho njengentaka?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:2">11:2</a> Ngokuba nabo abangendawo begoba isaphetha, Bezilungisile iintolo zabo entanjeni, Ukuba batole besithele kwabantliziyo zithe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:3">11:3</a> Xa iziseko zithe zagungxulwa, Ilungisa linokuthini na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:4">11:4</a> UYehova, ulotempile yakhe iyingcwele, UYehova, ulotrone yakhe isemazulwini, Amehlo akhe ayababona, iinkophe zakhe ziyabacikida oonyana babantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:5">11:5</a> UYehova uyalicikida ilungisa; Ke yena ongendawo nothanda ukugonyamela, umthiyile umphefumlo wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:6">11:6</a> Uya kubanisela abangendawo imigibe; Umlilo, nesulfure,  nomoya olulophu, yindebe yabo abayabelweyo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:7">11:7</a> Ngokuba lilungisa uYehova; uthanda imisebenzi yobulungisa;  Othe tye uya kububona ubuso bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:1">12:1</a> Kumongameli: ngelamadoda ilizwi. Umhobe kaDavide.  Sindisa, Yehova, ngokuba uphelile owenceba, Ngokuba bathe shwaka abanyanisileyo koonyana babantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:2">12:2</a> Bathetha inkohlakalo omnye nomnye; Bathetha ngomlomo ogudileyo, nangentliziyo embaxa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:3">12:3</a> Ngamana uYehova angayinqumla yonke imilebe yomlomo ogudileyo, Ulwimi oluthetha izinto ezinkulu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:4">12:4</a> Abathe, Ulwimi lwethu siyalupheza; Imilomo yethu yeyethu;  ngubani na oyinkosi kuthi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:5">12:5</a> Ngenxa yokubhuqwa kweentsizana, ngenxa yokuncwina kwamahlwempu, Ndiya kusuka ndime ngoku, utsho uYehova; Ndiya kumbeka elusindisweni lowo ululangazelelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:6">12:6</a> Amazwi kaYehova ngamazwi acocekileyo, Yisilivere enyibilikiselwe eziko, yela emhlabeni, Ehluzwe kasixhenxe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:7">12:7</a> Wena, Yehova, uya kubagcina, Uya kubalondoloza kwesi sizukulwana ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:8">12:8</a> Abangendawo bahambahamba ngeenxa zonke, Xa kuphakanyiswe abangeni phakathi koonyana babantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:1">13:1</a> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Kunini na, Yehova,  undilibele kwaphela? Kunini na ubusithelisa ubuso bakho kum?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:2">13:2</a> Kunini na ndicebacebisana nomphefumlo wam, Ndinesingqala entliziyweni yam imini le? Kunini na lundiphakamele utshaba lwam?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:3">13:3</a> Bheka undiphendule, Yehova, Thixo wam; Khanyisa amehlo am,  hleze ndilale ukufa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:4">13:4</a> Hleze utshaba lwam luthi, Ndimeyisile; Bagcobe abandibandezelayo, xa ndithe ndashukunyiswa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:5">13:5</a> Mna ndikholose ngenceba yakho, Mayigcobe intliziyo yam ngosindiso lwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:6">13:6</a> Ndiya kuvuma kuYehova, Ngokuba endiphethe kakuhle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:1">14:1</a> Kumongameli. EkaDavide. Sithi isidenge entliziyweni yaso,  Akukho Thixo. Bonakalisile, balisikizi ngeentlondi zabo; Akukho wenza okulungileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:2">14:2</a> UYehova esemazulwini uqondele koonyana babantu, Ukubona ukuba ukho na oqiqayo, Oquqela kuThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:3">14:3</a> Bonke batyekile, bayimbozisa bephelele; Akukho wenza okulungileyo, Akukho nokuba abe mnye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:4">14:4</a> Abanakwazi na bonke abasebenzi bobutshinga, Abathi, bebadla abantu bam, bathi badla isonka, Bangamnquli uYehova?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:5">14:5</a> Apho bankwantya benkwantyile; Ngokuba uThixo usesizukulwaneni samalungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:6">14:6</a> Icebo losizana ningalidanisa, Kodwa uYehova ulihlathi lalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:7">14:7</a> Akwaba bekuvela eZiyon ukusindiswa kwamaSirayeli!  Ekubabuyiseni kukaYehova abantu bakhe ekuthinjweni, Wogcoba uYakobi, avuye uSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:1">15:1</a> Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, ngubani na owophambukela ententeni yakho? Ngubani na owohlala entabeni yakho engcwele?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:2">15:2</a> Ngohamba ngokugqibeleleyo, esenza ubulungisa, Othetha inyaniso ngentliziyo yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:3">15:3</a> Ngongahlebiyo ngolwimi lwakhe, Ongamenziyo into embi uwabo,  Ongamngcikiviyo ummelwane wakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:4">15:4</a> Odelekileyo, ecekiseka, kwawakhe amehlo, Obazukisayo ke bona abamoyikayo uYehova; Ofunga, angajiki, nokuba kubi kuye,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:5">15:5</a> Ongayinikeliyo imali yakhe ukuba adle abantu ngayo,  Ongenakugaqelwa ngaye omsulwa. Okwenzayo oko akayi kuza ashukunyiswe naphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:1">16:1</a> Eyona iligugu likaDavide. Ndigcine, Thixo, ngokuba ndizimela ngawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:2">16:2</a> Ndithe kuYehova, UyiNkosi yam, Andinanto indilungeleyo ngaphezu kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:3">16:3</a> Ndithe kwabangcwele abasehlabathini, Bona bazizinhanha apho, kukhona konke endikunanzileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:4">16:4</a> Ziya kwanda iimbulaleko zabo bamananisa ngathixo wumbi uYehova. Andiyi kuyithulula iminikelo yabo ethululwayo yegazi;  Andiyi kuwaphatha amagama abo ngomlomo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:5">16:5</a> NguYehova isahlulo endasabelwayo, nendebe endayabelwayo;  Ulenze banzi ilifa lam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:6">16:6</a> Amacandelo andiwele ezindaweni ezimnandi; Hee! Ndide ndaba nelifa elihle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:7">16:7</a> Ndiya kumbonga uYehova ondinike icebo; Nasebusuku ziyandithethisa izintso zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:8">16:8</a> Ndimmisile uYehova phambi kwam amaxesha onke; Ngokuba esekunene kum nje, andiyi kushukunyiswa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:9">16:9</a> Ngako oko iyavuya intliziyo yam, luyagcoba uzuko lwam:  Nenyama yam iya kuhlala ikholosile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:10">16:10</a> Ngokuba akuyi kuwushiya umphefumlo wam kwelabafileyo;  Akuyi kumyekela owakho wenceba ukuba abonane nesihogo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:11">16:11</a> Uya kundazisa umendo wobomi; Ebusweni bakho yinzaliseko yemivuyo; Ekunene kwakho yimihlali ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:1">17:1</a> Umthandazo kaDavide. Buve, Yehova, ubulungisa; kubazele indlebe ukuhlahlamba kwam; Wubekele indlebe umthandazo wam,  ongengamlomo ukhohlisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:2">17:2</a> Ibango lam malivele ebusweni bakho, Amehlo akho akhangele ngokuthe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:3">17:3</a> Uyicikidile intliziyo yam; undivelele ebusuku;  Undinyibilikisile, akwafumana nto; Ndiyinkqangiyele into embi,  ayiyi kuwugqitha umlomo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:4">17:4</a> Malunga nemisebenzi yabantu, ngelizwi lomlomo wakho, Mna ndizigcinile, andangena kwiindlela zamanyangaza.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:5">17:5</a> Imikhondo yam ibambe iindlela zakho, Azashukuma iinyawo zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:6">17:6</a> Mna ndinqula wena, ngokuba undiphendula, Thixo; Ndithobele indlebe yakho, kuve ukuthetha kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:7">17:7</a> Zibalule iinceba zakho, wena wabasindisayo abazimela ngawe,  Ngesandla sakho sokunene, ngenxa yabasukela phezulu kubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:8">17:8</a> Ndigcine njengeliso, njengokhozo lwalo, Ndisithelise ngesithunzi samaphiko akho,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:9">17:9</a> Phambi kwabangendawo abandibhuqayo, Phambi kweentshaba zam ngokwasemphefumlweni ezindingungelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:10">17:10</a> Zithe fithi kukutyeba; Ngomlomo wazo zithetha ngekratshi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:11">17:11</a> Zindijikelezile ngoku ekuhambeni kwam; Amehlo azo ziwamisele ukundinqumela emhlabeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:12">17:12</a> Ukufana kwazo kunjengengonyama engxamele ukuqwenga,  Kunjengengonyama entsha ihleli entsithelweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:13">17:13</a> Khawusuk ume, Yehova, Uyihlangabeze, uyiwise yona;  Wusindise umphefumlo wam kongendawo ngekrele lakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:14">17:14</a> Kubafo, ngesandla sakho, Yehova, Kubafo beli phakade,  abasahlulo sikobu bomi; Osizalisileyo isisu sabo ngeengqwebo zakho; Bakholisile ngoonyana, Ukuphuphuma kwabo bakushiya neentsapho zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:15">17:15</a> Mna ndiya kububona ubuso bakho ndisebulungiseni; Ndiya kwaneliswa sisithomo sakho ekuvukeni kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:1">18:1</a> Kumongameli. Eyomkhonzi kaYehova. EkaDavide, owawathethayo kuYehova amazwi ale ngoma, mhlenikweni uYehova wamhlangulayo esandleni seentshaba zakhe zonke nasesandleni sikaSawule;  wathi: Ndikuthanda ngembilini yam, Yehova, lomelelo lwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:2">18:2</a> Yehova, ngxondorha yam, mboniselo yam, msindisi wam, Thixo wam, liwa lam endizimela ngalo, Ngweletshetshe yam, luphondo losindiso lwam, ngxonde yam!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:3">18:3</a> Ndinqula uYehova ongowokudunyiswa, Ndiyasindiswa ezintshabeni zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:4">18:4</a> Izintya zokufa zandijikela; Imilambo yobutshijolo yandidandathekisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:5">18:5</a> Izintya zelabafileyo zandibhijela; Izirhintyelo zokufa zabetha kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:6">18:6</a> Ekubandezelekeni kwam ndanqula uYehova, Ndazibika kuThixo wam; Waliva etempileni yakhe izwi lam, Ukuzibika kwam kwafika phambi kwakhe ezindlebeni zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:7">18:7</a> Lahexa ke lanyikima ihlabathi, Iziseko zeentaba zagungqa,  Zahexa, ngokuba enomsindo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:8">18:8</a> Kwathi thaphu umsi emathatheni akhe, Wadla umlilo, uphuma emlonyeni wakhe, Kwavutha amalahle ephuma kuwo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:9">18:9</a> Wawathoba amazulu, wehla, Yangamafu amnyama phantsi kweenyawo zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:10">18:10</a> Wakhwela ekerubhini, waphaphazela, Wee tshwebelele ngamaphiko omoya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:11">18:11</a> Wamisa ubumnyama baba lisithe lakhe, umnquba wakhe ngeenxa zonke kuye; Ubumnyama bamanzi, iingqimba zamafu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:12">18:12</a> Ekukhanyeni okuphambi kwakhe, kwatyhoboza emafini akhe Isiphango samatye, namalahle omlilo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:13">18:13</a> Wadudumisa ezulwini uYehova, Ophezu konke walikhupha ilizwi lakhe. Yasisiphango samatye namalahle omlilo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:14">18:14</a> Wathuma iintolo zakhe, wabaphangalalisa; Yamininzi imibane, wabadubaduba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:15">18:15</a> Imiphantsi yamanzi yabonakala, Kwatyhileka iziseko zelimiweyo Ngokukhalima kwakho, Yehova, Ngokufutha komoya womsindo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:16">18:16</a> Wolula isandla ephezulu, wandibamba, Wandirhola emanzini amaninzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:17">18:17</a> Wandihlangula elutshabeni lwam olunamandla,  Kwabandithiyileyo, ngokuba bebomelele kunam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:18">18:18</a> Bandifikela ngemini yokusindeka kwam, UYehova wandixhasa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:19">18:19</a> Wandikhuphela endaweni ebanzi, Wandihlangula, ngokuba endithandile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:20">18:20</a> UYehova wandiphatha kakuhle ngokobulungisa bam,  Wandibuyisela ngokobunyulu bezandla zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:21">18:21</a> Ngokuba ndizigcina iindlela zikaYehova, Andemka ngokungendawo kuThixo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:22">18:22</a> Ngokuba onke amasiko akhe aphambi kwam, Nemimiselo yakhe andiyisusi kum;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:23">18:23</a> Ndaye ndingogqibeleleyo kuye, Ndazigcina, andaba nabugwenxa,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:24">18:24</a> Wandibuyisela ke uYehova ngokobulungisa bam, Ngokobunyulu bezandla zam phambi kwamehlo akhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:25">18:25</a> Kowenceba uzenza owenceba, Kwigorha eligqibeleleyo uzenza ogqibeleleyo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:26">18:26</a> Kozenze nyulu uzenza onyulu, Kojibilizayo uzenza onobuqhokolo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:27">18:27</a> Ngokuba wena uyabasindisa abantu ababandezelekileyo,  Uwathobe amehlo aqwayingileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:28">18:28</a> Ngokuba uyasilumeka isibane sam wena; UYehova uThixo wam uyabukhanyisela ubumnyama bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:29">18:29</a> Ngokuba ngawe ndigila amajarha, NgoThixo wam ndiqabela ezindongeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:30">18:30</a> UThixo yena, igqibelele indlela yakhe; Ilizwi likaYehova linyibilikisiwe, Uyingweletshetshe kubo bonke abazimela ngaye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:31">18:31</a> Ngokuba ngubani na onguThixo, ingenguye uYehova? Ngubani na oliliwa, ingenguThixo wethu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:32">18:32</a> UloThixo undibhinqise ubukroti, Uyigqibelelisileyo indlela yam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:33">18:33</a> Uzifanisayo iinyawo zam nezamaxhamakazi, Undimisayo emimangweni yam:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:34">18:34</a> Uzifundisayo ukulwa izandla zam, Zityede isaphetha sobhedu iingalo zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:35">18:35</a> Undinikileyo ingweletshetshe yosindiso lwakho: Sandixhasa isandla sakho sokunene; Ululamo lwakho lwandikhulisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:36">18:36</a> Wawenzela indawo ebanzi amanyathela am phantsi kwam,  Amaxhwele am akahexa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:37">18:37</a> Ndazisukela iintshaba zam, ndazifumana; Andabuya zada zaphela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:38">18:38</a> Ndaziqoba; azaba nakuvuka, Zawa phantsi kweenyawo zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:39">18:39</a> Wandibhinqisa ubukroti ekulweni, Wabaguqisa phantsi kwam abasukela phezulu kum;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:40">18:40</a> Wandinika ikhosi leentshaba zam, Abandithiyayo ndababhangisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:41">18:41</a> Bazibika, akwabakho msindisi; Bazibika kuYehova,  akabaphendula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:42">18:42</a> Ndabacola, banjengothuli phambi komoya, Ndabaphalaza njengodaka lwezitrato.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:43">18:43</a> Wandisiza ekubambaneni kwabantu, Wandimisa ndayintloko yeentlanga; Abantu ebe ndingabazi bandikhonza.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:44">18:44</a> Besave ngeendlebe, bandithobela, Oonyana bolunye uhlanga bahanahanisa kum;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:45">18:45</a> Oonyana bolunye uhlanga bantshwenya, Baphuma bengcangcazela ekuvingcelweni kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:46">18:46</a> UYehova uhleli; lelokubongwa iliwa lam, Aphakanyiswe uThixo ondisindisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:47">18:47</a> UloThixo wandinika impindezelo, Uzikhandaniselayo izizwe phantsi kwam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:48">18:48</a> Undisiza ezintshabeni zam; Ewe, wena undiphakamisayo kwabasukela phezulu kum, Undihlangule kumfo ogonyamelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:49">18:49</a> Ngenxa yoko ndiya kubulela kuwe, Yehova, phakathi kweentlanga, Ndivume kwigama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:50">18:50</a> Ulokhulisa iintsindiso zokumkani wakhe: Wenzayo inceba kumthanjiswa wakhe, KuDavide, nakwimbewu yakhe kude kuse ephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:1">19:1</a> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Izulu libalisa uzuko lukaThixo, Saye isibhakabhaka sixela umsebenzi wezandla zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:2">19:2</a> Imini impompozelela imini intetho, Ubusuku buxelela ubusuku ukwazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:3">19:3</a> Akukho ntetho, akukho mazwi, Apho singavakaliyo isandi sawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:4">19:4</a> Intambo yawo yokulinganisa iphume yaya ehlabathini lonke,  Kwaba seziphelweni zelimiweyo ukukhuluma kwawo. Ilanga ulimisele intente kuwo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:5">19:5</a> Lona linjengomyeni ke ephuma egumbini lakhe; Linemihlali njengegorha, ukugidima ngomendo walo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:6">19:6</a> Kusesiphelweni sezulu ukuphuma kwalo, Ukujikeleza kwalo kusa eziphelweni zalo; Akukho nto inokusithela ebushushwini balo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:7">19:7</a> Umyalelo kaYehova ugqibelele, ubuyisa umphefumlo; Isingqino sikaYehova sinyanisekile, sinika isiyatha ubulumko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:8">19:8</a> Izimiselo zikaYehova zithe tye, zivuyisa intliziyo;  Umthetho kaYehova unyulu, ukhanyisela amehlo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:9">19:9</a> Ukoyika uYehova kucocekile, kumi ngonaphakade; Izigwebo zikaYehova ziyinyaniso, zibubulungisa kwaphela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:10">19:10</a> Zinokunqweneleka kunegolide zona, nakunengcwengiweyo eninzi; Zimnandi kunobusi, kunencindi yobusi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:11">19:11</a> Zikwamkhanyisela umkhonzi wakho; Ekuzigcineni mkhulu umvuzo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:12">19:12</a> Ukulahleka, ngubani na okuqondayo? Ndenze msulwa kokusitheleyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:13">19:13</a> Kwanasekukhukhumaleni mnqande umkhonzi wakho;  Makungandilawuli; ukuze ndandule ukuba ngogqibeleleyo, Ndibe msulwa ekukreqeni okukhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:14">19:14</a> Makakholeke amazwi omlomo wam, nezicamango zentliziyo yam,  Phambi kwakho, Yehova, liwa lam, mkhululi wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:1">20:1</a> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Ngamana wakuphendula uYehova ngemini yembandezelo, Ngamana lakusa engxondeni igama likaThixo kaYakobi!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:2">20:2</a> Wakuthumela uncedo lwasengcweleni, Wakuxhasa eseZiyon!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:3">20:3</a> Wayikhumbula yonke iminikelo yakho yokudla, Wawafumana etyebile amadini akho anyukayo! (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:4">20:4</a> Wakunika ngokwentliziyo yakho, Walizalisa lonke icebo lakho!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:5">20:5</a> Singamemelela ngosindiso lwakho, Siphakamise iibhanile zethu egameni loThixo wethu; Azizalise uYehova zonke izicelo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:6">20:6</a> Ndiyazi ngoku ukuba uYehova ngumsindisi womthanjiswa wakhe;  Uya kumphendula emazulwini akhe angcwele Ngobugorha obusindisayo besandla sakhe sokunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:7">20:7</a> Abanye bakhankanya iinqwelo zokulwa, abanye bakhankanye amahashe, Ke thina sikhankanya igama likaYehova uThixo wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:8">20:8</a> Bona baguqile bawa; Thina siphakamile sema.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:9">20:9</a> Yehova, sindisa; Ukumkani asiphendule ngemini yokubiza kwethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:1">21:1</a> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, uvuyile ngamandla akho ukumkani, Asikuko nokuba uyagcoba ngosindiso lwakho!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:2">21:2</a> Umnike umnqweno wentliziyo yakhe Akwasilandula isicelo somlomo wakhe. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:3">21:3</a> Ngokuba umkhawulela ngeentsikelelo zokulungileyo, Umthwesa isithsaba segolide engcwengekileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:4">21:4</a> Wacela ubomi kuwe, wampha, Wamnika imihla emide ngonaphakade kanaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:5">21:5</a> Lukhulu uzuko lwakhe ngosindiso lwakho; Ubeka phezu kwakhe indili nobungangamela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:6">21:6</a> Ngokuba umenze waba yintsikelelo ngonaphakade, Umvuyisa ngovuyo ebusweni bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:7">21:7</a> Ngokuba ukumkani ukholose ngoYehova, Ngenceba yOsenyangweni akayi kushukunyiswa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:8">21:8</a> Isandla sakho siya kuzifumana zonke iintshaba zakho,  Esokunene sakho siya kubafumana abakuthiyayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:9">21:9</a> Uya kubenza babe njengeziko lomlilo, wakubonakala. UYehova uya kubaginya ngomsindo wakhe, Nomlilo ubadle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:10">21:10</a> Uya kusitshabalalisa isiqhamo sabo emhlabeni, Imbewu yabo koonyana babantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:11">21:11</a> Ngokuba bakuthobela ububi, Bacinga iyelenqe; abayi kufeza nto.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:12">21:12</a> Ngokuba uya kubenza bakunikele umhlana; Ngesaphetha sakho uya kuxuna iintolo zakho ebusweni babo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:13">21:13</a> Phakama, Yehova, ngamandla akho; Siya kuvuma sibethe uhadi ngobugorha bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:1">22:1</a> Kumongameli: ngeyelexhama lesifingo. Umhobe kaDavide.  Thixo wam, Thixo wam, undilahleleni na? Ukude ngani na ekusindisweni kwam, nasemazwini okubonga kwam?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:2">22:2</a> Thixo wam, ndiyabiza emini, ungaphenduli; Nasebusuku ndiyabiza, andithozanyiswa noko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:3">22:3</a> Ungcwele ke wena, Ungulohlala ezindumisweni zakwaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:4">22:4</a> Oobawo bakholosa ngawe, Bakholosa, wabasiza;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:5">22:5</a> Bakhala kuwe, basinda; Bakholosa ngawe, abadana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:6">22:6</a> Ke mna ndingumbungu, andimntu; Ndisisingcikivo soluntu,  into edelekileyo ebantwini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:7">22:7</a> Bonke abandibonayo bayandigculela; Bayasineka, bahlunguzela intloko;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:8">22:8</a> Bathi, Makazilahlele kuYehova, amsize, Amhlangule kaloku,  ngokuba emthandile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:9">22:9</a> Ewe, nguwe umtyhobozisi wam esizalweni, Inkolosisi yam ndisemabeleni kama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:10">22:10</a> Ndalahlelwa kuwe kwasesizalweni; Kwasembilinini kama ubunguThixo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:11">22:11</a> Musa ukuba kude nam, ngokuba isondele imbandezelo, Ngokuba akukho mncedi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:12">22:12</a> Ndingqongwe ziinkunzi ezininzi, Ndihlanganyelwe zeziziimbalasane zaseBhashan.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:13">22:13</a> Zindakhamele umlomo wazo, Njengengonyama eqwengayo,  egqumayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:14">22:14</a> Ndiphalele njengamanzi, Ahlukene onke amathambo am;  Yanjengomthwebeba intliziyo yam, Inyibilikile phakathi kwezibilini zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:15">22:15</a> Omile njengegophe amandla am, Ulwimi lwam lunamathele ekhuhlangubeni lam; Undibeka eluthulini lokufa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:16">22:16</a> Ngokuba izinja zindirhawule, Ibandla labenzi bokubi lindingungele; Bagqobhoza izandla zam neenyawo zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:17">22:17</a> Ndinokuwabala onke amathambo am; Bona bayandijonga,  bayandibonela,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:18">22:18</a> Babelana ngeengubo zam, Isambatho sam basenzela amaqashiso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:19">22:19</a> Ke wena, Yehova, musa ukuba kude; Mandla am, khawuleza undincede.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:20">22:20</a> Wuhlangule ekreleni umphefumlo wam, Okuphela kwawo,  ethupheni lenja.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:21">22:21</a> Ndisindise emlonyeni wengonyama, Nasezimpondweni zenqu uya kundiphendula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:22">22:22</a> Ndiya kulazisa igama lakho kubazalwana bam, Ndikudumise phakathi kwebandla, ndithi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:23">22:23</a> Nina nimoyikayo uYehova, mdumiseni; Nonke, mbewu kaYakobi,  mzukiseni, Nimhlonele nina, mbewu yonke kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:24">22:24</a> Kuba azidelekanga, azibanga nazothe kuye iintsizi zolusizana; Akabusithelisanga ubuso bakhe kuye; Ekuzibikeni kwakhe kuye waphulaphula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:25">22:25</a> Ivela kuwe indumiso yam ebandleni elikhulu;  Nezibhambathiso zam ndiya kuzizalisa phambi kwabamoyikayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:26">22:26</a> Baya kudla abalulamileyo, bahluthe; Baya kudumisa uYehova abamngxamelayo. Ngamana yaphila intliziyo yenu ngonaphakade!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:27">22:27</a> Ziya kukhumbula zibuyele kuYehova zonke iziphelo zehlabathi, Iqubude phambi kwakhe yonke imizalwane yeentlanga:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:28">22:28</a> Ngokuba bobukaYehova ubukumkani, Nguye umlawuli ezintlangeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:29">22:29</a> Baya kudla, baqubude, bonke abatyebileyo behlabathi; Baya kuguqa phambi kwakhe bonke abatshona eluthulini,  Abangawugciniyo umphefumlo wabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:30">22:30</a> Imbewu iya kumkhonza; Kuya kubaliselwa isizukulwana ngayo iNkosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:31">22:31</a> Baya kuza baxele ubulungisa bayo Kubantu abaza kuzalwa,  ukuba oko ukwenzile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:1">23:1</a> Umhobe kaDavide. UYehova ngumalusi wam, andisweli lutho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:2">23:2</a> Wenza ukuba mandibuthe emakriweni aluhlaza; Undithundezela emanzini angawokuphumla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:3">23:3</a> Uyawubuyisa umphefumlo wam; Undikhaphela ezindleleni zobulungisa ngenxa yegama lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:4">23:4</a> Nokuba ndihamba emfuleni wethunzi lokufa, Andiyi koyika bubi, ngokuba unam wena; Intonga yakho, umsimelelo wakho,  uyandithuthuzela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:5">23:5</a> Undilungisela isithebe phambi kwababandezeli bam,  Uyithambisa ngeoli intloko yam, Indebe yam iyaphalala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:6">23:6</a> Inene, ndiya kulandelwa kokulungileyo nenceba Yonke imihla yobomi bam, Ndihlale endlwini kaYehova Imihla emide.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:1">24:1</a> Umhobe kaDavide. LelikaYehova ihlabathi nenzaliseko yalo,  Elimiweyo, nabahleli kulo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:2">24:2</a> Ngokuba yena waliseka phezu kweelwandle, Walizinzisa phezu kwemilambo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:3">24:3</a> Ngubani na onokunyuka aye entabeni kaYehova? Ngubani na onokuma endaweni yakhe engcwele?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:4">24:4</a> Ngozandla zimsulwa, ontliziyo inyulu, Ongawuphakamiseli kwinkohlakalo umphefumlo wakhe, Ongafungiyo ngenkohliso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:5">24:5</a> Uya kwamkela intsikelelo kuYehova, Nobulungisa kuThixo ongumsindisi wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:6">24:6</a> Siso eso isizukulwana sabamngxameleyo, Sababufunayo ubuso bakho, Thixo kaYakobi.(phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:7">24:7</a> Phakamisani iintloko zenu, masango; Niziphakamise, minyango yaphakade, Angene uKumkani wozuko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:8">24:8</a> Ngubani na ke lo Kumkani wozuko? NguYehova onamandla,  oligorha; NguYehova, igorha emfazweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:9">24:9</a> Phakamisani iintloko zenu, masango, Niziphakamise, minyango yaphakade, Angene lo Kumkani wozuko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:10">24:10</a> Ngubani na ke yena uKumkani wozuko? NguYehova wemikhosi,  Nguye lo Kumkani wozuko. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:1">25:1</a> EkaDavide. Ndiwuphakamisela kuwe, Yehova, umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:2">25:2</a> Thixo wam, ndikholose ngawe, Mandingadani;  Mazingandivuyeleli iintshaba zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:3">25:3</a> Ewe, bonke abo bakuthembayo abayi kudana; Kuya kudana abo banginiza ngelize.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:4">25:4</a> Ndazise iindlela zakho, Yehova, Ndifundise umendo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:5">25:5</a> Ndinyathelise enyanisweni yakho, undifundise; Ngokuba unguThixo ongumsindisi wam; Ndithembe wena yonke imihla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:6">25:6</a> Khumbula iimfesane zakho, Yehova, neenceba zakho; Ngokuba kususela kwaphakade zikho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:7">25:7</a> Musa ukuzikhumbula izono zobutsha bam, nokreqo lwam;  Ndikhumbule ngokwenceba yakho wena, Ngenxa yokulunga kwakho,  Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:8">25:8</a> Ulungile, uthe tye uYehova; Ngenxa yoko uyabayalela indlela aboni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:9">25:9</a> Uyabanyathelisa abalulamileyo emasikweni akhe, Abafundise abalulamileyo indlela yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:10">25:10</a> Zonke iindlela zikaYehova ziyinceba nenyaniso, Kwabagcina umnqophiso wakhe nezingqino zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:11">25:11</a> Ngenxa yegama lakho, Yehova, xolela ubugwenxa bam, Ngokuba bukhulu bona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:12">25:12</a> Ngubani na ke umntu omoyikayo uYehova? Womyalela indlela aya kuyinyula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:13">25:13</a> Umphefumlo wakhe wohlala wonwabile, Imbewu yakhe ilidle ilifa ilizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:14">25:14</a> Ukucweya kukaYehova kunabamoyikayo; Ubazisa umnqophiso wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:15">25:15</a> Amehlo am ahlala emi kuYehova, Ngokuba nguye ozirholayo eluthanjeni iinyawo zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:16">25:16</a> Ndibheke, undibabale, Ngokuba ndindodwa, ndibandezelekile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:17">25:17</a> Iimbandezelo zentliziyo yam ziphangalalisiwe; Ndikhuphe ekucuthekeni kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:18">25:18</a> Khangela ukucinezeleka kwam nokwaphuka kwam, Uxolele zonke izono zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:19">25:19</a> Zikhangele iintshaba zam, ngokuba zininzi; Zindithiye ngentiyo egonyamelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:20">25:20</a> Wugcine umphefumlo wam, undihlangule; Mandingadani,  ngokuba ndizimela ngawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:21">25:21</a> Ukugqibelela nokuthi tye makundilondoloze, Ngokuba ndithembele kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:22">25:22</a> Khulula uSirayeli, Thixo, Ezimbandezelweni zakhe zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:1">26:1</a> EkaDavide. Lithethe ityala lam, Yehova, ngokuba mna ndihambe engqibelelweni yam, Ndakholosa ngoYehova, andahexa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:2">26:2</a> Ndicikide, Yehova, undilinge; Nyibilikisa izintso zam nentliziyo yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:3">26:3</a> Ngokuba inceba yakho iphambi kwamehlo am, Ndihamba enyanisweni yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:4">26:4</a> Andihlali namadoda akhohlakeleyo, Andihambi nabanyhwalazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:5">26:5</a> Ndilithiyile ibandla labenzi bobubi, Andihlali nabangendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:6">26:6</a> Ndizihlamba kokumsulwa izandla zam, Ndisiphahle isibingelelo sakho, Yehova,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:7">26:7</a> Ukuba ndivakalise izwi lokubulela, Ndibalise ngayo yonke imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:8">26:8</a> Yehova, ndiyalithanda ikhaya eliyindlu yakho, Nendawo yokuhlala kozuko lwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:9">26:9</a> Musa ukuwubuthela umphefumlo wam ndawonye naboni, Ubomi bam ndawonye namadoda anamagazi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:10">26:10</a> Wona azandla zinamanyala, Wona ezokunene zawo zizeleyo zizicengo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:11">26:11</a> Mna ke okwam ndihamba engqibelelweni yam; Ndikhulule,  undibabale.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:12">26:12</a> Unyawo lwam lumi endaweni ebanzi; Ndimbonga uYehova ndisemabandleni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:1">27:1</a> EkaDavide. NguYehova umkhanyiseli wam nomsindisi wam,  ndiya koyika bani na? NguYehova inqaba yobomi bam, ndiya kunkwantya ngabani na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:2">27:2</a> Bakusondela kum abenzi bobubi ukuba badle inyama yam,  Bakuza ababandezeli bam neentshaba zam kum, bakhubeka bawa bona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:3">27:3</a> Bendingafanelana ndirhawulwe ngumkhosi isuka ingoyiki intliziyo yam; Bendingafanelana ndiphakanyelwe yimfazwe,  ndisuka ndithembe noko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:4">27:4</a> Ndicele nto-nye kuYehova, ndifuna yona: Ukuba ndihlale endlwini kaYehova yonke imihla yobomi bam, Ndibone ubuhle bukaYehova, ndiphicothe etempileni yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:5">27:5</a> Ngokuba undigusha emnqubeni wakhe ngemini yobubi,  Undisithelisa esitheni lentente yakhe, Undimisa eweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:6">27:6</a> Ngoku ke iya kuphakama intloko yam phezu kweentshaba zam ezindijikelezayo, Ndibingelele ententeni yakhe imibingelelo yokuduma, Ndivume, ndibethe uhadi kuYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:7">27:7</a> Yiva, Yehova, ndakubiza ngezwi lam; Ndibabale,  undiphendule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:8">27:8</a> Intliziyo yam ithi kuwe, kweli uthi, Funani ubuso bam,  Ubuso bakho, Yehova, ndiya kubufuna.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:9">27:9</a> Musa ukubusithelisa ubuso bakho kum; Musa ukumgila umkhonzi wakho ngomsindo; Uluncedo lwam, musa ukundilahla; Musa ukundishiya, Thixo ondisindisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:10">27:10</a> Ngokuba ubawo noma bandishiyile, Wesuka uYehova wandichola.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:11">27:11</a> Ndiyalele, Yehova, indlela yakho, Ndikhaphe emendweni othe tye, ngenxa yabandilaleleyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:12">27:12</a> Musa ukundinikela elitheni labandibandezelayo, Ngokuba ndiphakanyelwe ngamangqina axokayo, nabafutha ukugonyamela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:13">27:13</a> Ndinge ndiphelelwe, koko bendikholwa kukuba ndokubona ukulunga kukaYehova Ezweni lobu bomi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:14">27:14</a> Thembela kuYehova; Yomelela, ikhaliphe intliziyo yakho,  Uthembele kuYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:1">28:1</a> EkaDavide. Ndidanduluka kuwe, Yehova; Liwa lam, musa ukuzenza isithulu; Hleze, wakuthi cwaka kum, Ndifane nabahla baye emhadini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:2">28:2</a> Yiva izwi lokukhunga kwam ekuzibikeni kwam kuwe,  Ekuziphakamiseleni kwam izandla zam kwingcwele kangcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:3">28:3</a> Musa ukundiqweqwedisa nabangendawo, Nabenzi bobutshinga;  Abathetha uxolo kummelwane wabo, Benobubi ezintliziyweni zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:4">28:4</a> Banike ngokwemisebenzi yabo, ngokobubi beentlondi zabo;  Banike ngokwezenzo zezandla zabo; Babuyisele ngokwempatho yabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:5">28:5</a> Ekubeni bengayiqondi imisebenzi kaYehova, Nezenzo zezandla zakhe, Uya kubagungxula, angabakhi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:6">28:6</a> Makabongwe uYehova, Kuba elivile ilizwi lokukhunga kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:7">28:7</a> NguYehova amandla am nengweletshetshe yam; Yakholosa ngaye intliziyo yam, ndancedeka. Iyadlamka ke intliziyo yam,  Ndiyamdumisa ngengoma yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:8">28:8</a> UYehova ungamandla kubo; Uligwiba losindiso kumthanjiswa wakhe yena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:9">28:9</a> Sindisa abantu bakho, Usikelele ilifa lakho, Ubaluse,  ubathwale kude kuse ephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:1">29:1</a> Umhobe kaDavide. Mnikeni uYehova, nina nyana bakaThixo,  Mnikeni uYehova uzuko namandla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:2">29:2</a> Mnikeni uYehova uzuko lwegama lakhe; Qubudani kuYehova nivethe ezingcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:3">29:3</a> Izwi likaYehova liphezu kwamanzi; UThixo wozuko uyadudumisa, KwauYehova phezu kwamanzi amaninzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:4">29:4</a> Izwi likaYehova linamandla, Izwi likaYehova linobungangamela;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:5">29:5</a> Izwi likaYehova laphula imisedare, UYehova waphula imisedare yaseLebhanon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:6">29:6</a> Uyidlobisa njengenkonyana, ILebhanon neSiriyon njengethole lenqu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:7">29:7</a> Izwi likaYehova lilenyise okwamalangatye omlilo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:8">29:8</a> Izwi likaYehova liyenza isaqhwithi intlango, UYehova uyenza isaqhwithi intlango yaseKadeshe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:9">29:9</a> Izwi likaYehova lizuzisa amaxhamakazi, Lihlube amahlathi;  Etempileni yakhe into yonke iphela ithi, Luzuko!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:10">29:10</a> UYehova wahlala kunogumbe, UYehova uhleli enguKumkani ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:11">29:11</a> UYehova uya kubanika abantu bakhe amandla; UYehova uya kubasikelela abantu bakhe ngoxolo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:1">30:1</a> Umhobe: ingoma yokusungulwa kwayo indlu. EkaDavide. Ndiya kukuphakamisa, Yehova, kuba undirholile wandinyusa,  Akwazivuyisa iintshaba zam ngam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:2">30:2</a> Yehova, Thixo wam, Ndazibika kuwe, wandiphilisa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:3">30:3</a> Yehova, uwunyusile kwelabafileyo umphefumlo wam, Wandidlisa ubomi, ukuba ndingehli ndiye emhadini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:4">30:4</a> Mbetheleni uhadi uYehova, nina bakhe benceba, Nibulele isikhumbuzo sakhe esingcwele,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:5">30:5</a> Ngokuba yinto yephanyazo umsindo wakhe, Itarhu lakhe liyinto yobomi; Ngokuhlwa kulalisa ukulila, Kusasa kubakho ukumemelela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:6">30:6</a> Ke mna ndathi ebunqobeni bam, Andiyi kushukunyiswa naphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:7">30:7</a> Yehova, enkolosekweni yakho ubuyiqinisile intaba yam;  Ubusithelisile ubuso bakho, ndakhwankqiswa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:8">30:8</a> Ndadanduluka kuwe, Yehova, Ndakhunga kuYehova:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:9">30:9</a> Ndathi, Kukho nzuzo yani na egazini lam, ekuhleni kwam ndiye esihogweni? Lokudumisa na uthuli? loyixela na inyaniso yakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:10">30:10</a> Yiva, Yehova, undibabale; Yehova, yiba ngumncedi wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:11">30:11</a> Wakuguqula ukulila kwam, kwaba kukuqamba; Wandikhulula ezirhwexayo, wandibhinqisa uvuyo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:12">30:12</a> Ukuze uzuko lwam luvume ngawe, lungathi cwaka. Yehova,  Thixo wam, ndiya kubulela kuwe ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:1">31:1</a> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Ndizimela ngawe, Yehova,  mandingaze ndidaniswe; Ndisize ngobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:2">31:2</a> Ndithobele indlebe yakho, ungxame undihlangule; Yiba liliwa eliligwiba kum, Indlu yemboniselo yokundisindisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:3">31:3</a> Ngokuba ingxondorha yam nemboniselo yam nguwe; Ngenxa yegama lakho uya kundikhapha undithundeze.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:4">31:4</a> Uya kundirhola esibatheni ababesigqumele mna, Ngokuba uyinqaba yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:5">31:5</a> Ndiwuyaleza umoya wam esandleni sakho; Uyandikhulula,  Yehova, Thixo wenyaniso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:6">31:6</a> Ndibathiyile abagcine amampunge angento yanto. Ndikholose ngoYehova mna.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:7">31:7</a> Ndiya kugcoba ndivuye ngenceba yakho, Ngenxa enokuba uzibonile iintsizi zam, Wazazi iingxingongo zomphefumlo wam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:8">31:8</a> Akwandivingcela ngesandla seentshaba, Wazimisa endaweni ebanzi iinyawo zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:9">31:9</a> Ndibabale, Yehova, ngokuba ndibandezelekile; Lonakele kukukhathazeka iliso lam, nomphefumlo wam, nesisu sam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:10">31:10</a> Ngokuba buphelile sisingqala ubomi bam, Neminyaka yam kukuncwina; Ayagexa amandla am ngobugwenxa bam, Namathambo am aluphele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:11">31:11</a> Ngenxa yababandezeli bam bonke ndaba sisingcikivo,  Ngokukodwa kubamelwane bam; ndaba yinto yokunkwantyisa kwabandaziyo; Abandibonayo ngaphandle baya ndibaleka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:12">31:12</a> Ndilityelwe njengomfi ongasakhunjulwayo; Ndinjengesitya esiza kulahlwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:13">31:13</a> Ngokuba ndive intlebendwane yabaninzi, Ukunxunguphala ngeenxa zonke. Ekugquguleni kwabo ngam, Bankqangiyela ukuthabatha umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:14">31:14</a> Ke mna ndikholose ngawe, Yehova; Ndithi, UnguThixo wam wena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:15">31:15</a> Asesandleni sakho amaxesha am; Ndihlangule esandleni seentshaba zam nakwabandisukelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:16">31:16</a> Khanyisa ubuso bakho phezu komkhonzi wakho; Ndisindise ngenceba yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:17">31:17</a> Yehova, andiyi kudana, ngokuba ndinqula wena; Makudane abangendawo, bathi cwaka kwelabafileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:18">31:18</a> Mawubotshwe umlomo wobuxoki, Othetha ngelungisa ngokusa,  Unekratshi, udela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:19">31:19</a> Hayi, ubukhulu bokulunga kwakho, obuqwebele abakoyikayo,  Obenzela abazimela ngawe, ebusweni boonyana babantu!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:20">31:20</a> Ubasithelisa esitheni lobuso bakho kumayelenqe abantu;  Uyabagusha emnqubeni ekubambaneni kweelwimi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:21">31:21</a> Makabongwe uYehova, Ngokuba endenzele inceba ebalulekileyo emzini onqabileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:22">31:22</a> Ke mna ndathi ekuphakuzeleni kwam, Ndinqanyulwe andabakho emehlweni akho. Waliva noko izwi lokukhunga kwam ekuzibikeni kwam kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:23">31:23</a> Thandani uYehova, nonke nina bakhe benceba; NguYehova umlondolozi wabanyanisileyo, Umphindezeli ngokukhulu kowenza ngekratshi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:24">31:24</a> Yomelelani, ikhaliphe intliziyo yenu Nonke nina nithembele kuYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:1">32:1</a> EkaDavide. Eyokuqiqa. Hayi, uyolo lwakhe olukreqo luxolelweyo, osono siselelweyo!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:2">32:2</a> Hayi, uyolo lomntu angabubaleliyo uYehova kuye ubugwenxa,  Ekungekho kukhohlisa emoyeni wakhe!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:3">32:3</a> Ndithi ndakuthi cwaka, aluphale amathambo am Ngokubhonga kwam imihla yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:4">32:4</a> Ngokuba imini nobusuku, besinzima phezu kwam isandla sakho,  Baguquka ubumanzi bam, baba kukubalela kwasehlotyeni.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:5">32:5</a> Ndikwazisile isono sam, ubugwenxa bam andabugquma; Ndathi,  Ndoluvuma ukreqo lwam kuYehova; Wabuxolela ke wena ubugwenxa besono sam. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:6">32:6</a> Ngenxa yoko mabathandaze kuwe bonke abenceba ngexesha lokukufumana; Inene, ekukhukuleni kwamanzi amaninzi Akayi kufika kubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:7">32:7</a> Wena uyindawo yokuzimela kwam; uyandilondoloza embandezelweni, Undingqonge ngomemelelo lokusiza.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:8">32:8</a> Ndiya kukuqiqisa ndikuyalele indlela owohamba ngayo: Ndiya kukucebisa, iliso lam likuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:9">32:9</a> Musani ukuba njengamahashe, njengoondlebende, ukungabi nangqondo; Abazivatho zingumkhala, neentambo zokubabopha umlomo; Bengenazo abasayi kusondela kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:10">32:10</a> Mkhulu umvandedwa wongendawo; Ke okholosa ngoYehova, yena uya kumjikela ngenceba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:11">32:11</a> Vuyani kuYehova, nigcobe, nina malungisa, Nimemelele, nina nonke bantliziyo zithe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:1">33:1</a> Memelelani kuYehova, nina malungisa; Ibafanele abathe tye indumiso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:2">33:2</a> Bulelani kuYehova ngohadi, Mbetheleni umrhubhe ontambo zilishumi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:3">33:3</a> Mvumeleni ingoma entsha, Nilungise ukubetha ngelokuduma;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:4">33:4</a> Nokuba lithe tye ilizwi likaYehova, Konke akwenzayo kuthembekile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:5">33:5</a> Ngumthandi wobulungisa nokusesikweni, Lizele ihlabathi yinceba kaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:6">33:6</a> Lenzeka ngelizwi likaYehova izulu, Umkhosi walo lonke ngomoya womlomo wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:7">33:7</a> Ulobutha njengemfumba amanzi olwandle, Ulobeka koovimba amanzi enzonzobila.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:8">33:8</a> Malimoyike uYehova lonke ihlabathi, Bamhlonele bonke abemi belimiweyo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:9">33:9</a> Ngokuba wathetha, kwabakho; Wawisa umthetho yena, kwema.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:10">33:10</a> UYehova ulitshitshisile icebo leentlanga; Uzalele iingcinga zezizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:11">33:11</a> Icebo likaYehova limi ngonaphakade, Iingcinga zentliziyo yakhe kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:12">33:12</a> Hayi, uyolo lohlanga oluThixo walo unguYehova; Lwabantu abanyulileyo, baba lilifa kuye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:13">33:13</a> Uqondele esemazulwini uYehova; Uyababona bonke oonyana babantu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:14">33:14</a> Esendaweni yakhe yokuhlala, wondele Kubemi bonke behlabathi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:15">33:15</a> Ulobumba ngakunye intliziyo yabo, Uloqonda zonke izenzo zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:16">33:16</a> Akukho kumkani osindiswa yimpi enkulu; Igorha alihlangulwa ngamandla alo amakhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:17">33:17</a> Liyaxoka ihashe ukuba lingasindisa, Nangamandla alo amakhulu alinakusiza.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:18">33:18</a> Yabona, iliso likaYehova likubo abamoyikayo, Abalindele inceba yakhe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:19">33:19</a> Ukuba awuhlangule ekufeni umphefumlo wabo, Abagcine ngexesha lendlala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:20">33:20</a> Umphefumlo wethu ulindele kuYehova; Nguye uncedo lwethu,  nengweletshetshe yethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:21">33:21</a> Ngokuba iya kuvuya ngaye intliziyo yethu, Sikholosile nje ngegama lakhe elingcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:22">33:22</a> Inceba yakho mayibe phezu kwethu, Yehova, Njengoko sikulindeleyo kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:1">34:1</a> EkaDavide; oko wazenza ophambene ingqondo phambi koAbhimeleki, waza yena wamgxotha, wahamba. Ndiya kumbonga uYehova ngamaxesha onke, Ihlale isemlonyeni wam indumiso yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:2">34:2</a> Uya kuqhayisa umphefumlo wam ngoYehova; Bova abalulamileyo,  bavuye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:3">34:3</a> Menzeni mkhulu kunye nam uYehova, Siliphakamise kunye igama lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:4">34:4</a> Ndamfuna uYehova, wandiphendula; Wandihlangula kwiinto zonke endinxunguphala zizo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:5">34:5</a> Babheka kuye, bakhazimla; Ubuso babo ababa nazintloni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:6">34:6</a> Usizana lwadanduluka, weva uYehova, Walusindisa ezimbandezelweni zalo zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:7">34:7</a> Isithunywa sikaYehova sibangqinga ngeenxa zonke abamoyikayo, Sibahlangule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:8">34:8</a> Yivani, nibone ukuba ulungile uYehova. Hayi, uyolo lomfo ozimela ngaye!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:9">34:9</a> Moyikeni uYehova, nina bangcwele bakhe, Ngokuba abanakuswela abamoyikayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:10">34:10</a> Iingonyama ezintsha ziyaswela, zilambe; Ke bona abamfunayo uYehova abasweli nanye into elungileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:11">34:11</a> Yizani, bonyana, phulaphulani kum; Ndonifundisa ukoyika uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:12">34:12</a> Ngubani na umntu obungxameleyo ubomi, Othanda imihla yokubona okulungileyo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:13">34:13</a> Gcina ulwimi lwakho ebubini, Umlomo wakho ungathethi nkohliso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:14">34:14</a> Suka ebubini, wenze okulungileyo; Funa uxolo, uluphuthume.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:15">34:15</a> Amehlo kaYehova akumalungisa, Iindlebe zakhe zisekuzibikeni kwawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:16">34:16</a> Ubuso bukaYehova bujonge abenzi bokubi, Ukuba akunqumle ehlabathini ukukhunjulwa kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:17">34:17</a> Akhala, weva uYehova; Wawahlangula ezimbandezelweni zawo zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:18">34:18</a> Usondele uYehova kwabantliziyo zaphukileyo, Abasindise abamoya utyumkileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:19">34:19</a> Buninzi ububi obulihlelayo ilungisa, Ke uYehova ulihlangula kubo bonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:20">34:20</a> Uyawagcina onke amathambo alo, Akwaphuki nalinye kuwo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:21">34:21</a> Ububi buyambulala ongendawo; Abathiyi belungisa bayalithwala ityala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:22">34:22</a> UYehova uyawukhulula umphefumlo wabakhonzi bakhe,  Bangathwali tyala bonke abazimela ngaye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:1">35:1</a> EkaDavide. Bambana, Yehova, nababambana nam. Yilwa nabalwa nam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:2">35:2</a> Qubula ikhaka nengweletshetshe, Usukume undincede.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:3">35:3</a> Rhola umkhonto, uvingce indlela yabandisukelayo; Yithi kumphefumlo wam, Ndilusindiso lwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:4">35:4</a> Mabadane, bahlazeke, abazungula umphefumlo wam; Mababuye umva babe neentloni abacinga ububi ngam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:5">35:5</a> Mababe njengomququ phambi komoya, Sibatyhale isithunywa sikaYehova, bawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:6">35:6</a> Indlela yabo mayibe mnyama, ibe buthelezi, Sibasukele isithunywa sikaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:7">35:7</a> Ngokuba basigqumele mna isibatha sabo ngelize; Bawumbela isihogo umphefumlo wam ngelize.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:8">35:8</a> Mayimfikele intshabalalo engazi; Sibambise yena isibatha sakhe awasigqumayo, Eyele kuso ngesithonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:9">35:9</a> Wogcoba ke umphefumlo wam kuYehova, Ube nemihlali ngosindiso lwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:10">35:10</a> Onke amathambo am aya kuthi, Yehova, ngubani na onjengawe,  Mhlanguli wosizana kowomeleleyo kunalo, Kwausizana nehlwempu kumxhakamfuli walo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:11">35:11</a> Kusuke kwema amangqina angenakulungisa, Andibuza into endingayaziyo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:12">35:12</a> Bandibuyekeza ngobubi esikhundleni sokulungileyo;  Uxhwalekile umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:13">35:13</a> Ke mna, xa babesifa, iingubo zam bezizezirhwexayo;  Ndawucinezela umphefumlo wam ngokuzila ukudla; Umthandazo wam wabuyela esifubeni sam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:14">35:14</a> Ndaziphatha njengokungathi unguwethu, njengokungathi ungumzalwana kum, ukuhamba-hamba kwam; Ndanga ndingombambazelela unina, ukuthobeka kwam, ndinezimnyama zokuzila.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:15">35:15</a> Ke ekuqhwaleleni kwam avuya, ahlangana, Ahlangana ngam amagxidolo, nendingabaziyo, Bandihlalela ngentlamba, abayeka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:16">35:16</a> Ngokweentshembenxa ezizihiba ngenxa yesonka,  Banditshixizela amazinyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:17">35:17</a> Nkosi, kunini na ubonela? Buyisa umphefumlo wam kwiintshabalaliso zabo, Okuphela kwawo ezingonyameni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:18">35:18</a> Ndiya kubulela kuwe ebandleni elikhulu, Ebantwini abaninzi ndiya kukudumisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:19">35:19</a> Mazingandivuyeleli iintshaba zam ngobuxoki,  Bangatyandelani ngoshiyi abandithiyayo ngelize:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:20">35:20</a> Ngokuba abathethi luxolo; Bacinga amazwi enkohliso ngabanyhamnyhekileyo belizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:21">35:21</a> Bayandisinekela, Bathi, Tshotsho! Tshotsho! Abonile amehlo ethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:22">35:22</a> Ubonile, Yehova; musa ukuba sisithulu; Nkosi, musa ukuba kude kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:23">35:23</a> Zivuse, uphaphe ngenxa yebango lam, Thixo wam, Nkosi yam,  ngenxa yento esibambene ngayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:24">35:24</a> Lithethe ityala lam ngokobulungisa bakho, Yehova Thixo wam; Mabangandivuyeleli;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:25">35:25</a> Mabangathi entliziyweni yabo, Tshotsho! Nantso into ebe siyfuna! Mabangathi, Simginyile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:26">35:26</a> Mabadane, babe neentloni kunye Abavuyela ububi bam;  Bambathe ukudana nehlazo Abazikhulisayo kunam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:27">35:27</a> Mabamemelele, bavuye, abananze ubulungisa bam, Bahlale besithi, Makabe mkhulu uYehova, Ulonanze uxolo lomkhonzi wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:28">35:28</a> Ulwimi lwam luya kuxela ubulungisa bakho Nendumiso yakho,  imihla yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:1">36:1</a> Kumongameli. Eyomkhonzi kaYehova. EkaDavide. Ongendawo unezihlabo zokreqo entliziyweni yakhe ngaphakathi, ezithi,  Akukho koyika Thixo emehlweni akhe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:2">36:2</a> Ngokuba zithetha kuye ngokugudileyo emehlweni akhe, Zide zimfumanise ubugwenxa bakhe, zimthiye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:3">36:3</a> Amazwi omlomo wakhe abubutshinga nenkohliso; Uyekile ukwenza ngokuqiqa nangokulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:4">36:4</a> Ucinga ubutshinga elukhukweni lwakhe; Uzimisa endleleni engalungileyo; Akabucekisi ububi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:5">36:5</a> Yehova, inceba yakho ifikelela ezulwini, Ukuthembeka kwakho esibhakabhakeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:6">36:6</a> Ubulungisa bakho bunjengeentaba zikaThixo; Izigwebo zakho zingamanzi enzonzobila; Usindisa umntu neenkomo, Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:7">36:7</a> Hayi, ixabiso lenceba yakho, Thixo! Oonyana babantu bazimela ngethunzi lamaphiko akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:8">36:8</a> Bayahluthiswa kukutyeba kwendlu yakho; Ubaseza emlanjeni weziyolo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:9">36:9</a> Ngokuba likuwe ithende lobomi; Ekukhanyeni kwakho sibona ukukhanya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:10">36:10</a> Bolulele inceba yakho abakwaziyo, Ubolulele ubulungisa bakho abantliziyo zithe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:11">36:11</a> Malungandinyatheli unyawo lonekratshi. Singandiphekuzi isandla sabangendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:12">36:12</a> Nabo bewile abasebenzi bobutshinga; Batyhalwe bawa, ababa nakuvuka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:1">37:1</a> EkaDavide. Musa ukuzivuthisa ngomsindo ngabenzi bobubi;  Musa ukubamonela abenzi bobugqwetha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:2">37:2</a> Ngokuba baya kusikwa kamsinyane njengengca, Babune njengohlaza oluphumayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:3">37:3</a> Kholosa ngoYehova, wenze okulungileyo; Lime ilizwe,  ulandelane nokuthembeka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:4">37:4</a> Ziyolise ngoYehova; Wokunika okunqwenelwa yintliziyo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:5">37:5</a> Yiyekele kuYehova indlela yakho, Ukholose ngaye;  wokwenzela,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:6">37:6</a> Abuvelise njengokukhanya ubulungisa bakho, Nebango lakho njengemini enkulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:7">37:7</a> Yithi cwaka kuYehova, ulindele kuye; Musa ukuzivuthisa ngomsindo ngonempumelelo ngendlela yakhe, Ngomntu ofeza amayelenqe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:8">37:8</a> Lahla umsindo, ushiye ubushushu; Musa ukuzivuthisa ngomsindo, kuba oko kusingisa ekwenzeni ububi kuphela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:9">37:9</a> Ngokuba abenzi bobubi baya kunqunyulwa; Ke bona abamthembayo uYehova, baya kulidla ilifa ilizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:10">37:10</a> Kusaya kuba mzuzwana, angabikho ongendawo; Uthi wakuyikhangela indawo yakhe, angabikho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:11">37:11</a> Ke bona abalulamileyo baya kulidla ilifa ilizwe,  Baziyolise ngobuninzi boxolo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:12">37:12</a> Ongendawo ulenzela amayelenqe ilungisa, Ulitshixizela amazinyo akhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:13">37:13</a> INkosi iyamhleka, Ngokuba ibona ukuba iyeza imini yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:14">37:14</a> Barhole ikrele abangendawo, bagobe isaphetha sabo, Ukuba bawise usizana nehlwempu, Basike abandlela zithe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:15">37:15</a> Ikrele labo liya kungena kwakweyabo intliziyo, Zaphuke izaphetha zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:16">37:16</a> Ilungile intwana elinayo ilungisa, Kunentabalala abanayo abangendawo abaninzi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:17">37:17</a> Ngokuba iingalo zabangendawo ziya kwaphulwa; NguYehova umxhasi wamalungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:18">37:18</a> NguYehova umazi wemihla yabagqibeleleyo, Nelifa labo liya kuba ngunaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:19">37:19</a> Abayi kudana ngexesha lobubi; Baya kuhlutha ngeemini zendlala:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:20">37:20</a> Ngokuba abangendawo bayatshabalala; Iintshaba zikaYehova zinjengobuhle bamadlelo; Ziya kuphela njengomsi, ziphele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:21">37:21</a> Uyaboleka ongendawo, angabuyisi; Ke lona ilungisa liyababala, liphe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:22">37:22</a> Ngokuba abasikelelweyo nguye baya kulidla ilifa ilizwe,  Banqanyulwe abatshabhisiweyo nguye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:23">37:23</a> Amanyathela omfo aqiniswa nguYehova, Ayithande indlela yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:24">37:24</a> Ewile, akayi kuqungquluza, Ngokuba nguYehova umxhasi wesandla sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:25">37:25</a> Ndaka ndamtsha, kungokunje ndimdala; Ukanti andizanga ndilibone ilungisa lishiywa, Nembewu yalo ivukela ukutya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:26">37:26</a> Imihla yonke liyababala, liboleke abanye; Nembewu yalo iyintsikelelo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:27">37:27</a> Suka ebubini, wenze okulungileyo, Uhlale ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:28">37:28</a> Ngokuba uYehova uthanda okusesikweni, Angabashiyi abenceba bakhe; Bagciniwe ngonaphakade: Ke yona imbewu yongendawo iyanqanyulwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:29">37:29</a> Amalungisa aya kulidla ilifa ilizwe, Ahlale kulo ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:30">37:30</a> Umlomo welungisa uxela ubulumko, Nolwimi lwalo luthetha okusesikweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:31">37:31</a> Umyalelo woThixo walo usentliziyweni yalo; Akayi kuhexa amanyathela alo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:32">37:32</a> Ongendawo uyalilalela ilungisa, Ufuna ukulibulala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:33">37:33</a> UYehova akalinikeli esandleni sakhe, Angaligwebi ekuthethweni kwetyala lalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:34">37:34</a> Thembela kuYehova, ugcine indlela yakhe; Wokuphakamisa,  ulidle ilifa ilizwe; Ekunqanyulweni kongendawo wobonela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:35">37:35</a> Ndimbonile ongendawo, oyingqwangangqwili, Exanda njengomthi omilileyo, uluhlaza;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:36">37:36</a> Kwadlula umntu, nanko engasekho; Ndamfuna, akafumaneka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:37">37:37</a> Gcina ogqibeleleyo, ukhangele othe tye; Ngokuba izivela-mva zezomntu woxolo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:38">37:38</a> Ke bona abangendawo batshatyalaliswa kuphele; Izivela-mva zongendawo ziyanqanyulwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:39">37:39</a> Usindiso lwamalungisa luphuma kuYehova; Uligwiba lawo ngexesha lembandezelo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:40">37:40</a> UYehova uyawanceda, awasindise, Awasindise kongendawo,  awasindise, Ngokuba azimela ngaye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:1">38:1</a> Umhobe kaDavide: eyokukhumbuza. Yehova, musa ukundohlwaya unoburhalarhume, Ungandithethisi unobushushu:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:2">38:2</a> Ngokuba iintolo zakho zitshone kum, Sehla kanzima kum isandla sakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:3">38:3</a> Akukho ndawo iphilileyo enyameni yam, ngenxa yokubhavuma kwakho; Akukho kuphila emathanjeni am, ngenxa yezono zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:4">38:4</a> Ngokuba ubugwenxa bam bugqithile entlokweni yam, Bundisinda njengomthwalo onzima.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:5">38:5</a> Iyanuka, iyabhiqiza imivumbo yam, Ngenxa yokumatha kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:6">38:6</a> Ndiyapenapena, ndisibekeke kakhulu; Yonke imini ndihamba-hamba ngezimnyama zokuzila.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:7">38:7</a> Ngokuba kuyatshisa emihlubulweni yam, Akukho ndawo iphilileyo enyameni yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:8">38:8</a> Ndiqobekile, ndityumkile kakhulu; Ndibhongiswa kukugcuma kwentliziyo yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:9">38:9</a> Nkosi yam, uphambi kwakho wonke umnqweno wam, Nokuncwina kwam akusithele kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:10">38:10</a> Iphaphu lam liyabetha, ndiphelelwe ngamandla; Ukukhanya kwamehlo am, nako oko, akukho kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:11">38:11</a> Abandithandayo nowethu bamele mgama ekubethweni kwam,  Nezalamane zam zimi kude.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:12">38:12</a> Bandithiyele abafuna umphefumlo wam; Abangxamele ukuba ndihlelwe bububi bathetha izinto zokweyelisela, Bacamanga inkohliso imini yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:13">38:13</a> Ke mna ndinjengesithulu, andiva; Njengesidenge esingawuvuliyo umlomo waso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:14">38:14</a> Ndinjengomntu ongeva nto, Omlomo ungenakuthethisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:15">38:15</a> Ngokuba ndilindele kuwe, Yehova; Kuya kuphendula wena,  Nkosi yam, Thixo wam,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:16">38:16</a> Ngokuba ndithi, Hleze bandivuyelele Bona abo bangazikhulisayo kum ekutyibilikeni konyawo lwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:17">38:17</a> Ngokuba ndihlalele ukujingxela, Umvandedwa wam uphambi kwam amaxesha onke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:18">38:18</a> Ngokuba ndiya kubuxela ubugwenxa bam; Ndinesithukuthezi ngenxa yesono sam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:19">38:19</a> Ke zona iintshaba zam ziphilile, ziziimfidi; Baninzi abandithiyileyo bexoka;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:20">38:20</a> Abandibuyekeza ngobubi esikhundleni sokulungileyo Bayandichasa, ngenxa yokuphuthuma kwam okulungileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:21">38:21</a> Musa ukundishiya, Yehova; Thixo wam, musa ukuba kude nam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:22">38:22</a> Khawuleza undincede, Nkosi yam, Msindisi wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:1">39:1</a> Kumongameli, kuYedutun. Umhobe kaDavide. Ndathi, Ndiya kuzigcina iindlela zam, Ndingoni ngolwimi lwam; Ndiya kuwugcina ngokuwubopha umlomo wam, Xa ongendawo asephambi kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:2">39:2</a> Ndaba sisidenge, ndathozama, Ndazisulungisa nakokulungileyo; Wagxobha-gxobheka umvandedwa wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:3">39:3</a> Yaba nobushushu intliziyo yam phakathi kwam, Ekucamangeni kwam wavutha umlilo. Ndathetha ke ngolwimi lwam,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:4">39:4</a> Ndathi, Ndazise, Yehova, isiphelo sam, Nomlinganiso wemihla yam, into oyiyo; Mandikwazi ukunqamka kwam, into okuyiyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:5">39:5</a> Yabona, uyenze imihla yam yangangobubanzi besandla; Nobomi bam bunjengento engento phambi kwakho; Ngumphunga nje bonke abantu, nakuba bemi. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:6">39:6</a> Uhamba-hamba umntu enjengesithunzi nje kodwa; Baxokozela ngomphunga nje kodwa; Bafumba, bengazi ukuba ngubani na oya kukuhlanganisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:7">39:7</a> Ngoku ndiya kuthembela kwintoni na, Nkosi yam? Ukulinda kwam kukuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:8">39:8</a> Ndihlangule elukreqweni lwam lonke; Musa ukundimisela ingcikivo yesidenge.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:9">39:9</a> Ndisisidenge, umlomo wam andiwuvuli, Ngokuba oko kwenziwe nguwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:10">39:10</a> Sisuse kum isibetho sakho; Mna ndiyaphela kukutyundyutha kwesandla sakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:11">39:11</a> Wakumthethisa umntu ngezohlwayo ngenxa yobugwenxa,  Uyasonakalisa njengenundu isoya sakhe; Bangumphunga nje kodwa bonke abantu. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:12">39:12</a> Yiva umthandazo wam, Yehova, Kubekele indlebe ukuzibika kwam. Musa ukuthi tu ezinyembezini zam; Ngokuba ndingumphambukeli kuwe, Undwendwe, njengoobawo bonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:13">39:13</a> Bheka phaya, ungandikhangeli, khendincumeze, Ndingekemki ndingabi sabakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:1">40:1</a> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Ndathembela, ndithembele kuYehova, Wathoba, wakuva ukuzibika kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:2">40:2</a> Wandirhola emhadini wentshabalalo, naseludakeni lomgxobhozo, Wazimisa eliweni iinyawo zam, wakuqinisa ukunyathela kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:3">40:3</a> Wabeka emlonyeni wam ingoma entsha, indumiso kuThixo wethu;  Abaninzi bayabona, boyike, Bakholose ngoYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:4">40:4</a> Hayi, uyolo lwendoda emenze uYehova inkoloseko yayo,  Ingabheki kwabagwagwisayo, nakubanxaxhi abanamanga!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:5">40:5</a> Yehova, Thixo wam, wena wenze okuninzi ngemisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo, Nangeengcinga zakho kuthi; Akukho nto inokulinganiswa nawe; Okanye bendiya kuyixela, ndithethe ngayo;  Ke ziyinkohla engenakubalwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:6">40:6</a> Akunanze mbingelelo namnikelo wakudla; Iindlebe zam uzivulile; Akubizi dini linyukayo nadini lasono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:7">40:7</a> Ndaza ndathi, Yabona, Ndiyeza; encwadini esongwayo kubhaliwe ngam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:8">40:8</a> Ukwenza okulikholo kuwe, Thixo wam, ndikunanzile; Nomyalelo wakho usezibilinini zam ngaphakathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:9">40:9</a> Ndashumayela iindaba ezilungileyo zobulungisa ebandleni elikhulu; Yabona, andiwuthintelanga umlomo wam; Yehova, wena uyazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:10">40:10</a> Ubulungisa bakho andibugqumanga phakathi kwentliziyo yam;  Ndakukhankanya ukuthembeka kwakho nosindiso lwakho;  Andiyikhanyelanga inceba yakho nenyaniso yakho ebandleni elikhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:11">40:11</a> Wena, Yehova, akuyi kuzithintela iimfesane zakho kum;  Inceba yakho nenyaniso yakho iya kuhlala indilondoloza.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:12">40:12</a> Ngokuba zindijikele izinto ezimbi, ezide azaba nakubalwa;  Bundifikele ubugwenxa bam, andinakubukhangela; Buninzi kuneenwele zentloko yam; Ndimkelwe yintliziyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:13">40:13</a> Ngamana, Yehova, wandihlangula; Yehova, wakhawuleza wandinceda!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:14">40:14</a> Mabadane babe neentloni kuphele Abazungula umphefumlo wam ukuze bawuphephethe; Mababuye muva bahlazeke</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:15">40:15</a> Mabamangaliswe ngumvuzo wehlazo labo Abathi kum, Tshotsho!  Tshotsho!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:16">40:16</a> Mababe nemihlali bavuye ngawe bonke abakufunayo,  Abaluthandayo usindiso lwakho bahlale besithi, Makenziwe mkhulu uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:17">40:17</a> Mna ke ndilusizana, ndilihlwempu; INkosi iya kundikhumbulela. Umncedi wam nomsindisi wam nguwe; Thixo wam,  musa ukulibala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:1">41:1</a> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Hayi, uyolo lwalowo unyamekela ihlwempu! Ngomhla wobubi uYehova uya kumhlangula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:2">41:2</a> UYehova uya kumlondoloza amgcine, aphile. Kuya kuthiwa unoyolo yena ehlabathini; Ungamnikeli elitheni leentshaba zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:3">41:3</a> UYehova uya kumxhasa elukhukweni lobulwelwe; Uya kuluguqula ukhuko lwakhe lonke esifeni sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:4">41:4</a> Ndithi mna, Yehova, tarhu; Philisa umphefumlo wam, ngokuba ndonile kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:5">41:5</a> Iintshaba zam zithetha kakubi ngam; Zithi, Uya kufa nini na, lidake igama lakhe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:6">41:6</a> Nothe weza kundilunguza, uthetha into ekhohlakeleyo;  Intliziyo yakhe ibutha ubutshinga; Uphuma phandle, abuthethe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:7">41:7</a> Basebezelana ngam bonke abandithiyayo; Bacinga ububi ngam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:8">41:8</a> Bathi, Unanyekwe bubutshijolo, Engoleleyo nje, akayi kubuya avuke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:9">41:9</a> Kwanendoda ebixolelene nam, ebe ndikholose ngayo, Ebisidla isonka sam, indiphakamisele isithende sayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:10">41:10</a> Wena Yehova, ndibabale, undiphakamise, Ndibabuyekeze.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:11">41:11</a> Ndazi ngale nto, ukuba undinonelele, Yokokuba lungenakundidumela utshaba lwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:12">41:12</a> Mna ekugqibeleleni kwam uyandixhasa, Undimisa phambi kwakho ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:13">41:13</a> Makabongwe uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli, kususela kwaphakade kude kuse ephakadeni. Amen, amen.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:1">42:1</a> Kumongameli: eyokuqiqa; eyoonyana bakaKora. Njengexhama elitsalela emifuleni yamanzi, Wenjenjalo ukutsalela kuwe,  Thixo, umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:2">42:2</a> Umphefumlo wam unxanela uThixo, uThixo ophilileyo; Ndiya kufika nini na, ndibonakale ebusweni bukaThixo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:3">42:3</a> Iinyembezi zam zaba kukudla kwam imini nobusuku, Bakuthi kum imihla yonke, Uphi na uThixo wakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:4">42:4</a> Ndikhumbula oku, ndiwuphalazela kum umphefumlo wam,  Ukuhamba kwam nezihlwele ndisiya endlwini kaThixo, Sinezwi lokumemelela nokubulela, siyingxokolo evuyayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:5">42:5</a> Kungani na ukuba usibekeke, mphefumlo wam; Kungani na ukuba ugule ngaphakathi kwam? Lindela kuThixo, ngokuba ndisaya kubuya ndibulele kuye, Olusindiso lobuso bam, noThixo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:6">42:6</a> Thixo wam, umphefumlo wam usibekekile kum; ngenxa yoko ndikhumbula wena Ezweni laseYordan, nakweleHermon, entabeni yeMitsare.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:7">42:7</a> Amanzi anzongonzongo abiza amanzi anzongonzongo ngesandi seengxangxasi zakho; Onke amaza akho alwayo, amaza akho agugumayo, adlule phezu kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:8">42:8</a> Emini uYehova uya kuyiwisela umthetho inceba yakhe,  Nasebusuku ukuvuma ngaye kunam, Ukuthandaza kuThixo wobomi bam.</p>
