 <p><a name="an_42:9">42:9</a> Ndithi ke kuThixo oyingxondorha yam, Undilibele ngani na?  Ndihambelani na ngezimnyama zokuzila ngokuxina kotshaba?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:10">42:10</a> Ngento ephehlayo emathanjeni am, bayandingcikiva abandibandezelayo, Ngokuthi kwabo kum imihla yonke, Uphi na uThixo wakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:11">42:11</a> Kungani na ukuba usibekeke, mphefumlo wam; Kungani na ukuba ugule ngaphakathi kwam? Lindela kuThixo, ngokuba ndisaya kubuya ndibulele kuye, Olusindiso lobuso bam, noThixo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:1">43:1</a> Lithethe ityala lam, Thixo, ubambane ngenxa yam nohlanga olungenanceba; Ndisindise endodeni ekhohlisayo, enobugqwetha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:2">43:2</a> Ngokuba unguThixo oyinqaba yam; undihlambelani na?  Ndihambelani na ngezimnyama zokuzila, ngokuxina kotshaba?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:3">43:3</a> Thuma ukukhanya kwakho nenyaniso yakho, zindikhaphe,  Zindise entabeni yakho engcwele, Naseminqubeni yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:4">43:4</a> Ndoya ke esibingelelweni sikaThixo, KuThixo wovuyo lwam olugcobayo, Ndibulele kuwe ngohadi, Thixo onguThixo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:5">43:5</a> Kungani na ukuba usibekeke, mphefumlo wam? Kungani na ukuba ugule ngaphakathi kwam? Lindela kuThixo, ngokuba ndisaya kubuya ndibulele kuye, Olusindiso lobuso bam, noThixo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:1">44:1</a> Kumongameli: eyoonyana bakaKora: eyokuqiqa. Thixo, sivile ngeendlebe zethu, oobawo basibalisela, Ngomsebenzi owawenza ngemihla yabo, ngemihla yamandulo:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:2">44:2</a> Okokuba isandla sakho sagqogqa iintlanga, sabatyala bona;  Saviva izizwe, sabanabisa bona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:3">44:3</a> Ngokuba abalihluthanga ilizwe ngekrele labo,  Abazisindisanga ngengalo yabo; Sisandla sakho sokunene, nengalo yakho, nokukhanya kobuso bakho; Ngokuba wawunesisa kubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:4">44:4</a> Wena unguKumkani wam, Thixo; Yitsho lubekho usindiso kuYakobi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:5">44:5</a> Ngawe sobangqula abasibandezelayo; Egameni lakho sobagqusha abasukela phezulu kuthi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:6">44:6</a> Ngokuba andikholose ngasaphetha sam; Andisindiswa ngakrele lam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:7">44:7</a> Hayi! Nguwe osisindisayo kwabasibandezelayo, Ubadanise abasithiyileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:8">44:8</a> NgoThixo sidumisa imihla yonke, Sibulele kwigama lakho ngonaphakade. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:9">44:9</a> Noko ke usihlambile, usihlazile, Akwaphuma nemikhosi yethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:10">44:10</a> Usibuyise umva phambi kombandezeli; Abasithiyileyo basiphangile okwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:11">44:11</a> Wasinikela njengeegusha ezidliwayo; Wasichitha-chitha ezintlangeni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:12">44:12</a> Wathengisa ngabantu bakho, akwazuza, Akwalinyusa ixabiso labo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:13">44:13</a> Wasenza isingcikivo kubamelwane bethu, Isigculelo nesicukucezo kwabasijikelezileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:14">44:14</a> Wasenza umzekelo ezintlangeni, Abokuhlunguzelelwa intloko ezizweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:15">44:15</a> Yonke imihla ihlazo lam liphambi kwam, Nokudana kobuso bam kundigubungele,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:16">44:16</a> Ngenxa yezwi lomngcikivi nomnyelisi, Ngenxa yokukhangela kotshaba nomphindezeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:17">44:17</a> Oko konke kusifikele, asikulibalanga wena, Asixokanga emnqophisweni wakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:18">44:18</a> Ayibuyanga umva intliziyo yethu, Ukunyathela kwethu akuthanga gu bucala emendweni wakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:19">44:19</a> Ukuba usityumze endaweni yeempungutye, Usigubungele ngethunzi lokufa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:20">44:20</a> Ukuba besililibele igama loThixo wethu, Sazolulela kuthixo wasemzini izandla zethu,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:21">44:21</a> Ubengayi kuyigoca-goca na uThixo loo nto, Ngokuba ezazi iindawo ezifihlakeleyo zentliziyo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:22">44:22</a> Hayi, Ngenxa yakho sibulawa imihla yonke; Kuthiwa siziigusha zokuxhelwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:23">44:23</a> Vuka, ulaleleni na, Nkosi yam? Qabuka, ungasihlambi kuphele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:24">44:24</a> Ubusitheliselani na ubuso bakho, Ukulibale ukucinezelwa kwethu, nokuxinwa kwethu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:25">44:25</a> Ngokuba usibekeke eluthulini umphefumlo wethu, Sanamathela emhlabeni isisu sethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:26">44:26</a> Khawusuk ume usincede, Usikhulule ngenxa yenceba yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:1">45:1</a> Kumongameli: ngeyeenyibiba. Eyoonyana bakaKora; eyokuqiqa.  Ingoma yeentanda. Intliziyo yam iphuphuma ilizwi elihle,  Ndisithi, Into endiyenzayo isingise kukumkani; Ulwimi lwam lusiba lombhali okhawulezayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:2">45:2</a> Umhle wamhle ngaphezu koonyana babantu; Kugalelwe ubumnandi emlonyeni wakho; Ngenxa yoko ukusikelele uThixo wakho ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:3">45:3</a> Bhinqa ikrele lakho ethangeni, gorha, Bhinqa indili yakho nobungangamela bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:4">45:4</a> Tyhudisa, ukhwele uhambe, unobungangamela bakho, Ngenxa yenyaniso, nolulamo olunobulungisa. Sikuyale ngezinto ezoyikekayo isandla sakho sokunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:5">45:5</a> Iintolo zakho zitsolile; Kuya kuwa izizwe phantsi kwakho;  Zitsolile entliziyweni yeentshaba zokumkani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:6">45:6</a> Itrone yakho, itrone kaThixo, ingunaphakade kanaphakade;  Yintonga ethe tye intonga yobukumkani bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:7">45:7</a> Uthanda ubulungisa, uthiye okungendawo; Ngenxa yoko ukuthambisile uThixo, uThixo wakho, Ngeoli yemihlali ngaphezu kwabalingane bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:8">45:8</a> Ziyimore nehaloti nekasiya iingubo zakho zonke; Emabhotweni eempondo zeendlovu uhadi lukuvuyisile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:9">45:9</a> Kukho iintombi zokumkani phakathi kwabathandekayo bakho;  Ukumkanikazi umi ngasekunene kwakho, Enxibe igolide ecikizekileyo yakwaOfire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:10">45:10</a> Yiva, ntombi, ubone, uthobe indlebe yakho, Ubalibale abantu bakowenu, nendlu kayihlo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:11">45:11</a> Akubunqwenela ubunzwakazi bakho ukumkani, Woqubuda kuye,  ngokuba eyinkosi yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:12">45:12</a> Intombi enguTire, izityebi zabantu, Ziya kukuncekelela ngomnikelo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:13">45:13</a> Bubuyokoyoko bodwa intombi yokumkani kweliphakathi igumbi.  Isambatho sayo sesilukwe igolide.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:14">45:14</a> Isiwa kukumkani ineengubo ezimfakamfele; Ziyilandela iintombi ezingowayo, Zisiwa kuwe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:15">45:15</a> Zisiwa ngovuyo nangomgcobo, Zingene ebhotweni lokumkani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:16">45:16</a> Endaweni yooyihlo iya kuba ngoonyana bakho; Uya kubamisa babe ngabathetheli ehlabathini lonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:17">45:17</a> Ndiya kulikhankanya igama lakho kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana zonke; Ngenxa yoko izizwe ziya kubulela kuwe ngonaphakade kanaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:1">46:1</a> Kumongameli: eyoonyana bakaKora; ngeyeentombi. Ingoma.  UThixo ulihlathi, uligwiba kuthi; Ezimbandezelweni ufumaneke eluncedo kunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:2">46:2</a> Ngenxa yoko asoyiki ekuphendukeni kwehlabathi,  Ekudilikeleni kweentaba esazulwini solwandle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:3">46:3</a> Makagqume alephuze amanzi alo, Iintaba zinyikime ngokukratsha kwalo. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:4">46:4</a> Kukho umlambo ozibhaxa zivuyisa umzi kaThixo, Ingcwele yeminquba yOsenyangweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:5">46:5</a> UThixo uphakathi kwawo, awushukunyiswa; UThixo uyawunceda kwasekuzeni kokusa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:6">46:6</a> Ziyaxokozela iintlanga, ziyashukuma izikumkani: Ukhupha izwi lakhe, linyibilike ihlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:7">46:7</a> UYehova wemikhosi unathi, Ingxonde yethu nguThixo kaYakobi.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:8">46:8</a> Yizani nikhangele imisebenzi kaYehova: Owenze iziphanziso ehlabathini;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:9">46:9</a> Ulophelisa iimfazwe kude kuse eziphelweni zehlabathi;  Waphula isaphetha, angqumze umkhonto, Atshise iinqwelo zokulwa ngomlilo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:10">46:10</a> Yekani, nazi ukuba ndinguThixo mna. Ndiya kuphakanyiswa ezintlangeni, ndiya kuphakanyiswa ehlabathini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:11">46:11</a> UYehova wemikhosi unathi, Ingxonde yethu nguThixo kaYakobi. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:1">47:1</a> Kumongameli; eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe. Nonke zizwe,  bethani izandla, Dumani kuThixo ngezwi lokumemelela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:2">47:2</a> Ngokuba uYehova Osenyangweni uyoyikeka; Ngukumkani omkhulu ehlabathini lonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:3">47:3</a> Uzikhandanisela phantsi kwethu izizwe, Izizwe phantsi kweenyawo zethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:4">47:4</a> Usinyulela ilifa lethu, Iqhayiya likaYakobi awamthandayo.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:5">47:5</a> UThixo unyukile, kudunywa; Unyukile uYehova, kuhlokoma isigodlo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:6">47:6</a> Mbetheleni uhadi uThixo, mbetheleni, Mbetheleni uhadi uKumkani wethu, mbetheleni!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:7">47:7</a> Ngokuba uKumkani wehlabathi lonke nguThixo; Mbetheleni ngeyokuqiqa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:8">47:8</a> UThixo nguKumkani weentlanga; UThixo uhleli etroneni yakhe engcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:9">47:9</a> Amanene ezizwe ahlanganisene, Abantu boThixo ka-Abraham;  Ngokuba iingweletshetshe zehlabathi zezikaThixo; Unyusiwe kakhulu yena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:1">48:1</a> Ingoma. Umhobe. Eyoonyana babaKora. Mkhulu uYehova,  engowokudunyiswa kunene Emzini kaThixo wethu, entabeni yakhe engcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:2">48:2</a> Intle ukuphakama kwayo, yimihlali yehla bathi lonke Intaba yaseZiyon, intlomo yasentla, Umzi woKumkani omkhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:3">48:3</a> UThixo, ezingxandeni zawo ezinde, Wazelwa ukuba yingxonde.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:4">48:4</a> Kuba nabo ookumkani babenqophisene, Bawela beza kunye;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:5">48:5</a> Bakuthi ukubona, abakhuluma; Bakhwankqa, babaleka buphuthuphuthu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:6">48:6</a> Babanjwa khona kukuthuthumela, Kukuzibhijabhija njengozalayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:7">48:7</a> Ngomoya wasempumalanga Uyazivitha iinqanawa zaseTarshishe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:8">48:8</a> Njengoko sikuvileyo, sibone kunjalo Emzini kaYehova wemikhosi, emzini kaThixo wethu: UThixo uyawuzinzisa ngonaphakade. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:9">48:9</a> Sayikhumbula, Thixo, inceba yakho Phakathi kwetempile yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:10">48:10</a> Njengoko linjalo igama lakho, Thixo, Lunjalo udumiso lwakho, Kwesa eziphelweni zehlabathi; Isandla sakho sokunene sizele bubulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:11">48:11</a> Mayivuye intaba yaseZiyon, Agcobe amagxamesi akwaYuda,  Ngenxa yezigwebo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:12">48:12</a> Yijikelezeni iZiyon, niyizunguleze; Zibaleni iinqaba zayo ezinde.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:13">48:13</a> Gqalani ungqameko lomsele wayo; Candani ezingxandeni zayo ezinde; Ukuze nibalisele isizukulwana esizayo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:14">48:14</a> Ukuba lo Thixo nguThixo wethu ngonaphakade kanaphakade,  Yena uya kusikhapha kude kuse ekufeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:1">49:1</a> Kumongameli: eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe. Yivani oku, nina nonke zizwe; Bekani indlebe, nina nonke, bemi beli phakade,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:2">49:2</a> Nina nyana boluntu, nani nyana bamadoda, Nina zityebi, nani mahlwempu kunye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:3">49:3</a> Umlomo wam uza kuthetha ubulumko; Nokucamanga kwentliziyo yam kukuqonda.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:4">49:4</a> Ndiya kuyithobela emzekelisweni indlebe yam, Ndiya kuyivulela ngohadi intsonkotha yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:5">49:5</a> Ndoyikelani na emihleni yobubi, Xa ubugwenxa babandibambisayo bundijikelayo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:6">49:6</a> Abo bakholose ngemfuyo yabo, Baqhayisa ngobuninzi bobutyebi babo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:7">49:7</a> Akukho bani unokukhulula umzalwana; Akanakumnika uThixo isicamagusho ngaye</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:8">49:8</a> (Sinqabile isikhululo somphefumlo wabo, Masincanywe ngonaphakade),</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:9">49:9</a> Sokuba ahlale esidla ubomi ngamaxesha onke, Angasiboni isihogo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:10">49:10</a> Ngokuba ubona izilumko zibhubha, Bedaka kunye abanyabileyo nezityhakala, Bayishiye nabanye imfuyo yabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:11">49:11</a> Imbilini yabo ithi izindlu zabo zingunaphakade. Iminquba yabo ikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana; Bayithiya imihlaba yabo ngamagama abo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:12">49:12</a> Ke umntu enobuhandiba akanakuhlala, Ufana neenkomo ezi zitshabalalayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:13">49:13</a> Yiyo le indlela yabanyabileyo, Neyabo babalandelayo,  bekholiswa ngumlomo wabo. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:14">49:14</a> Babuthe ngokweegusha kwelabafileyo; Ukufa kuyabalusa;  Abathe tye bayabanyathela kwakusa; Isithomo sabo abo siyonakala kwelabafileyo, singabi nandawo yakuhlala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:15">49:15</a> Kodwa uThixo uya kuwukhulula umphefumlo wam esandleni selabafileyo, Ngokuba eya kundithabatha. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:16">49:16</a> Musa ukoyika, yakuba sisityebi indoda, Bakwanda ubuqaqawuli bendlu yayo:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:17">49:17</a> Ngokuba ekufeni kwayo ayiyi kuthabatha nento, Aluyi kuhla emva kwayo uzuko lwayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:18">49:18</a> Nakuba umntu ekudleni kwakhe ubomi ebewusikelela umphefumlo wakhe, Bekudumisa ngokuzichwayithisa kwakho,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:19">49:19</a> Uya kuya noko esizukulwaneni sooyise; Abayikukubona ukukhanya naphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:20">49:20</a> Ke umntu onobuhandiba, abe engaqondi, Ufana neenkomo ezi zitshabalalayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:1">50:1</a> Umhobe ka-Asafu. UThixo, uThixo uYehova uyathetha;  Uyalibiza ihlabathi, ethabathela ekuphumeni kwelanga esisa ekutshoneni kwalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:2">50:2</a> EZiyon, ukuphela kweenzwana, Uyakhazimla uThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:3">50:3</a> Uyeza uThixo wethu, akayi kuthi cwaka. Kudla umlilo phambi kwakhe, Ngeenxa zonke kuye sisaqhwithi esikhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:4">50:4</a> Ubiza izulu phezulu, Nehlabathi, ukuba agwebe phakathi kwabantu bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:5">50:5</a> Uthi, Bahlanganiseleni kum abam benceba, Abenze umnqophiso nam ngombingelelo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:6">50:6</a> Izulu lixela ubulungisa bakhe, Ngokuba uThixo eza kugweba yena. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:7">50:7</a> Yivani, bantu bam, ndithethe; Sirayeli, ndiqononondise kuwe; NdinguThixo, uThixo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:8">50:8</a> Andikohlwayi ngenxa yemibingelelo yakho, Namadini akho anyukayo aphambi kwam amaxesha onke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:9">50:9</a> Andiyi kuthabatha zinkunzi zankomo endlwini yakho,  Nazinkunzi zabhokhwe esibayeni sakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:10">50:10</a> Ngokuba zezam zonke iinyamakazi zehlathi, Neenkomo ezisezintabeni eziliwaka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:11">50:11</a> Iintaka zonke zasezintabeni ndiyazazi, Nento edakasa endle inam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:12">50:12</a> Ukuba bendilambile, ndibe ndingayi kukuxelela; Ngokuba lelam elimiweyo nenzaliseko yalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:13">50:13</a> Ndidle inyama yeenkunzi eziziimbalasane na? Ndisele igazi leenkunzi zeebhokhwe na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:14">50:14</a> Bingelela kuYehova umbulelo, Uzizalise kOsenyangweni izibhambathiso zakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:15">50:15</a> Ubize mna ngemini yembandezelo, Ndikuhlangule, undizukise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:16">50:16</a> Ke kongendawo uthi uThixo, Useke phi na wena ukuxela ummiselo wam, Uwuphathe ngomlomo wakho umnqophiso wam,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:17">50:17</a> Uyithiyile nje intethiso wena, Uwaphose nje amazwi am emva kwakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:18">50:18</a> Xa ubona isela, ukholana nalo, Wabelane nabakrexezi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:19">50:19</a> Umlomo wakho uwuyekela ebubini; Ulwimi lwakho luthungela inkohliso;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:20">50:20</a> Uthi uhlale uthethe ngomzalwana wakho, Uhlaze umntwana kanyoko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:21">50:21</a> Uzenzile ezo nto, ndathi tu, Waba ndinjengawe. Ndiya kukohlwaya ndizicwangcise emehlweni akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:22">50:22</a> Khaniqonde ke oko, nina bamlibalayo uThixo, Hleze ndiqwenge, kungabikho uhlangulayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:23">50:23</a> Obingelela umbulelo uyandizukisa, Alungise indlela,  Endombonisa kuyo usindiso lukaThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:1">51:1</a> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide: ekuzeni kukaNatan umprofeti kuye, emveni kokuba ebengene uBhatshebha. Tarhu, Thixo,  ngokwenceba yakho! Ngokobuninzi benceba yakho, cima ukreqo lwam!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:2">51:2</a> Ndixovule kunene, busuke ubugwenxa bam, Undihlambulule esonweni sam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:3">51:3</a> Ngokuba ndiyalwazi mna ukreqo lwam, Nesono sam siphambi kwam ngamaxesha onke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:4">51:4</a> Ndonile kuwe, kuwe wedwa, Ndenza okubi emehlweni akho;  Ukuze ube lilungisa ekuthetheni kwakho, Ucace ekugwebeni kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:5">51:5</a> Uyabona, ndizalelwe ebugwenxeni, Ndakhawulwa nguma esonweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:6">51:6</a> Uyabona, ufuna inyaniso ezintsweni, Esitheni undazisa ubulumko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:7">51:7</a> Ndihlambulule isono ngehisope, ndihlambuluke; Ndixovule,  ndibe mhlophe kunekhephu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:8">51:8</a> Ndivise imihlali nemivuyo, Agcobe amathambo owacolileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:9">51:9</a> Sithelisa ubuso bakho ezonweni zam, Ubucime bonke ubugwenxa bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:10">51:10</a> Dala phakathi kwam, Thixo, intliziyo ehlambulukileyo,  Uhlaziye umoya oqinisekileyo phakathi kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:11">51:11</a> Musa ukundilahla ebusweni bakho, UMoya wakho oyiNgcwele ungamsusi kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:12">51:12</a> Buyisela kum imihlali yosindiso lwakho, Undixhase ngomoya wentumekelelo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:13">51:13</a> Ndobafundisa abangendawo iindlela zakho, Babuyele kuwe aboni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:14">51:14</a> Ndihlangule emagazini, Thixo, Thixo ondisindisayo;  Lomemelela ngobulungisa bakho ulwimi lwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:15">51:15</a> Nkosi yam, vula imilebe yomlomo wam, Uyixele indumiso yakho umlomo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:16">51:16</a> Ngokuba akunanze mibingelelo, bendiya kukunika; Akalikholo kuwe amadini anyukayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:17">51:17</a> Imibingelelo kaThixo ngumoya owaphukileyo, Intliziyo eyaphukileyo, etyumkileyo, Thixo, akuyi kuyidela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:18">51:18</a> Yenzele okulungileyo iZiyon ngokukholekileyo kuwe; Yakha iindonga zeYerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:19">51:19</a> Kuya kwandula ukuba mnandi kuwe imibingelelo yobulungisa,  amadini apheleleyo; Ziya kwandula ukunyuswa iinkunzi ezintsha zeenkomo esibingelelweni sakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:1">52:1</a> Kumongameli. Eyokuqiqa: ekaDavide: oko uDowegi umEdom waya waxelela uSawule, wathi kuye, UDavide ungene endlwini ka-Ahimeleki. Uqhayiselani na ngobubi, wena gorha? Inceba kaThixo ikho imihla yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:2">52:2</a> Ulwimi lwakho lucinga ukweyelisela, Njengesitshetshe sokuguya iindevu esiloliweyo, wena mkhohlisi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:3">52:3</a> Uthanda okubi kunokulungileyo; Ubuxoki, kunokuthetha ubulungisa. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:4">52:4</a> Uthanda onke amazwi aginyayo, Lulwimindini lukhohlisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:5">52:5</a> Naye uThixo uya kukudiliza kuphele; Uva kukuxwila,  akuncothule ententeni, Akudonyule ezweni labaphilileyo.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:6">52:6</a> Obona amalungisa, oyike, Amhleke, athi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:7">52:7</a> Nanko umfo ongamenzanga igwiba lakhe uThixo, Owakholosa ngobuninzi bobutyebi bakhe, Waba nengcwangu ekweyeliseleni kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:8">52:8</a> Ke mna ndinjengomnquma oluhlaza endlwini kaThixo;  Ndikholose ngenceba kaThixo ngonaphakade kanaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:9">52:9</a> Ndiya kubulela kuwe ngonaphakade, kuba ukwenzile oku; Ndiya kuthemba igama lakho, ngokuba lilungile, phambi kwabenceba bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:1">53:1</a> Kumongameli: ngeyokhuzo. Eyokuqiqa; ekaDavide. Sithi isidenge entliziyweni yaso, Akukho Thixo. Bonakalisile,  balisikizi ngobugqwetha babo; Akukho wenza okulungileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:2">53:2</a> UThixo esemazulwini uqondele koonyana babantu, Ukubona ukuba ukho na oqiqayo, Ofuna uThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:3">53:3</a> Bonke babuye umva, bayimbozisa bephelele; Akukho wenza okulungileyo, Akukho nokuba abe mnye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:4">53:4</a> Abanakwazi na abasebenzi bobutshinga, Abathi, bebadla abantu bam, bathi badla isonka, Bangamnquli uThixo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:5">53:5</a> Apho bankwantya benkwantyile, phofu kungekho nto inkwantyisayo; Ngokuba uThixo wawathi saa amathambo omngqingi wakho; Wabadanisa, ngokuba uThixo ebebacekisile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:6">53:6</a> Akwaba bekuvela eZiyon ukusindiswa kwamaSirayeli!  Ekubuyiseni kukaThixo abantu bakhe ekuthinjweni, Wogcoba uYakobi, avuye uSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:1">54:1</a> Eyokubethelwa ngezinto ezineentambo. Kumongameli.  Eyokuqiqa. EkaDavide: ekufikeni kwabaseZifi, bathi kuSawule,  UDavide akazimele phakathi kwethu na? Thixo, ndisindise ngegama lakho, Uligwebe ityala lam ngobugorha bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:2">54:2</a> Thixo, yiva umthandazo wam; Wabekele indlebe amazwi omlomo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:3">54:3</a> Ngokuba abasemzini basukela phezulu kum,  Nabanobungqwangangqwili bafuna umphefumlo wam; Abammisi uThixo phambi kwabo. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:4">54:4</a> Yabona, uThixo ngumncedi wam; INkosi yam ikwabasekela umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:5">54:5</a> Uya kubuyisela ububi kwabandilalelayo; Ngenyaniso yakho babhangise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:6">54:6</a> Ndiya kubingelela kuwe ngokuqhutywa yintliziyo; Ndiya kubulela kwigama lakho, Yehova, kuba lilungile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:7">54:7</a> Ngokuba lindihlangule embandezelweni yonke; Iliso lam libonela iintshaba zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:1">55:1</a> Kumongameli. Eyokubethelwa ngezinto ezineentambo.  Eyokuqiqa: ekaDavide. Wubekele indlebe umthandazo wam, Thixo,  Musa ukuzifihla esikhungweni sam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:2">55:2</a> Ndibazele indlebe undiphendule. Ndiyaphaphatheka ekucamngceni kwam, ndincwine,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:3">55:3</a> Ngenxa yelizwi lotshaba, Ngenxa yokuxinzelelwa phantsi ngabangendawo; Ngokuba zindiqengqela ubutshinga, Ziyandisukela ngomsindo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:4">55:4</a> Intliziyo yam iyazibhija-bhija phakathi kwam; Izothuso zokufa zindiwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:5">55:5</a> Ukoyika nokuthuthumela kundingene; Ndigutyungelwe kukududuzela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:6">55:6</a> Ndathi, Andaba bendinamaphiko njengehobe! Bendiya kubaleka ndiye ndihlale!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:7">55:7</a> Nanko ndibalekela kude, Ndilalise entlango. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:8">55:8</a> Bendiya kukhawuleza, ndisinde Emoyeni ovuthuzayo naseluqhwitheleni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:9">55:9</a> Tshabalalisa, Nkosi yam, yahlula ulwimi lwazo; Ngokuba ndibone ukugonyamela nokubambana phakathi komzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:10">55:10</a> Imini nobusuku bajikeleza ezindongeni zawo; Ubutshinga nokwaphula kuphakathi kwawo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:11">55:11</a> Ukweyelisela kuphakathi kwawo; Endaweni yembutho yawo akusuki ukuxinezela nokukhohlisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:12">55:12</a> Ngokuba asilutshaba olu lundingcikivayo; Bendiya kukuthwala oko. Asingondithiyileyo lo uzikhulisayo kum; Bendiya kusithela kuye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:13">55:13</a> Nguwe, mntu ubungumlingane wam, Ikholwane lam endazana nalo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:14">55:14</a> Ebesicweya kamnandi, Siye endlwini kaThixo silihlokondiba eligcobayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:15">55:15</a> Ukufa makubaqubule, Mabehle baye kwelabafileyo besaphilile; Ngokuba ububi busemizini yabo phakathi kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:16">55:16</a> Mna ndinqula uThixo; UYehova uya kundisindisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:17">55:17</a> Ngokuhlwa, nakusasa, nasemini enkulu ndiya kucamngca,  ndincwine; Uya kuliva izwi lam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:18">55:18</a> Uwukhulula umphefumlo wam unoxolo, ukuze bangasondeli kum,  Ngokuba baninzi abandichasayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:19">55:19</a> UThixo uya kuva, abaphendule, Uselokwamandulo ehleli,  (Phakamisani.) Abo bangenanguquko, Bangamoyikiyo uThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:20">55:20</a> Babasa isandla abaxolelene nabo; Bahlambela umnqophiso wabo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:21">55:21</a> Ubuthelezi njengamasi umlomo wabo, Ke yimfazwe intliziyo yabo. Athambile amazwi abongaphezu kweoli, Kanti aziintlangothi zekrele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:22">55:22</a> Umthwalo wakho wulahlele kuYehova; yena wokuzimasa; Akayi kuliyekela ilungisa lishukunyiswe naphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:23">55:23</a> Wena ke, Thixo, uya kubahlisela emngxunyeni wesihogo.  Abantu bamagazi nenkohliso abayi kuyiqingathisa imihla yabo; Ke mna ndikholose ngawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:1">56:1</a> Kumongameli; ngeyehobe elithe cwaka phakathi kwabakude.  EkaDavide. Eliligugu. Ukubanjwa kwakhe ngamaFilisti eGati.  Ndibabale, Thixo, ngokuba abantu bendizonda; Bandixinile,  besilwa yonke imini;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:2">56:2</a> Abandilalelayo bandizonda yonke imini, Ngokuba baninzi abalwa nam beziphakamisile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:3">56:3</a> Mhlana ndinxunguphalayo mna, Ndokholosa ngawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:4">56:4</a> Ndiya kulidumisa ngoThixo ilizwi lakhe, Ndikholose ngoThixo, ndingoyiki; Inokundenza ntoni na inyama?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:5">56:5</a> Yonke imini bayawaphambanisa amazwi am; Zingam zonke iingcinga zabo zobubi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:6">56:6</a> Baqukene, babonisele, Bona bagcine izithende zam, Ngokokuba belinde umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:7">56:7</a> Bengamatshinga nje, bosinda na? Zihlise ngomsindo izizwe,  Thixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:8">56:8</a> Ukuphalaphala kwam ukubhalile wena; Yitha iinyembezi zam entsubeni yakho; Azisencwadini yakho na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:9">56:9</a> Ziya kubuya umva ke iintshaba zam, mhlana ndibizayo;  Ndiyakwazi oku, ukuba uThixo unam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:10">56:10</a> Ndilidumisa ngoThixo ilizwi, Ndilidumisa ngoYehova ilizwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:11">56:11</a> Ndikholose ngoThixo, ndingoyiki; Unokundenza ntoni na umntu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:12">56:12</a> Ziphezu kwam, Thixo, izibhambathiso zakho; Ndiya kuyizalisa kuwe imibingelelo yombulelo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:13">56:13</a> Ngokuba uwuhlangule ekufeni umphefumlo wam, Iinyawo zam ekukhubekeni, Ukuba ndihambe phambi koThixo Ekukhanyeni kobomi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:1">57:1</a> Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi. EkaDavide. Eliligugu:  ekumbalekeni kwakhe uSawule emqolombeni. Ndibabale, Thixo,  ndibabale; Ngokuba uzimela ngawe umphefumlo wam; Ndizimela esithunzini samaphiko akho, Kude kudlule inkxwaleko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:2">57:2</a> Ndinqula uThixo Osenyangweni, UThixo ondifezelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:3">57:3</a> Uya kuthuma esemazulwini andisindise, Emngcikiva nje ondizondayo; (Phakamisani.) UThixo uya kuthuma inceba yakhe nenyaniso yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:4">57:4</a> Umphefumlo wam uphakathi kweengonyama; Ndiya kulala phantsi nabafutha umlilo, Oonyana babantu abamazinyo aziintshuntshe neentolo, Ulwimi lwabo lulikrele elibukhali.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:5">57:5</a> Ziphakamisele ngaphezu kwamazulu, Thixo, Lube phezu kwehlabathi lonke uzuko lwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:6">57:6</a> Isibatha basilungisele iinyawo zam; Bawugobile umphefumlo wam; Bandimbela isihogo, Beyela kuso ngokwabo. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:7">57:7</a> Izimasekile intliziyo yam, Thixo, izimasekile intliziyo yam; Ndiya kuvuma, ndiya kubetha uhadi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:8">57:8</a> Vuka, luzuko lwam! Vukani, mrhubhe nohadi! Ndiya kusiphangela isifingo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:9">57:9</a> Ndiya kubulela kuwe phakathi kwezizwe, Nkosi yam; Ndiya kukubethela uhadi phakathi kwezizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:10">57:10</a> Ngokuba inkulu, yada yaya ezulwini, inceba yakho; Yada yesa esibhakabhakeni inyaniso yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:11">57:11</a> Ziphakamisele ngaphezu kwezulu, Thixo, Lube phezu kwehlabathi lonke uzuko lwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:1">58:1</a> Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi. EkaDavide. Eliligugu.  Yinene na kodwa ukuba nithetha ubulungisa, nina bothixo?  Nigweba oonyana babantu ngokuthe tye?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:2">58:2</a> Hayi, entliziyweni nenza ngobugqwetha; Ezweni nilinganisela ukugonyamela kwezandla zenu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:3">58:3</a> Abangendawo baphambukile kwasesizalweni; Bandwendwile kwasesiswini abathethi bamanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:4">58:4</a> Banobuhlungu obunjengobuhlungu benyoka, Njengephimpi elizenza isithulu, elivingca indlebe yalo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:5">58:5</a> Ukuze lingaliva izwi labanyangi, Lababopha ngomabophe,  beziingcibi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:6">58:6</a> Thixo, yaphula amazinyo abo emlonyeni wabo; Amabamba eengonyama ezintsha wavithe, Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:7">58:7</a> Mabaphalale njengamanzi equkuqela; Akuxuna iintolo zakhe,  mazinge zicutshiwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:8">58:8</a> Mababe njengenkumba ehamba inyibilika, Njengemva-mbilini yomfazi, engalibonanga ilanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:9">58:9</a> Zingekaziva iintsasa iimbiza zenu, Nokuba ikrwada inyama,  nokuba iza kuvuthwa, uyayiqweqwedisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:10">58:10</a> Liya kuvuya ilungisa, lakuyibona impindezelo; Liya kuzihlamba iinyawo zalo egazini longendawo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:11">58:11</a> Athi umntu, Inene, ilungisa linesiqhamo; Inene, ukho uThixo ogwebayo ehlabathini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:1">59:1</a> Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi. EkaDavide. Eliligugu:  ekuthumeleni kukaSawule, bayilinda indlu ukuba bambulale.  Ndihlangule ezintshabeni zam, Thixo wam, Ndise engxondeni kwabasukela phezulu kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:2">59:2</a> Ndihlangule kubasebenzi bobutshinga; Ndisindise ebantwini abanamagazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:3">59:3</a> Ngokuba nabo bewulalela umphefumlo wam; Baqukana ngam abanamandla, Kungekho lukreqo kum, kungekho sono kum, Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:4">59:4</a> Ndingenabugwenxa nje, bagidime baxhoba. Vuka,  undikhawulele, ubone.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:5">59:5</a> Wena Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Thixo kaSirayeli, Phapha,  uzivelele zonke iintlanga; Musa ukubayeka bonke abanginizayo bengabagqithi. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:6">59:6</a> Bayabuya ngokuhlwa, bayavungama njengezinja,  Bawuhamba-hambe umzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:7">59:7</a> Nabo belephuza amagwebu ngomlomo; Ngamakrele emlonyeni wabo; Ngokuba bathi, Kuva bani na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:8">59:8</a> Wena, Yehova, uyabahleka, Uyazigculela zonke iintlanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:9">59:9</a> Mandla am, ndiva kulindela kuwe; Ngokuba uThixo uyingxonde yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:10">59:10</a> UThixo wam uya kundikhawulela ngenceba yakhe; UThixo uya kundibonisa abandilaleleyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:11">59:11</a> Musa ukubabulala, hleze balibale abantu bakowethu;  Babhadulise ngamandla akho, ubawise, Ngweletshetshe yethu,  Nkosi yethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:12">59:12</a> Isono somlomo wabo lilizwi lemilebe yomlomo wabo;  Mababanjiswe likratshi labo, Nangenxa yokushwabula nokuhanahanisa abakuthethayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:13">59:13</a> Bagqibe ngobushushu; gqiba, bangabi sabakho; Baqonde ukuba uThixo ngumlawuli kwaYakobi, Wesa eziphelweni zehlabathi.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:14">59:14</a> Bayabuya ngokuhlwa, bayavungama njengezinja,  Bawuhamba-hambe umzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:15">59:15</a> Bona babhadulela ukudla; Ukuba bathe abahlutha, balala apho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:16">59:16</a> Ke mna, ndiya kuvuma ngamandla akho, Ndimemelele kwakusasa ngenceba yakho, Kuba ubuyingxonde kum, Nendawo endisabela kuyo ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:17">59:17</a> Mandla am, ndiya kukubethela uhadi; Ngokuba uThixo yingxonde yam, nguThixo wam onenceba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:1">60:1</a> Kumongameli; ngeyenyibiba yesingqino. Eliligugu.  EkaDavide. Eyokufundisa: ekulweni kwakhe nama-Aram phakathi kweMilambo nama-Aram aseTsobha; wabuya uYowabhi, wawabulala amaEdom emfuleni wetyuwa, amawaka alishumi elinamabini.  Thixo,  usihlambile, wasichitha, Waqumba; ngamana wasibuyisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:2">60:2</a> Ulinyikimisile ilizwe, ulikrazule; Philisa iintanda zalo ngokuba lishukuma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:3">60:3</a> Ubabonisile abantu bakho into elukhuni, Usiseze iwayini ehexisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:4">60:4</a> Ubanike ibhanile abakoyikayo, Ukuba bayiphakamise ngenxa yenyaniso. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:5">60:5</a> Ukuze zihlangulwe iintanda zakho, Sindisa ngesandla sakho sokunene, undiphendule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:6">60:6</a> UThixo uthethe engcwele: mandivuyelele, Ndimabe uShekem,  ndiyilinganisele intili yaseSukoti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:7">60:7</a> Ngowam uGiliyadi, ngowam uManase, UEfrayim sisigcina-ntloko sam, UYuda yintonga yam yommiselo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:8">60:8</a> UMowabhi sisitya sam sokuhlambela, Ndiyiphosa kuEdom imbadada yam; Filisti, nkqangaza wena ngam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:9">60:9</a> Ngubani na owondisa emzini wamandla? Ngubani na owondikhaphela kwaEdom?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:10">60:10</a> Asinguwe na, kwawena Thixo, osihlambileyo? Akwaphuma,  Thixo, nemikhosi yethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:11">60:11</a> Sincede kumbandezeli wethu; Alunto yanto usindiso lomntu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:12">60:12</a> NgoThixo siya kweyisa, Wobagqusha yena ababandezeli bethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:1">61:1</a> Kumongameli; eyokubethelwa ngezinto ezineentambo.  EkaDavide. Kuve, Thixo, ukuhlahlamba kwam; Wubazele indlebe umthandazo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:2">61:2</a> Ndidanduluka kuwe ndisesiphelweni sehlabathi, ekutyhafeni kwentliziyo yam; Ndikhaphele eweni elisemalengalengeni kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:3">61:3</a> Ngokuba ulihlathi lam, Uyinqaba ende eliqele phambi kotshaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:4">61:4</a> Ndiya kuphambukela ententeni yakho ngonaphakade, Ndiya kuzimela ngesithe lamaphiko akho. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:5">61:5</a> Ngokuba wena, Thixo, uzivile izibhambathiso zam; Ubanike ilifa abaloyikayo igama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:6">61:6</a> Uya kongeza imihla emihleni yokumkani; Iminyaka yakhe iya kuba njengezizukulwana ngezizukulwana;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:7">61:7</a> Uya kuhlala ngonaphakade phambi koThixo; Mmisele inceba nenyaniso, ukuba zimlondoloze.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:8">61:8</a> Kukhona ndiya kulibethela uhadi igama lakho ngonaphakade,  Ndizizalise izibhambathiso zam imihla ngemihla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:1">62:1</a> Kumongameli. KuYedutun. Umhobe kaDavide. Uthozamele kuThixo kwaphela umphefumlo wam; Kuvela kuye ukusindiswa kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:2">62:2</a> Nguye kwaphela iliwa lam, umsindisi wam, Ingxonde yam;  andiyi kushukunyiswa kakhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:3">62:3</a> Kunini na nisuka indulumbane emntwini? Kunini na nimncinitha nonke niphela, enjengodonga oluzimkayo,  enjengothango oluwayo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:4">62:4</a> Bagqibe kwelokuba bamtyhale bamsuse ekuphakameni kwakhe kuphele; Bakholene namanga; Basikelela elowo ngomlomo,  embilinini yabo bayatshabhisa. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:5">62:5</a> Thozamela kuThixo yedwa, mphefumlo wam, Ngokuba livela kuye ithemba lam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:6">62:6</a> Nguye kwaphela iliwa lam, umsindisi wam, Ingxonde yam;  andiyi kushukunyiswa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:7">62:7</a> KunoThixo ukusindiswa kwam nozuko lwam; Iliwa lokunqaba kwam nehlathi lam likuThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:8">62:8</a> Kholosani ngaye ngamaxesha onke, nina bantu; Phalazani intliziyo yenu phambi kwakhe. UThixo ulihlathi kuthi.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:9">62:9</a> Bangumphunga kwaphela onyana boluntu, ngamanga oonyana bamadoda; Esikalini bangenyuka, Bangumphunga bephelele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:10">62:10</a> Musani ukukholosa ngokudla abantu, Ningazenzi into engeyanto ngento exhakamfuliweyo. Yakwanda imfuyo, musani ukuyinyamekela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:11">62:11</a> Uthethe nto-nye uThixo, Ezi zinto zimbini ndizivile: Ukuba amandla ngakaThixo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:12">62:12</a> Nenceba yeyakho, Nkosi yam; Ngokuba uyababuyekeza, elowo ngokwezenzo zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:1">63:1</a> Umhobe kaDavide: oko ebesentlango yakwaYuda. Thixo,  unguThixo wam, ndiya kukuquqela kwakusasa, Umphefumlo wam unxanele wena; inyama yam iyakulangazelela Ezweni elingumqwebedu, elibharhileyo, eligenamanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:2">63:2</a> Ndenjenjalo ukukhangela kuwe engcweleni, Ukuba ndibone amandla akho nobuqaqawuli bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:3">63:3</a> Ngokuba inceba yakho ilungile ngaphezu kobomi, Umlomo wam uya kukuncoma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:4">63:4</a> Ndiya kwenjenjalo ukukubonga lo gama ndihleliyo,  Ndiphakamise izandla zam egameni lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:5">63:5</a> Umphefumlo wam uhluthi umongo namanqatha; Ngemilebe yomlomo wam omemelelayo uya kukudumisa umlomo wam,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:6">63:6</a> Ndakukukhumbula emandlalweni wam, Emilindweni yobusuku ndicamanga ngawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:7">63:7</a> Ngokuba uluncedo kum, Ndinokumemelela esithunzini samaphiko akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:8">63:8</a> Umphefumlo wam uthene mbende nawe; Isandla sakho sokunene sindibambile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:9">63:9</a> Ke bona bafuna umphefumlo wam ukuze batshabalale, Baya kutshona kwezisezantsi iindawo zehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:10">63:10</a> Baphalazelwa emandleni ekrele; Baba sisabelo seempungutye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:11">63:11</a> Ke yena ukumkani uya kuvuya ngoThixo; Baya kuqhayisa abo bonke bafunga yena; Ngokuba uya kuvingcwa umlomo wabathetha ubuxoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:1">64:1</a> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Live, Thixo, izwi lam ekukhalazeni kwam; Ekunkwantyiseni kotshaba bulondoloze ubomi bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:2">64:2</a> Ndisithelise egquguleni labanobubi, Ehlokondibeni labasebenzi bobutshinga;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:3">64:3</a> Abalulola njengekrele ulwimi lwabo, Abaxuna iintolo zabo,  amazwi akrakra,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:4">64:4</a> Bamtole ogqibeleleyo besentsithelweni; Bamtola ngesiquphe,  bangoyiki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:5">64:5</a> Bazomelezela ilizwi elibi, Bagqiba kwelokuba bafihle izirhintyelo, Bathi, Singabonwa ngubani na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:6">64:6</a> Baceba ubugqwetha; Baligqibile icebo abalicebileyo;  Imbilini yendoda nentliziyo yayo yinzulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:7">64:7</a> Ke uThixo uyabatola ngotolo; Amanxeba abo abakho ngesiquphe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:8">64:8</a> Baya kukhutyekiswa, lufikele kwabona ulwimi lwabo;  Bayahlunguzela intloko bonke abababonayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:9">64:9</a> Basuka boyike bonke abantu, Bawuxele umsebenzi kaThixo,  Basiqiqe isenzo sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:10">64:10</a> Liya kuvuya ilungisa ngoYehova, lizimele ngaye, Baqhayise bonke abantliziyo zithe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:1">65:1</a> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Ingoma. Ukuthozama kuyindumiso kuwe, Thixo, eZiyon; Sizaliswa kuwe isibhambathiso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:2">65:2</a> Wena mphulaphuli wemithandazo, Iza kuwe inyama yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:3">65:3</a> Zindoyisile nje iindawo zobugwenxa, Ukreqo lwethu uyaluxolela wena ngocamagushelo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:4">65:4</a> Hayi, uyolo lomnyulayo, umsondeze Ukuba ahlale ezintendelezweni zakho! Siya kuzihluthisa ngokulunga kwendlu yakho, Kwetempile yakho engcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:5">65:5</a> Usiphendula ngezenzo ezoyikekayo zobulungisa, Thixo osisindisayo; Nkoloseko yeziphelo zonke zehlabathi, neyolwandle olukude;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:6">65:6</a> Ulozinzisa iintaba ngamandla akhe, Ebhinqe ubugorha;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:7">65:7</a> Ulodambisa ukugquma kweelwandle, ukugquma kwamaza azo,  Nokuxokozela kwezizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:8">65:8</a> Bayayoyika imiqondiso yakho abemi beziphelo zehlabathi.  Umemelelisa ukuvela kokusa nokuhlwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:9">65:9</a> Uwuvelele umhlaba, wawunyela, Wawutyebisa kakhulu. Umjelo kaThixo uzele ngamanzi: Walungisa ingqolowa yabo, ngokuba uwenjenje ukuwulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:10">65:10</a> Useza ihluthe imisele yawo; Unyakamisa imiqela yawo.  Uthambisa ngeziphango; Usikelela izilimo zawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:11">65:11</a> Uwuthwesile umnyaka wokulunga kwakho, Imikhondo yakho itsitsa ukutyeba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:12">65:12</a> Ayatsitsa amakriwa entlango, Iinduli zizibhinqise umgcobo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:13">65:13</a> Amadlelo anxibe imihlambi yeenkomo; Iintili zambethe ingqolowa. Yonke into iyaduma, yonke into iyavuma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:1">66:1</a> Kumongameli. Ingoma. Umhobe. Dumani kuThixo, nonke hlabathi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:2">66:2</a> Lubetheleni uhadi uzuko lwegama lakhe, Mzukiseni,  mdumiseni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:3">66:3</a> Yithini kuThixo, Hayi, ukoyikeka kwemisebenzi yakho! Ngenxa yobuninzi bamandla akho ziya kuhanahanisa kuwe iintshaba zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:4">66:4</a> Lonke ihlabathi liya kukunqula, Bakubethele uhadi;  Balibethele uhadi igama lakho. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:5">66:5</a> Yizani, nibone imisebenzi emikhulu kaThixo, Engowoyikekayo ekwenzeni kwakhe koonyana babantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:6">66:6</a> Waluguqula ulwandle lwayinto eyomileyo; Bawuwela umlambo ngeenyawo; Apho savuya ngaye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:7">66:7</a> Ulolawula ngobugorha bakhe ngonaphakade; Amehlo akhe ayabonisela ezintlangeni; Abaziinjubaqa mabangaziphakamisi.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:8">66:8</a> Mbongeni, zizwe, uThixo wethu, Nivakalise ilizwi lendumiso yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:9">66:9</a> Ulomisa umphefumlo wethu ebomini, Akalunikela unyawo lwethu ekutyibilikeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:10">66:10</a> Ngokuba usicikidile, Thixo; Usinyibilikisile njengokunyibilikiswa kwesilivere;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:11">66:11</a> Usingenise emboniselweni; Ubeke uxinzelelo esinqeni sethu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:12">66:12</a> Ukhwelise abantu entlokweni yethu; Singene emlilweni nasemanzini; Waza wasikhuphela endaweni enendyebo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:13">66:13</a> Ndiya kungena endlwini yakho ndinamadini anyukayo; Ndiya kuzizalisa kuwe izibhambathiso zam,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:14">66:14</a> Eyazivulelayo imilebe yomlomo wam, Owazithethayo umlomo wam ekubandezelweni kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:15">66:15</a> Ndiya kunyusela kuwe amadini anyukayo eemvana ezityebileyo, Ndawonye nesiqhumiso seenkunzi zeegusha; Ndiya kwenza aweenkomo ndawonye naweenkunzi zeebhokhwe.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:16">66:16</a> Yizani, nive, ndinixelele, nonke nina bamoyikayo uThixo,  Oko akwenzele umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:17">66:17</a> Ndadanduluka kuye ngomlomo wam; Kwaye ukubonga kuphantsi kolwimi lwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:18">66:18</a> Ukuba bendisekeleze ubutshinga ngentliziyo yam, INkosi yam ibingayi kuphulaphula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:19">66:19</a> Hayi ke, uThixo uphulaphule, Ulibazele indlebe ilizwi lomthandazo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:20">66:20</a> Makabongwe uThixo, Yena ungawugxothanga umthandazo wam,  Nobubele bakhe kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:1">67:1</a> Kumongameli; eyokubethelwa ngezinto ezineentambo. Umhobe.  Ingoma. Ngamana uThixo wasibabala, wasisikelela, Wabukhanyisa ubuso bakhe kuthi; (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:2">67:2</a> Ukuze yaziwe ehlabathini indlela yakho, Usindiso lwakho ezintlangeni zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:3">67:3</a> Ngamana zabulela izizwe kuwe, Thixo, Zabulela izizwe kuwe zonke ziphela;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:4">67:4</a> Zavuya zamemelela izizwe: Ngokuba uya kugweba phakathi kwezizwe ngokuthe tye, Uzikhaphe izizwe ehlabathini.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:5">67:5</a> Ngamana zabulela izizwe kuwe, Thixo, Zabulela izizwe kuwe zonke ziphela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:6">67:6</a> Umhlaba uyivelisile indyebo yawo; Uya kusisikelela uThixo,  uThixo wethu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:7">67:7</a> Uya kusisikelela uThixo, Zimoyike zonke iziphelo zehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:1">68:1</a> Kumongameli; ekaDavide. Umhobe. Ingoma. Makasuk eme uThixo, zibe ziintsali iintshaba zakhe, Basabe ebusweni bakhe abamthiyayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:2">68:2</a> Njengokuphetshethwa komsi, baphephethe; Njengokunyibilika komthwebeba phambi komlilo, Mabadake ngokunjalo abangendawo ebusweni bukaThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:3">68:3</a> Ke wona amalungisa makavuye, adlamke phambi koThixo, Abe nemihlali, enemivuyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:4">68:4</a> Vumani kuThixo, libetheleni uhadi igama lakhe; Menzeleni umendo ophakamileyo, ulokhwela ecanda ezinkqantosini, Ogama lakhe linguYehova; nidlamke phambi kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:5">68:5</a> Uyise weenkedama, umthetheleli wabahlolokazi, NguThixo ekhayeni lakhe elingcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:6">68:6</a> UThixo nguhlalisa endlwini ababebodwa, Ngukhuphela enywebeni ababanjiweyo; Ngabaziinjubaqa bodwa abahlala kwelibalelelweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:7">68:7</a> Thixo, ekuphumeni kwakho uphambi kwabantu bakho,  Ekunyatheleni kwakho enkangala, (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:8">68:8</a> Lanyikima ihlabathi, Lavuza izulu ebusweni bukaThixo,  ISinayi leya ebusweni bukaThixo, uThixo kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:9">68:9</a> Walitshiza ngemvula eninzi yesisa sakho, Thixo, ilifa lakho; Lakubharha, walizimasa wena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:10">68:10</a> Wahlala khona umhlambi wakho, Wamlungisela olusizana ngokulunga kwakho, Thixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:11">68:11</a> INkosi iya kukhupha izwi elinamandla, Ube mkhulu umkhosi weentokazi ezishumayela iindaba ezilungileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:12">68:12</a> Ookumkani bemikhosi baya kusaba besabile; Intokazi esele ekhaya iya kuwaba amaxhoba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:13">68:13</a> Nakulala phantsi phakathi kweentlanti, Noxelisa amaphiko evukuthu alekwe ngesilivere, Neentsiba zalo ezalekwe ngegolide ebengezelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:14">68:14</a> Ekubadubadubeni kukaSomandla ookumkani kulo, Koba mhlophe ngowekhephu eTsalimon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:15">68:15</a> Yintaba kaThixo intaba yaseBhashan, Yintaba encopho zininzi intaba yaseBhashan.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:16">68:16</a> Niyigxeleshelani na, zintaba zincopho zininzi, Intaba ayinqweneleyo uThixo ukuba ahlale kuyo? Ewe, uYehova uya kuhlala kuyo ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:17">68:17</a> Iinqwelo zokulwa zikaThixo zizigidi, ngamawaka-waka;  INkosi ikuzo; yiSinayi ebungcweleni,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:18">68:18</a> Unyuke waya phezulu, uthimbe abathinjwa, Uthabathe izipho phakathi kwabantu, Naphakathi kwabaziinjubaqa, ukuba ahlale uYehova uThixo khona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:19">68:19</a> Mayibongwe iNkosi; Ithwala imithwalo yethu imihla ngemihla; NguThixo umsindisi wethu. (Phakamisani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:20">68:20</a> Yena uThixo kuthi nguThixo wosindiso, KokukaYehova, iNkosi yethu, ukukhupha ekufeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:21">68:21</a> Kodwa uThixo uya kuyiphalusa intloko yeentshaba zakhe,  Nentloko enesihlwitha yohambayo kwizigqitho zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:22">68:22</a> Yathi iNkosi, Ndiya kuzibuyisa eBhashan, Ndiya kuzibuyisa iintshaba zakho ezinzulwini zolwandle;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:23">68:23</a> Ukuze uziphaluse, unyawo lwakho lusegazini, Nolwimi lwezinja zakho lube nesabelo salo ezintshabeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:24">68:24</a> Bakubona ukunyathela kwakho, Thixo, Ukunyathela koThixo wam, koKumkani wam, esebungcweleni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:25">68:25</a> Phambili ziimvumi, ngasemva ngababethi bohadi, Emacaleni ziintombi ezibetha iingqongqo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:26">68:26</a> Emabandleni bongani uThixo, INkosi, nina basemthonjeni wakwaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:27">68:27</a> Balapho ooBhenjamin, inci yabo, umphathi wabo, Abathetheli bakwaYuda, ihlokondiba labo; Abathetheli bakwaZebhulon,  abathetheli bakwaNafetali.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:28">68:28</a> UThixo wakho wakuwisela umthetho wokuba uqine; Kuqinise,  Thixo, oko usenzeleyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:29">68:29</a> Bevela etempileni yakho eyongamele iYerusalem, Ookumkani mabeze nezithabathaba kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:30">68:30</a> Khalimela amarhamncwa asengcongolweni, Umhlambi weenkunzi eziziimbalasane, kunye namathole ezizwe, Ukuze baziwise benezijungqe zesilivere. Wazibhangisa izizwe eziyithandayo imfazwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:31">68:31</a> Kovela amanono eYiputa; UKushi wozolulela msinya izandla zakhe kuThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:32">68:32</a> Zikumkani zehlabathi, vumani kuThixo, Niyibethele uhadi iNkosi; (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:33">68:33</a> Ekhwela ecanda emazulwini awo amazulu amandulo; Nanko elikhupha ilizwi lakhe, ilizwi elinamandla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:34">68:34</a> Mnikeni amandla uThixo; Buphezu koSirayeli ubungangamsha bakhe; Asesibhakabhakeni amandla akhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:35">68:35</a> UloThixo woyikekayo ezingcweleni zakho. UloThixo kaSirayeli, ubanikayo amandla nokomelela abantu. Makabongwe uThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:1">69:1</a> Kumongameli; ngeyeenyibiba. EkaDavide. Ndisindise, Thixo;  Ngokuba amanzi andifikele, ada eza emphefumlweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:2">69:2</a> Nditshonile eludakeni olunzulu, akukho kuma; Ndingene emmbithini onamanzi, umsinga uyandintywilisela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:3">69:3</a> Ndidiniwe kukudanduluka; womile umqala wam; Aphelile amehlo am; mna ndilindele kuThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:4">69:4</a> Abandithiyayo ngelize baninzi ngaphezu kweenwele zentloko yam; Baninzi abandibangisayo, abaziintshaba zam bexoka; Into endingayiphanganga bathi mandiyibuyise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:5">69:5</a> Thixo, wena uyakwazi ukumatha kwam; Namatyala am akanakugushwa kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:6">69:6</a> Mabangadani ngam abakuthembayo, Nkosi yam, Yehova wemikhosi; Mabangangcikivwa ngam abakufunayo, Thixo kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:7">69:7</a> Ngokuba ndithwele ingcikivo ngenxa yakho; Ihlazo libugqubuthele ubuso bam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:8">69:8</a> Ndingowasemzini kubazalwana bam; Ndingowolunye uhlanga kubantwana bakama:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:9">69:9</a> Ngokuba lindidlile ikhwele ngenxa yendlu yakho: Iingcikivo zabakungcikivayo ziwe phezu kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:10">69:10</a> Mna, umphefumlo wam walila, uzila ukudla; Oko kwaba yingcikivo kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:11">69:11</a> Iingubo zam zaba zezirhwexayo, Ndaba yinto yokuzekelisa kubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:12">69:12</a> Bathetha ngam abahleli esangweni; Ndiyingoma yamanxila.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:13">69:13</a> Ke mna ndithandaza kuwe, Yehova, ngexesha elikholekileyo:  Thixo, ngobuninzi benceba yakho, Ndiphendule ngenyaniso yosindiso lwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:14">69:14</a> Ndihlangule eludakeni, ndingatshoni; Mandihlangulwe kwabandithiyayo nasemimbithini enamanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:15">69:15</a> Mawungandintywiliseli umsinga wamanzi; Ingandiginyi inzulu; Iqula malingandivingceli ngomlomo walo</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:16">69:16</a> Ndiphendule, Yehova, ngokuba ilungile inceba yakho,  Ngangobuninzi bemfesane yakho ndibheke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:17">69:17</a> Musa ukubusithelisa ubuso bakho kumkhonzi wakho, Ngokuba ndibandezelekile; khawuleza undiphendule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:18">69:18</a> Sondela emphefumlweni wam, uwukhulule; Ngenxa yeentshaba zam ndikhulule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:19">69:19</a> Wena uyakwazi ukungcikivwa kwam, nokudaniswa kwam,  nokuhlazwa kwam; Baphambi kwakho bonke abandibandezelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:20">69:20</a> Ingcikivo yaphula intliziyo yam, ndaphantsa ukufa;  Ndathemba ukukhuzwa, akwabakho; Nokuthuthuzelwa, andakufumana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:21">69:21</a> Ukudla bandinika inyongo; Ekunxanweni kwam bandiseza iviniga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:22">69:22</a> Isithebe sabo phambi kwabo masibe ngumgibe; Sibe sisirhintyelo kwabanemasi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:23">69:23</a> Makabe mnyama amehlo abo, bangaboni, Usigxadazelise isinqe sabo amaxesha onke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:24">69:24</a> Baphalazele ngobhavumo lwakho, Kubafikele ukuvutha komsindo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:25">69:25</a> Ingqili yabo mayibe senkangala, Ezintenteni zabo kungahlali mntu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:26">69:26</a> Ngokuba bayamsukela obethwe nguwe, Bancokole ngomvandedwa wobahlabileyo wena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:27">69:27</a> Yongeza ubugwenxa ebugwenxeni babo, Bangangeni ebulungi senibakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:28">69:28</a> Mabacinywe encwadini yobomi, Bangabhalwa namalungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:29">69:29</a> Ke mna ndilusizana, ndinomvandedwa; Usindiso lwakho,  Thixo, malundise engxondeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:30">69:30</a> Ndiya kulidumisa igama likaThixo ngokuvuma, Ndilenze likhulu ngokubulela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:31">69:31</a> Oko kuya kukholeka kuYehova ngaphezu kweenkunzi ezintsha,  Ezineempondo neempuphu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:32">69:32</a> Bebona abalulamileyo, bovuya; Nina bamquqelayo uThixo,  intliziyo yenu mayiphile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:33">69:33</a> Ngokuba uYehova uyaweva amahlwempu, Akabadeli ababanjiweyo bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:34">69:34</a> Malimdumise izulu nomhlaba, Ulwandle nento yonke enambuzelayo kulo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:35">69:35</a> Ngokuba uThixo uya kuyisindisa iZiyon, ayakhe imizi yakwaYuda, Bahlale khona, bayime;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:36">69:36</a> Ilidle ilifa imbewu yabakhonzi bakhe; Bahlale kuyo abalithandayo igama lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:1">70:1</a> Kumongameli; ekaDavide; eyokukhumbuza. Thixo, khawuleza undihlangule; Yehova, khawuleza undincede.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:2">70:2</a> Mabadane babe neentloni abawufunayo umphefumlo wam;  Mababuye umva bahlazeke abananze ukuba ndihlelwe bububi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:3">70:3</a> Mababuye ngenxa yomvuzo wedano labo Abathi, Tshotsho!  Tshotsho!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:4">70:4</a> Mababe nemihlali bavuye ngawe bonke abakuquqelayo;  Abaluthandayo usindiso lwakho Mabahlale besithi, Makenziwe mkhulu uThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:5">70:5</a> Ke mna ndilusizana, ndilihlwempu; Thixo, khawuleza uze kum.  Umncedi wam nomsindisi wam nguwe; Yehova, musa ukulibala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:1">71:1</a> Ndizimela ngawe, Yehova, Mandingaze ndidane naphakade:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:2">71:2</a> Ngobulungisa bakho ndihlangule, ndisize; Ndithobele indlebe yakho, undisindise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:3">71:3</a> Yiba liliwa elilikhaya kum, ndize kulo ngamaxesha onke.  Uwise umthetho wokuba ndisindiswe, Ngokuba ingxondorha yam nemboniselo yam nguwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:4">71:4</a> Thixo wam, ndisize esandleni songendawo, Esandleni sogqwethayo nosisibhovubhovu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:5">71:5</a> Ngokuba ulithemba lam, Nkosi yam, Yehova, Inkoloseko yam kwasebuncinaneni bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:6">71:6</a> Ndixhaswe nguwe kwasesizalweni; Nguwe owandityhobozisayo ezibilinini zikama. Indumiso yam ingawe ngamaxesha onke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:7">71:7</a> Ndinjengesimanga kwabaninzi; Ke wena ulihlathi lam elinqabileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:8">71:8</a> Umlomo wam uya kuzala yindumiso yakho, Sisihombo sakho imini yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:9">71:9</a> Musa ukundilahla ngexesha lobuxhego; Musa ukundishiya akuphela amandla am.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:10">71:10</a> Ngokuba zithetha ngam iintshaba zam; Abawulindayo umphefumlo wam bayacebisana,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:11">71:11</a> Besithi, UThixo umlahlile; Msukeleni nimbambe, ngokuba akukho mhlanguli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:12">71:12</a> Thixo, musa ukuba kude kum; Thixo wam, khawuleza undincede.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:13">71:13</a> Mabadane, bagqitywe, abawuchasayo umphefumlo wam, Bathiwe wambu yingcikivo nehlazo abafuna ukuba ndihlelwe bububi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:14">71:14</a> Ke mna ndiya kuhlala ndilindile, Ndongeze endumisweni yakho yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:15">71:15</a> Umlomo wam uya kubalisa ngemisebenzi yobulungisa bakho,  Neyosindiso lwakho imini yonke, ngokuba ndingawazi amanani ayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:16">71:16</a> Ndiya kuza nemisebenzi yobugorha beNkosi uYehova; Ndiya kukhankanya ubulungisa bakho, bakho wedwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:17">71:17</a> Thixo, undifundisile kwasebuncinaneni bam; Unangoku ndiyayixela imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:18">71:18</a> Thixo, musa ukundishiya kude kuye ebuxhegweni nasezimvini;  Ndide ndiyixele ingalo yakho kwisizukulwana esitsha, Nobugorha bakho kubo bonke abaya kuza.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:19">71:19</a> Thixo, ubulungisa bakho buye bafika phezulu; Wena uzenzayo izinto ezinkulu, Thixo, ngubani na onjengawe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:20">71:20</a> Wena, usibonisileyo iimbandezelo ezininzi ezinobubi, Uya kubuya usiphilise, Ubuye usirhole ezinzonzobileni zamanzi ehlabathi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:21">71:21</a> Uya kubandisa ubukhulu bam, Ubuye wena undithuthuzele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:22">71:22</a> Ndiya kuyibulela nokuyibulela kuwe ngomrhubhe Inyaniso yakho, Thixo wam; Ndiya kukubethela uhadi, Ngcwele kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:23">71:23</a> Uya kumemelela umlomo wam, ndakukubethela uhadi,  Nomphefumlo wam owukhululeyo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:24">71:24</a> Nolwimi lwam luya kuxela ubulungisa bakho imini yonke,  Ngokuba bedanile beneentloni abafuna ukuba ndihlelwe bububi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:1">72:1</a> EkaSolomon. Thixo, mnike ukumkani imigwebo yakho, Mnike unyana wokumkani ubulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:2">72:2</a> Makagwebe ebantwini bakho ngobulungisa, Nakwabaziintsizana zakho ngokwesiko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:3">72:3</a> Iintaba mazibathwalele uxolo abantu, Kwaneenduli zibathwalele ebulungiseni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:4">72:4</a> Makagwebe ityala labaziintsizana ebantwini, Asindise oonyana bamahlwempu, Abatyumze abacudisi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:5">72:5</a> Mabakoyike, ukuhlala elihleliyo ilanga Kwanenyanga,  izizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:6">72:6</a> Makehle njengemvula ehla phezu kotyani obusikwayo,  Njengeziphango, njengemvula emathontsi makhulu, emhlabeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:7">72:7</a> Malityatyambe ngemihla yakhe ilungisa, Nobuninzi boxolo,  ide ingabi sabakho inyanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:8">72:8</a> Makaphathe ubukhosi ethabathela elwandle ase elwandle,  Ethabathela kuwo uMlambo ase eziphelweni zehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:9">72:9</a> Baya kuguqa phambi kwakhe abemi bomqwebedu, Zikhothe uthuli iintshaba zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:10">72:10</a> Ookumkani baseTarshishe nabeziqithi baya kunika iminikelo;  Ookumkani bakwaShebha nabakwaSebha baya kusondeza isithabathaba;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:11">72:11</a> Baqubude kuye bonke ookumkani, Zimkhonze sonke iintlanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:12">72:12</a> Ngokuba uya kulihlangula ihlwempu elizibikayo,  Nabaziintsizana abangenaluncedo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:13">72:13</a> Abenzele inceba abasweleyo nabangamahlwempu; Asindise imiphefumlo yamahlwempu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:14">72:14</a> Akhulule imiphefumlo yawo ekuxinezelweni nasekugonyamelweni; Linqabile emehlweni akhe igazi lawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:15">72:15</a> Uya kuphila anikwe igolide yakwaShebha, Bahlale bemthandazela, Bamsikelele imini yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:16">72:16</a> Makubekho intabalala yengqolowa ezweni, ise encotsheni yeentaba; Ukuqhama kwayo makurhashaze njengeLebhanon;  Mabatyatyambe emizini yabo njengemifuno yomhlaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:17">72:17</a> Malibe ngunaphakade igama lakhe; Malivelise amagatya igama lakhe phambi kwelanga, Bazisikelele ngaye; Mazithi zonke iintlanga ungonoyolo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:18">72:18</a> Makabongwe uYehova uThixo, uThixo kaSirayeli. Ulomenzi wemisebenzi ebalulekileyo yena yedwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:19">72:19</a> Malisikelelwe igama lakhe elizukileyo ngonaphakade, Lizale lonke ihlabathi luzuko lwakhe. Amen, amen.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:20">72:20</a> Iphelile imithandazo kaDavide unyana kaYese.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:1">73:1</a> Umhobe ka-Asafu. Ulungile kwaphela uThixo kuSirayeli,  Kwabantliziyo zinyulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:2">73:2</a> Ke mna, beziphantse ukumka iinyawo zam; Gcwizi ukutyibilika ukunyathela kwam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:3">73:3</a> Ngokuba bendibamonela abaqhayisayo, Ndakukubona ukuphumelela kwabangendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:4">73:4</a> Ngokuba abanazintlungu ekufeni kwabo; Baphilile, batyebile umzimba wabo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:5">73:5</a> Ebubini babantu abakho bona; Abakhathazwa njengabanye abantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:6">73:6</a> Ngako oko intamo yabo inxitywe ikratshi; Ukugonyamela kubathe wambu ngokwengubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:7">73:7</a> Amehlo abo avelile kukutyeba; Amabhongo eentliziyo zabo aphumela phandle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:8">73:8</a> Bahlalela ngentlamba, bathetha ngokubandezela, benobubi;  Bathetha iindumbisa zamazwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:9">73:9</a> Bawubeka ezulwini umlomo wabo, Ulwimi lwabo luhamba emhlabeni wonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:10">73:10</a> Ngako oko abantu babo babuyela apha; Bafinca amanzi amaninzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:11">73:11</a> Bathi, Unokuthini na ukwazi uThixo? Kukho ukwazi na kOsenyangweni?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:12">73:12</a> Yabona abangendawo abaya Banokuchulumacha ngonaphakade,  bandile ngokutyeba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:13">73:13</a> Sifumane sayiqaqambisa intliziyo yethu kanti, Sazihlamba izandla zethu ngokuba msulwa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:14">73:14</a> Ndakhathazeka imini yonke, Ukohlwaywa kwethu kwaba kokwemiso yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:15">73:15</a> Ukuba bendithe, Ndiya kwenjenjalo ukuthetha, Yabona,  ngendinginizile kwisizukulwana soonyana bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:16">73:16</a> Ndathi ke ndakucinga ukuba ndikwazi oko, Kwayinkohla emehlweni am;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:17">73:17</a> Ndada ndaya kungena ezingcweleni zikaThixo, Ndakugqala ke ukuphela kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:18">73:18</a> Inene, ubamise ezindaweni ezibuthelezi, Wabawisa baba yintshabalala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:19">73:19</a> Hayi, ukuphanziswa kwabo ngephanyazo; Baphelile,  bagqityiwe kukukhwankqa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:20">73:20</a> Njengephupha ekuqabukeni komntu, Ekuvukeni kwakho, Nkosi,  wowudela umfanekiso wabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:21">73:21</a> Ukuba ndithe ndabindeka intliziyo, Ndahlabeka ezintsweni,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:22">73:22</a> Ndoba ke ndisisityhakala, ndingenakwazi; Ndoba ke ndisisilo kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:23">73:23</a> Mna ke ndihlala ndinawe; Undibambile ngesandla sam sokunene;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:24">73:24</a> Uya kundikhapha ngecebo lakho. Undithabathe emveni koku,  ndibe nozuko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:25">73:25</a> Ndinabani na emazulwini? Ukuba wena ungowam, andilinanze nganto ihlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:26">73:26</a> Ingaphela inyama yam nentliziyo yam: Iliwa lentliziyo yam,  nesabelo sam, nguThixo ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:27">73:27</a> Ngokuba, yabona, abanyawukileyo kuwe baya kudaka;  Uyababhangisa bonke abahenyuzayo, bemke kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:28">73:28</a> Mna ke, ukusondela kuThixo kulungile kum, Ndiyenza ihlathi lam iNkosi uYehova, Ukuze ndiyibalise yonke imisebenzi yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:1">74:1</a> Eyokuqiqa; eka-Asafu. Yini na Thixo, ukuba uhlale usihlambile, Uqhume umsindo wakho kwizimvu zedlelo lakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:2">74:2</a> Likhumbule ibandla lakho olithengileyo kwakudala,  Olikhululeyo, laba sisizwe selifa lakho; Intaba yaseZiyon,  ohleli kuyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:3">74:3</a> Phakamisa ukunyathela kwakho, ukuya kumanxuwa ahlala ehleli: Utshaba luvive into yonke engcweleni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:4">74:4</a> Babharhula ababandezeli bakho endaweni yokuhlangana phakathi; Bamisa eyabo imiqondiso, yaba yiyo eyimiqondiso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:5">74:5</a> Kwanga kungenelwe Intshinyela yemithi ngezixengxe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:6">74:6</a> Kungoku, uqoqo lwayo lonke Balucanda ngamazembe neengxobonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:7">74:7</a> Bayifaka umlilo ingcwele yakho; Bawuhlambela ngokuwuwisela emhlabeni umnquba wegama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:8">74:8</a> Bathi ezintliziyweni zabo, Siya kubanyanzelela phantsi kuphele; Bazitshisile zonke iindawo zikaThixo zokuhlangana ezweni apha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:9">74:9</a> Imiqondiso yethu asiyiboni, Akusekho mprofeti; Kuthi akukho waziyo ukuba koda kuse phi na kunjalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:10">74:10</a> Kunini na, Thixo, umbandezeli engcikiva? Utshaba luhleli luligiba igama lakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:11">74:11</a> Usifinyezeleni na isandla sakho, nesokunene sakho? Sirhole esifubeni sakho, ulugqibe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:12">74:12</a> Ke uThixo nguKumkani wam kwakumandulo, Ulosebenza usindiso phakathi kwehlabathi lonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:13">74:13</a> Nguwe owahlula ulwandle ngamandla akho, Owaphula iintloko zeengwenya emanzini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:14">74:14</a> Nguwe owaxhaxha iintloko zeleviyatan, Wazinika zakukudla kubantu, kubemi bomqwebedu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:15">74:15</a> Nguwe owagqobhoza yayimithombo, yayimilanjana; Nguwe owomisa imilambo engomiyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:16">74:16</a> Yeyakho imini, bobakho nobusuku; Nguwe owalungisa ukukhanya nelanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:17">74:17</a> Nguwe owamisa yonke imida yehlabathi; Ihlobo, nobusika,  nguwe owazibumbayo ezo zinto.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:18">74:18</a> Khumbula oku; utshaba lungcikiva uYehova, Abantu abanobudenge baligibile igama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:19">74:19</a> Musa ukuwunikela erhamncweni umphefumlo wehobe lakho;  Ungahlali uwulibele umhlambi wakho oziintsizana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:20">74:20</a> Bheka emnqophisweni, Ngokuba iindawo ezimnyama zelizwe zizele zizindlu zogonyamelo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:21">74:21</a> Makangabuyi otyumkileyo ehlazisiwe; Makalidumise igama lakho olusizana nolihlwempu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:22">74:22</a> Khawusuk ume, Thixo, ubambane nababambene nawe; Khumbula ukukungcikiva kwesidenge yonke imini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:23">74:23</a> Musa ukulilibala izwi lababandezeli bakho, Ukungxola kwabasukela phezulu kuwe, okuhlala kunyuka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:1">75:1</a> Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi. Umhobe ka-Asafu.  Ingoma. Siyabulela kuwe, Thixo, siyabulela; Lisondele igama lakho; Babalisa imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:2">75:2</a> Ngokuba uthi, Ndiya kwenza ngexesha elimisiweyo, Mna ndiya kugweba ngokuthe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:3">75:3</a> Liyetha amandla ihlabathi, nabemi balo; Ke mna,  ndizizinzisile iintsika zalo. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:4">75:4</a> Ndithi kubaqhayisi, Musani ukuqhayisa; Nakwabangendawo,  Musani ukuphakamisa uphondo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:5">75:5</a> Musani ukuluphakamisela phezulu uphondo lwenu, Ningathethi ngokusa, nolule intamo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:6">75:6</a> Ngokuba ugwebo aluveli empumalanga nasentshonalanga,  Nasentlango yeentaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:7">75:7</a> Hayi, nguThixo ogwebayo; Uyamthoba lo, amphakamise lowa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:8">75:8</a> Ngokuba indebe isesandleni sikaYehova, Iphuphuma igwebu lewayini, izele yephithikeziweyo. Uthulula kuyo; ewe, iintlenga zayo Ziya kuselwa zifincwe ngabangendawo bonke behlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:9">75:9</a> Ke mna ndiya kushumayela ngonaphakade, Ndiya kuvuma kuThixo kaYakobi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:10">75:10</a> Zonke iimpondo zabangendawo ndiya kuzixakaxa, Iimpondo zelungisa ziya kuphakanyiswa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:1">76:1</a> Kumongameli; eyokubethelwa ngezinto ezineentambo. Umhobe ka-Asafu. Ingoma. Waziwa kwaYuda uThixo, Likhulu kwaSirayeli igama lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:2">76:2</a> Umnquba wakhe waba seSalem, Nekhaya lakhe eZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:3">76:3</a> Wayaphula apho imibane yesaphetha, Ingweletshetshe,  nekrele, nezixhobo zemfazwe. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:4">76:4</a> Ukhanyile, uyingangamsha ngaphezu kweentaba zokuqwenga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:5">76:5</a> Babhunyulwe abantliziyo iyimbalasane, Balala umlala kanye,  Akazifumana izandla zawo onke amakroti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:6">76:6</a> Ekukhalimeni kwakho, Thixo kaYakobi, Kwasindwa bubuthongo iinqwelo zokulwa namahashe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:7">76:7</a> Unguwena wena woyikekayo; Ngubani na onokuma phambi kwakho,  wakuba nomsindo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:8">76:8</a> Emazulwini usivakalisile isigwebo; Loyika ihlabathi,  lazola,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:9">76:9</a> Ekusukeni kukaThixo ukuba agwebe, Abasindise bonke abalulamileyo behlabathi. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:10">76:10</a> Ngokuba ubushushu bomntu buya kuba ngumbulelo kuwe; Uya kuwabhinqa amasalela obushushu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:11">76:11</a> Bhambathisani, nisizalise isibhambathiso kuYehova uThixo wenu; Bonke abamngqongileyo mabeze nezithabathaba kofanele kukoyikwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:12">76:12</a> Uya kunqumla ukufutha kweenganga, Uyoyikeka kookumkani behlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:1">77:1</a> Kumongameli. KuYedutun. Eka-Asafu. Umhobe. Izwi lam lisingisa kuThixo, ndikhala; Izwi lam lisingisa kuThixo, ukuba andibekele indlebe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:2">77:2</a> Ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam ndiquqela eNkosini yam; Isandla sam solukile ebusuku, asaqoba; Awavuma ukuthuthuzeleka umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:3">77:3</a> Ndikhumbula uThixo, ndincwine; Ndithelekelele, utyhafe umoya wam. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:4">77:4</a> Uzibambile iinkophe zamehlo am, Ndikhandiwe, andaba nakuthetha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:5">77:5</a> Ndicinga ngemihla yamandulo, Iminyaka yasephakadeni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:6">77:6</a> Ndiya kukhumbula ebusuku ukubetha kwam uhadi; Ndithetha nentliziyo yam, uphengulula umoya wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:7">77:7</a> Ndithi, Iya kundihlamba ngonaphakade na iNkosi yam, Ingabi saphinda iphathe ngetarhu na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:8">77:8</a> Iphele yaphela na inceba yayo? Sigqibele na isithembiso sayo kwisizukulwana ngesizukulwana?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:9">77:9</a> UThixo ukulibele na ukubabala? Uyivingcele ngomsindo kusini na imfesane yakhe? (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:10">77:10</a> Ndide ndithi ke, Sisifo sam esi; Yiminyaka yesandla sokunene sOsenyangweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:11">77:11</a> Ndikhankanya izenzo ezincamisayo zikaYehova; Ngokuba ndikhumbula imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo yamandulo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:12">77:12</a> Ndicamanga ngako konke ukusebenza kwakho, Ndithelekelele ngezenzo zakho zonke ezincamisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:13">77:13</a> Thixo, isebungcweleni indlela yakho; Ngubani na onguthixo omkhulu njengoThixo wethu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:14">77:14</a> UnguloThixo, wenza ngokubalulekileyo; Wawazisa amandla akho ezizweni,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:15">77:15</a> Wabakhulula ngengalo abantu bakho, Oonyana bakaYakobi noYosefu. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:16">77:16</a> Akubona amanzi, Thixo, Akubona amanzi, azibhija-bhija,  Ewe, agungqa amanzi enzonzobila;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:17">77:17</a> Amafu engqingqwa aphalaza amanzi, Isibhakabhaka savakalisa isandi; Ewe, iintolo zakho zahamba-hamba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:18">77:18</a> Izwi lendudumo yakho laba sesaqhwithini, Imibane yalikhanyisa elimiweyo, Lagungqa lanyikima ihlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:19">77:19</a> Yaba selwandle indlela yakho, Nomendo wakho waba semanzini amaninzi; Awaziwa umkhondo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:20">77:20</a> Wabakhokela njengezimvu abantu bakho, Ngesandla sooMoses noAron.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:1">78:1</a> Eyokuqiqa ka-Asafu. Wubekeleni indlebe umyalelo wam,  bantu bakowethu, Wathobeleni indlebe amazwi omlomo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:2">78:2</a> Ndiya kuwuvula umlomo wam ngomzekeliso; Ndiya kumpompozisa iintsonkotha zamandulo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:3">78:3</a> Esakuvayo sakwazi, Abasibaliselayo oobawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:4">78:4</a> Asiyi kukugusha koonyana babo; Sobalisela isizukulwana esizayo iindumiso zikaYehova, Namandla akhe, nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo awayenzayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:5">78:5</a> Wamisa isingqiniso kwaYakobi, Wabeka umyalelo kwaSirayeli,  Awawumisela oobawo, Ukuba bawazise oonyana babo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:6">78:6</a> Ukuze siwazi isizukulwana esizayo, oonyana abaza kuzalwa,  Basuke babalisele ababo oonyana;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:7">78:7</a> Bayame ngoThixo, Bangazilibali izenzo ezincamisayo zikaThixo, Bayilondoloze imithetho yakhe:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:8">78:8</a> Bangabi njengooyise, Isizukulwana esiyinjubaqa,  esineenkani, Isizukulwana esingayilungisanga intliziyo yaso,  Esimoya unganyanisanga kuThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:9">78:9</a> Oonyana bakaEfrayim, bexhobile, beziintoli ezinezaphetha,  Bajika ngemini yemfazwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:10">78:10</a> Abawugcinanga umnqophiso kaThixo, Abavumanga ukuhamba ngomyalelo wakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:11">78:11</a> Bazilibala izenzo zakhe ezincamisayo, Nezibalulekileyo zakhe awababonisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:12">78:12</a> Phambi kooyise wenza ngokubalulekileyo Ezweni lamaYiputa,  emhlabeni waseTsohan.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:13">78:13</a> Waludabula ulwandle, wabaweza, Wawamisa amanzi njengemfumba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:14">78:14</a> Wabakhapha ngelifu emini, Ngokukhanya komlilo ubusuku bonke,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:15">78:15</a> Walicanda iliwa entlango, Wabaseza amanzi anzongonzongo kakhulu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:16">78:16</a> Wavelisa imiqukuqela yamanzi engxondorheni, Wahlisa amanzi njengemilambo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:17">78:17</a> Baqokela noko ukona kuye, Nokumphikisa Osenyangweni emqwebedwini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:18">78:18</a> Bamlinga uThixo ngentliziyo yabo, Ngokuwubizela umphefumlo wabo ukudla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:19">78:19</a> Bathetha ngoThixo, bathi, Unako na uThixo ukulungisa isithebe entlango?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:20">78:20</a> Yabona, walibetha iliwa, abaleka amanzi, Yakhukula nemilanjana; Woba nako na nokubanika ukutya, Nokubalungiselela inyama abantu bakhe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:21">78:21</a> Weva ke uThixo, waphuphuma umsindo wakhe, Watsha umlilo kwaYakobi, Kwenyuka kwaya umsindo kwaSirayeli;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:22">78:22</a> Ngokuba bengakholwanga kuThixo, Bengakholosanga ngosindiso lwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:23">78:23</a> Waziwisela ke umthetho iingqimba zamafu ngaphezulu,  Wazivula iingcango zezulu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:24">78:24</a> Wabanisela ngemana ukuze badle, Wabanika ingqolowa yasezulwini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:25">78:25</a> Umntu wadla isonka sOnamandla; Wabathumela umphako bada badikwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:26">78:26</a> Wandulula umoya wasempumalanga ezulwini, Wawuqhuba ngamandla akhe umoya wasezantsi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:27">78:27</a> Wabanisela inyama njengothuli, Neentaka ezinamaphiko njengentlabathi yolwandle;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:28">78:28</a> Yawa phakathi kweminquba yabo, Ngeenxa zonke emakhayeni abo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:29">78:29</a> Badla, bahlutha kakhulu, Wabazisela ke inkanuko yabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:30">78:30</a> Bengekashenxi enkanukweni yabo, Kusekho ukudla kwabo emlonyeni wabo:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:31">78:31</a> Kwenyuka umsindo kaThixo waya kubo, Wabulala phakathi kwabatyebileyo babo, Wawawisa amadodana akwaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:32">78:32</a> Kuyo yonke loo nto bahambisa ngokona, Abakholwa yimisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:33">78:33</a> Wayiphelisa ke imihla yabo njengomphunga, Neminyaka yabo ngokukhwankqisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:34">78:34</a> Xa wathi wababulala, bamquqela; Babuya bamquqela uThixo ngenyameko,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:35">78:35</a> Bakhumbula ukuba uThixo uliliwa labo, UThixo Osenyangweni ungumkhululi wabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:36">78:36</a> Ke bamthomalalisa ngomlomo wabo, Bamxokisa ngolwimi lwabo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:37">78:37</a> Intliziyo yabo ayaqina kuye, Abanyaniseka emnqophisweni wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:38">78:38</a> Ke yena unemfesane, Uxolela ubugwenxa ngocamagushelo,  akonakalisi; Wawubuyisa futhi umsindo wakhe, Akabuxhoxha bonke ubushushu bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:39">78:39</a> Wakhumbula ukuba bayinyama, Bangumoya omkayo, ongabuyiyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:40">78:40</a> Kukangaphi bemphikisa entlango, Bemenza buhlungu enkangala!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:41">78:41</a> Babuya bamlinga uThixo, Bamenzakalisa oyiNgcwele wakwaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:42">78:42</a> Abasikhumbula isandla sakhe, Imini awabakhulula ngayo embandezelweni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:43">78:43</a> Awamisa ngayo imiqondiso yakhe eYiputa, Nezimanga zakhe emhlabeni waseTsohan.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:44">78:44</a> Wayiguqula imijelo yabo, yaba ligazi, Ababa nakuyisela imiqukuqela yabo yamanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:45">78:45</a> Wathumela kubo iingcongconi, zabadla; Namasele,  abatshabalalisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:46">78:46</a> Izilimo zabo wazinika iinkumbi ezinqunquthayo, Ukuxelenga kwabo wakunika iinkumbi ezandayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:47">78:47</a> Wawubulala ngesichotho umdiliya wabo, Nemithombe yabo ngomkhenkce.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:48">78:48</a> Wayinikela kwisichotho imfuyo yabo, Nemihlambi yabo ngemibane.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:49">78:49</a> Wathumela kubo ukuvutha komsindo wakhe, Ukuphuphuma kwawo,  nokubhavuma, nembandezelo, Ibutho lezithunywa zobubi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:50">78:50</a> Wawulungelelanisela umendo umsindo wakhe, Akawunqanda ekufeni umphefumlo wabo, Wabunikela ubomi babo kwindyikitya yokufa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:51">78:51</a> Wababulala bonke abamazibulo eYiputa, Iintlahlela zamandla obudoda ezintenteni zakwaHam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:52">78:52</a> Abantu bakhe wabafudusa njengezimvu, Wabaqhuba njengomhlambi entlango;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:53">78:53</a> Wabakhapha bekholosile, bengankwantyi; Ke zona iintshaba zabo lwazigubungela ulwandle</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:54">78:54</a> Wabazisa emdeni wakhe ongcwele, Kule ntaba sayizuzayo isandla sakhe sokunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:55">78:55</a> Wagxotha iintlanga ebusweni babo, Wazenzela amaqashiso zalilifa elicandiweyo; Izizwe zakwaSirayeli wazihlalisa ezintenteni zazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:56">78:56</a> Kodwa bamlinga, bamphikisa uThixo Osenyangweni, Abazigcina izingqiniso zakhe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:57">78:57</a> Babuya unuva, banginiza njengooyise. Bajika njengesaphetha esikhohlisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:58">78:58</a> Bamqumbisa ngeziganga zabo, Bamkhweletisa ngemifanekiso yabo eqingqiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:59">78:59</a> Weva uThixo, waphuphuma umsindo, Wawacekisa kakhulu amaSirayeli;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:60">78:60</a> Wawulahla umnquba waseShilo, Intente abeyimise esintwini;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:61">78:61</a> Wawanikela ekuthinjweni amandla akhe, Isihombo sakhe esandleni sombandezeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:62">78:62</a> Wabanikela abantu bakhe kwikrele, Umsindo wakhe waphuphumela ilifa lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:63">78:63</a> Amadodana abo adliwa ngumlilo, Iintombi zabo azagcotyelwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:64">78:64</a> Ababingeleli babo bawa likrele, Abahlolokazi babo abalila.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:65">78:65</a> Yaza yavuka njengobelele iNkosi, Njengegorha elimemeleliswa yiwayini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:66">78:66</a> Yababetha ngasemva ababandezeli bayo, Yabenza ingcikivo engunaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:67">78:67</a> Yayicekisa intente yakwaYosefu, Ayasinyula isizwe sakwaEfrayim.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:68">78:68</a> Yanyula isizwe sakwaYuda, Intaba yaseZiyon eyayithandayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:69">78:69</a> Yayakha njengokuphakama kwezulu ingcwele yakhe,  Njengomhlaba lo awusekileyo ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:70">78:70</a> Yanyula uDavide umkhonzi wayo, Yamthabatha ezibayeni zezimvu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:71">78:71</a> Yamthabatha elandela izimvu ezanyisayo, Yamzisa ukuba aluse kwaYakobi abantu bayo, KwaSirayeli ilifa layo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:72">78:72</a> Wabalusa ke ngengqibelelo yentliziyo yakhe, Wabakhapha ngokwazi kwezandla zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:1">79:1</a> Umhobe ka-Asafu. Thixo, iintlanga zingene elifeni lakho,  Ziyenze inqambi itempile yakho engcwele; Ziyenze yayimiwewe iYerusalem.</p>
