 <p><a name="an_79:2">79:2</a> Izidumbu zabakhonzi bakho zizinike iintaka zezulu ukuba zizidle, Nenyama yabakho benceba ziyinike amarhamncwa elizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:3">79:3</a> Ziliphalazile igazi labo njengamanzi ngeenxa zonke eYerusalem; Akwabakho mngcwabi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:4">79:4</a> Senziwe ingcikivo kubamelwane bethu, Isigculelo nesicukucezo kwabasingqongileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:5">79:5</a> Kunini na, Yehova, uhleli uqumbile? Liya kuvutha njengomlilo na ikhwele lakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:6">79:6</a> Phalaza ubushushu bakho ezintlangeni ezingakwaziyo,  Ezikumkanini ezingalinquliyo igama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:7">79:7</a> Ngokuba zimdlile uYakobi, Zalenza inxuwa ikhaya lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:8">79:8</a> Musa ukubukhumbula kuthi ubugwenxa bamanyange ethu,  Mayingxame isikhawulele imfesane yakho: Ngokuba siswele kakhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:9">79:9</a> Sincede, Thixo ongumsindisi wethu, ngenxa yozuko lwegama lakho, Usihlangule, uzixolele ngocamagushelo izono zethu ngenxa yegama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:10">79:10</a> Yini na ukuba iintlanga zithi kuthi, Uphi na uThixo wabo?  Makwazeke ezintlangeni, emehlweni ethu, Ukuphindezelwa kwegazi labakhonzi bakho eliphalaziweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:11">79:11</a> Makuze phambi kwakho ukugcuma kwamakhonkxwa; Ngokobukhulu bengalo yakho basalise oonyana bokufa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:12">79:12</a> Yibuyisele kubamelwane bethu kasixhenxe esondweni lengubo yabo Ingcikivo yabo, abakungcikive ngayo, Nkosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:13">79:13</a> Ke thina bantu bakho, zimvu zaluswa nguwe, Siya kubulela kuwe ngonaphakade, Sibalise ngendumiso yakho kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:1">80:1</a> Kumongameli; ngeyeenyibiba ezingqinisayo. Ka-Asafu.  Umhobe. Ulomalusi kaSirayeli, beka indlebe! Uloqhuba uYosefu njengezimvu, Ulohlala ezikerubhini, bengezela!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:2">80:2</a> Phambi koEfrayim noBhenjamin noManase, Vusa ubugorha bakho,  Uze kusisindisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:3">80:3</a> Thixo, sibuyise, Ukhanyise ubuso bakho, sisindiswe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:4">80:4</a> Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Kunini na uqhuma umsindo wakho ekuthandazeni kwabantu bakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:5">80:5</a> Ubadlisa isonka seenyembezi, Wabaseza iinyembezi ngemilinganiso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:6">80:6</a> Usenze into abaxabana ngayo abamelwane bethu; Iintshaba zethu ziyasigculela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:7">80:7</a> Thixo wemikhosi, sibuyise, Ukhanyise ubuso bakho,  sisindiswe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:8">80:8</a> Wanyothula umdiliya eYiputa, Wagxotha iintlanga, wawutyala;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:9">80:9</a> Wahlahla phambi kwawo, Wendelisa iingcambu, wazalisa ilizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:10">80:10</a> Zagutyungelwa iintaba ngumthunzi wawo, Nemisedare kaThixo ngamasebe awo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:11">80:11</a> Wasa amasebe awo elwandle, Namagatya awo kuwo uMlambo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:12">80:12</a> Uzityhobozeleni na iintango zawo, Ukuze bawukhe bonke abadlula ngendlela?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:13">80:13</a> Ingulube yasehlathini iyawubhuqa, Nento edakasa endle iyawudla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:14">80:14</a> Thixo wemikhosi, khawubuye, Uqondele usemazulwini, ubone,  Uwuvelele lo mdiliya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:15">80:15</a> Yikhusele into esiyityeleyo isandla sakho sokunene, Unyana lo uzizimaseleyo ngokwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:16">80:16</a> Utshisiwe ngumlilo, uhlahliwe; Bayadaka ngokusongela kobuso bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:17">80:17</a> Isandla sakho masibe phezu komfo wesandla sakho sokunene,  Phezu koonyana babantu, ozizimaseleyo ngokwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:18">80:18</a> Asiyi kumka kuwe; Siphilise, silinqule igama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:19">80:19</a> Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, sibuyise, Ukhanyise ubuso bakho,  sisindiswe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:1">81:1</a> Kumongameli; ngolwaseGati. Ka-Asafu. Memelelani kuThixo,  igwiba lethu, Dumani kuThixo kaYakobi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:2">81:2</a> Hlabani ingoma, nibethe ingqongqo, Uhadi olumnandi, kunye nomrhubhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:3">81:3</a> Vuthelani isigodlo ukuthwasa kwenyanga, Nokuhlangana kwenyanga, ngemini yomthendeleko wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:4">81:4</a> Ngokuba ngummiselo lowo kuSirayeli, Lisiko likaThixo kaYakobi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:5">81:5</a> Sisingqiniso awasimisayo kwaYosefu, Ekucandeni kwakhe ezweni laseYiputa; Ndeva intetho endingayaziyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:6">81:6</a> Ndawususa umthwalo egxalabeni lakhe; Izandla zakhe zasuka ezingobozini zokuthwala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:7">81:7</a> Embandezelweni wadanduluka wena, ndakuhlangula;  Ndakuphendula esitheni leendudumo, Ndakuvavanya emanzini aseMeribha. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:8">81:8</a> Ndathi, Yivani, bantu bam, ndiqononondise kuni; Sirayeli,  ukuba unokuphulaphula kum!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:9">81:9</a> Makungabikho thixo wasemzini kuwe; Unganquli thixo wolunye uhlanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:10">81:10</a> Ndim uYehova uThixo wakho, Okunyusileyo elizweni laseYiputa. Yakhamisa, ndiwuzalise umlomo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:11">81:11</a> Ke abantu bam abaliva izwi lam, USirayeli akandivumanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:12">81:12</a> Ndabanikela ebungqoleni beentliziyo zabo; Bahamba ngawabo amaqhinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:13">81:13</a> Akwaba abantu bam bebendiva, Akwaba uSirayeli ubehamba ngendlela yam!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:14">81:14</a> Bendiya kuzithoba kamsinya iintshaba zabo, Ndisibuyisele phezu kwababandezeli babo isandla sam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:15">81:15</a> Abamthiyayo uYehova bebeya kuhanahanisa kuye, Libe ngunaphakade ixesha labo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:16">81:16</a> Bendiya kubadlisa ingqolowa etyebileyo, Ndibahluthise ngobusi etsilini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:1">82:1</a> Umhobe ka-Asafu. UThixo umi ebandleni likaThixo, Ugweba phakathi koothixo; uthi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:2">82:2</a> Kunini na nigweba ngobugqwetha, Nibanonelela abangendawo?  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:3">82:3</a> Thethani ityala losweleyo nelenkedama, Gwebelani olusizana nolihlwempu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:4">82:4</a> Sizani osweleyo nolihlwempu, Bahlanguleni esandleni sabangendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:5">82:5</a> Abazi, abaqondi, Bahamba-hamba emnyameni; Ziyashukuma zonke iziseko zehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:6">82:6</a> Ndithe mna, Ningoothixo, Ningoonyana bOsenyangweni nonke niphela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:7">82:7</a> Noko niya kufa njengomntu, Niwe njengomnye kubathetheli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:8">82:8</a> Khawusuk ume, Thixo, gweba ehlabathini; Ngokuba uya kuzidla ilifa wena zonke iintlanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:1">83:1</a> Ingoma. Umhobe ka-Asafu. Thixo, musa ukuthi cwaka, Musa ukuthi tu, musa ukuzola, Thixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:2">83:2</a> Ngokuba nanzo iintshaba zakho zixokozela; Abakuthiyayo baphakamisa intloko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:3">83:3</a> Bagqugula igqugula elinobuqhophololo ngabantu bakho,  Bacebisane ngabagushiweyo nguwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:4">83:4</a> Bathi, Yizani sibethe bee shwaka, bangabi luhlanga, Lingabi sakhunjulwa igama likaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:5">83:5</a> Ngokuba bacebisana ngantliziyo-nye, Benza umnqophiso ngawe:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:6">83:6</a> Iintente zakwaEdom nezakwaIshmayeli, AmaMowabhi namaHagari,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:7">83:7</a> AmaGebhali nama-Amon nama-Amaleki, AmaFilisti kunye nabemi baseTire;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:8">83:8</a> Nama-Asiriya athelele kubo, Baba yingalo koonyana bakaLote.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:9">83:9</a> Yenza kubo njengoko wenza ngako kumaMidiyan, NakuSisera,  nakuYabhin esihlanjeni seKishon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:10">83:10</a> Batshabalala e-Endore, Baba ngumgquba wokugalelwa emhlabeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:11">83:11</a> Benze bona, amanene abo ke, babe njengo-Orebhe nanjengoZebhe; Zonke iinkosi zabo zibe njengoZebha nanjengoTsalimuna;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:12">83:12</a> Bona bathi, Masiwahluthe abe ngawethu amakhaya kaThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:13">83:13</a> Thixo wam, benze babe njengesaqhwithi, Njengomququ phambi komoya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:14">83:14</a> Njengomlilo odla ihlathi, Njengedangatye lilenya intaba,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:15">83:15</a> Yenjenjalo ukubasukela ngoqhwithela lwakho, Ubakhwankqise ngomoya wakho ovuthuzayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:16">83:16</a> Buzalise ubuso babo ngehlazo, Balifune igama lakho,  Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:17">83:17</a> Mabadane bakhwankqiswe ngonaphakade, Babe neentloni,  badake;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:18">83:18</a> Bazi ukuba wena, ugama linguYehova, unguwe wedwa Osenyangweni phezu kwehlabathi lonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:1">84:1</a> Kumongameli; ngolwaseGati. Eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe.  Hayi, ukuthandeka kweminquba yakho, Yehova wemikhosi!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:2">84:2</a> Umphefumlo wam ulangazelela, uyaphela kukuzilangazelela,  iintendelezo zikaYehova; Intliziyo yam nenyama yam imemelela kuThixo ophilileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:3">84:3</a> Intakana le ifumene ikhaya; Inkonjane izifumanele indlu,  Apho izalela khona amathole ayo: Izibingelelo zakho, Yehova wemikhosi, Kumkani wam, Thixo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:4">84:4</a> Hayi, uyolo lwabahlala endlwini yakho! Basaya kukudumisa.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:5">84:5</a> Hayi, uyolo lwabantu abamandla akuwe, Abakhumbula umendo oya eZiyon!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:6">84:6</a> Bephumela entilini yemithi yeBhaka, Bayenza ibe nemithombo;  Ewe, imvula iyithi wambu ngentsikelelo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:7">84:7</a> Baya besomelela ngokomelela; Babonakala phambi koThixo eZiyon, bathi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:8">84:8</a> Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Wuve umthandazo wam, Wubekele indlebe, Thixo kaYakobi. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:9">84:9</a> Khangela, Thixo, ngweletshetshe yethu, Ubukhangele ubuso bomthanjiswa wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:10">84:10</a> Ngokuba imini enye ezintendelezweni zakho ilungile kunewaka; Ndinyule ukuba semnyango endlwini kaThixo wam,  Kunokuhlala ngaphakathi kweentente zokungendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:11">84:11</a> Ngokuba ulilanga, uyingweletshetshe uYehova uThixo,  UYehova uyababala azukise; Abahamba ngokugqibeleleyo akabavimbi nto ilungileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:12">84:12</a> Yehova wemikhosi, Hayi, uyolo lomntu okholose ngawe!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:1">85:1</a> Kumongameli; eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe. Yehova, wabe unetarhu kwilizwe lakho. Ububabuyisa abathinjwa bakaYakobi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:2">85:2</a> Ububuxolela ubugwenxa babantu bakho, Ubuziselela zonke izono zabo. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:3">85:3</a> Ubuwufinyeza umsindo wakho ophuphumayo, Ububuya ekuvutheni komsindo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:4">85:4</a> Sibuyise, Thixo ongumsindisi wethu, Uyisuse ingqumbo yakho kuthi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:5">85:5</a> Uya kusiqumbela ngonaphakade na? Umsindo wakho uya kuwolulela kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:6">85:6</a> Akuyi kubuya usiphilise na, Abantu bakho bavuye ngawe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:7">85:7</a> Sibonise inceba yakho, Yehova, Siphe usindiso lwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:8">85:8</a> Mandive oko aya kukuthetha uThixo, uYehova; Hayi, uthetha uxolo kubantu bakhe nakwabakhe benceba; Mabangabuyeli ke ekunyabeni kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:9">85:9</a> Inene, usindiso lwakhe lusondele kwabamoyikayo, Ukuze luhlale uzuko ezweni lakowethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:10">85:10</a> Kuya kuqubisana inceba nenyaniso, Kuya kwangana ubulungisa noxolo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:11">85:11</a> Inyaniso iya kuntshula emhlabeni, Ubulungisa buqondele busemazulwini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:12">85:12</a> Kananjalo uYehova uya kusinika okulungileyo, Ilizwe lethu lisinike indyebo yalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:13">85:13</a> Ubulungisa buya kuhamba phambi kwakhe, Buyigqale ngentliziyo indlela yokunyathela kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:1">86:1</a> Umthandazo kaDavide. Thoba indlebe yakho, Yehova,  ndiphendule, Ngokuba ndilusizana, ndilihlwempu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:2">86:2</a> Wugcine umphefumlo wam, ngokuba ndingowenceba; Msindise,  wena Thixo wam, umkhonzi wakho, Lo ukholose ngawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:3">86:3</a> Ndibabale, Nkosi yam, Ngokuba ndidanduluka kuwe yonke imini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:4">86:4</a> Wuvuyise umphefumlo womkhonzi wakho, Ngokuba umphefumlo wam ndiwuphakamisela kuwe, Nkosi yam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:5">86:5</a> Ngokuba ulungile wena, Nkosi yam, uxolela; Umkhulu ngenceba kubo bonke abakunqulayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:6">86:6</a> Wubekele indlebe umthandazo wam, Yehova, Ulibazele indlebe izwi lokutarhuzisa kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:7">86:7</a> Ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam ndinqula wena, Ngokuba uya kundiphendula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:8">86:8</a> Akukho unjengawe, Nkosi yam, phakathi koothixo; Akukho zenzo zinjengezakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:9">86:9</a> Zonke iintlanga owazenzayo ziya kuza ziqubude phambi kwakho, Nkosi yam, Zizukise igama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:10">86:10</a> Ngokuba umkhulu, wenza imisebenzi ebalulekileyo, UnguThixo wena wedwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:11">86:11</a> Ndiyalele, Yehova, indlela yakho, Ndihambe ngenyaniso yakho; Yibandakanye intliziyo yam ukuba ndiloyike igama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:12">86:12</a> Ndiya kubulela kuwe, Nkosi yam, Thixo wam, ngentliziyo yonke, Ndilizukise igama lakho ngonaphakade:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:13">86:13</a> Ngokuba inceba yakho ibe inkulu kum; Wawuhlangula umphefumlo wam kwelingaphantsi labafileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:14">86:14</a> Thixo, abakhukhumali basukele phezulu kum; Ibandla labanobungqwangangqwili lifuna umphefumlo wam; Abakumisi wena phambi kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:15">86:15</a> Ke wena, Nkosi yam, unguThixo onemfesane, onobabalo, Ozeka kade umsindo, omkhulu ngenceba nenyaniso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:16">86:16</a> Ndibheke, undibabale; Mphe amandla akho umkhonzi wakho,  Umsindise unyana womkhonzazana wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:17">86:17</a> Ndenzele umqondiso wokulungileyo, Bawubone abandithiyayo,  badane, Kuba wena, Yehova, undincedile, wandithuthuzela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:1">87:1</a> Eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe. Ingoma. Useko alusekileyo lusezintabeni ezingcwele;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:2">87:2</a> Amasango eZiyon uYehova uwathanda Ngaphezu kweminquba yonke kaYakobi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:3">87:3</a> Kuthethwa iinto ezizukileyo ngawe, Mzi kaThixo.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:4">87:4</a> ORahabhi noBhabheli ndiya kubakhankanyela kwabandaziyo;  Nalo elamaFilisti nelaseTire, kunye nelakwaKushi, Aba bazalelwe khona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:5">87:5</a> Ngokusingisele kwiZiyon, kuya kuthiwa, Lo, nalo, uzalelwe kuyo, Abe yena Osenyangweni eyizinzisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:6">87:6</a> UYehova uya kubala, ekuzibhaleni izizwi, athi, Abaya bazalelwe khona: (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:7">87:7</a> Baze, bevuma beqamba, bathi, Yonke imithombo yam ikuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:1">88:1</a> Ingoma; umhobe woonyana bakaKora; kumongameli; ngosizi,  ngelidambileyo. Owokuqiqa kaHeman umEzra. Yehova, Thixo ongumsindisi wam, Mhlenikweni ndikhalayo ebusuku phambi kwakho,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:2">88:2</a> Mawuze phambi kwakho umthandazo wam; Thoba indlebe yakho ekuhlahlambeni kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:3">88:3</a> Ngokuba umphefumlo wam uhluthi zizinto ezimbi, Ubomi bam bufike kwelabafileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:4">88:4</a> Ndibalelwe kwabahla baye emhadini, Ndisuke ndanjengomfo ongenamandla</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:5">88:5</a> Ndingumkhululwa phakathi kwabafileyo, Njengababuleweyo,  belele engcwabeni, Ongasabakhumbuliyo; Bona banqunyulweyo esandleni sakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:6">88:6</a> Undibeke emhadini ongaphantsi, Ezindaweni ezimnyama,  ezinzulwini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:7">88:7</a> Ubushushu bakho bundishicilele, Undithobele onke amaza akho alwayo. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:8">88:8</a> Ubashenxisele kude kum abo ndazana nabo, Undenze isikizi kubo; Ndivalelwe, andinakuphuma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:9">88:9</a> Iliso lam liyaphela yingcinezelo. Ndidanduluka kuwe,  Yehova, yonke imini, Ndizolulela kuwe izandla zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:10">88:10</a> Uya kuyenzela abafileyo na imisebenzi ebalulekileyo? Kuya kuvuka abangasekhoyo, kusini na, babulele kuwe? (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:11">88:11</a> Ibaliswa engcwabeni na inceba yakho? Enzonzobileni na,  ukunyanisa kwakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:12">88:12</a> Yaziswa emnyameni na imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo?  Baziswa ezweni lokulibala na ubulungisa bakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:13">88:13</a> Ke mna, Yehova, ndizibika kuwe, Kwakusasa umthandazo wam wokuhlangabeza.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:14">88:14</a> Uwuhlambelani na, Yehova, umphefumlo wam? Ubusitheliselani na ubuso bakho kum?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:15">88:15</a> Ndilusizana, ndiyinto efayo kwasebuncinaneni bam,  Ndithwele izothuso zakho, lindikhohlile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:16">88:16</a> Kugqithe phezu kwamukuvutha kwakho, Izidandathekiso zakho zindibhangisile;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:17">88:17</a> Zindijikelezile njengamanzi imini yonke, Zindizungulezile kwaphela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:18">88:18</a> Umsusile kum ondithandayo nonguwethu; Abo ndazana nabo babubumnyama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:1">89:1</a> Eyokuqiqa kaEtan, umEzra. Iinceba zikaYehova ndiya kuvuma ngazo ngonaphakade, Kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana ndiya kwazisa ukuthembeka kwakho ngomlomo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:2">89:2</a> Ngokuba ndithi, Yakheka ngonaphakade inceba; Amazulu, uya kukuzinzisa kuwo ukuthembeka kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:3">89:3</a> Wathi, Ndenze umnqophiso nomnyulwa wam, Ndifungile kuDavide umkhonzi wam:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:4">89:4</a> Ndiya kuyizimasa ngonaphakade imbewu yakho, Ndiyakhe itrone yakho kwisizukulwana ngesizukulwana. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:5">89:5</a> Amazulu abulela imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo, Yehova,  Nokuthembeka kwakho ebandleni labangcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:6">89:6</a> Ngokuba ngubani na esibhakabhakeni olingana noYehova?  Ngubani na ofana noYehova phakathi koonyana bakaThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:7">89:7</a> UThixo ongowokungcangcazelelwa ebhungeni elikhulu labangcwele, Ongofanelwe kukoyikwa ngaphezu kwabo bonke abamngqongileyo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:8">89:8</a> Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Ngubani na onjengawe, oluqilima,  Yehova? Ukuthembeka kwakho kukungqongile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:9">89:9</a> Nguwena mlawuli wekratshi lolwandle; Ekuphakameni kwamaza alo uyawadambisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:10">89:10</a> Nguwena mtyumzi kaRahabhi njengongxwelerhiweyo, Wazithi saa iintshaba zakho ngengalo yakho eqinileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:11">89:11</a> Lelakho izulu, likwalelakho ihlabathi; Elimiweyo nenzaliseko yalo lasekwa nguwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:12">89:12</a> Umntla nomzantsi wadalwa nguwe; ITabhore neHermon zimemelela ngegama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:13">89:13</a> Yeyakho ingalo enobugorha; Sithe nkqi isandla sakho,  siphakamile esokunene sakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:14">89:14</a> Ummiso wetrone yakho bubulungisa nokusesikweni; Inceba nenyaniso ilungiselela phambi kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:15">89:15</a> Hayi, uyolo lwabantu abakwaziyo ukuduma! Baya kuhamba ekukhanyeni kobuso bakho, Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:16">89:16</a> Baya kugcoba egameni lakho imini yonke, Baphakame ngobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:17">89:17</a> Ngokuba isihombo samandla abo nguwe; Ekuthandeni kwakho,  uphondo lwethu luphakamile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:18">89:18</a> Ngokuba ikuYehova ingweletshetshe yethu, UkoyiNgcwele kaSirayeli ukumkani wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:19">89:19</a> Wakha wathetha ngombono kowenceba wakho, wathi, Ndibeke uncedo egorheni, Ndiphakamise indodana ebantwini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:20">89:20</a> Ndifumene uDavide umkhonzi wam; Ndimthambisile ngeoli yam engcwele,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:21">89:21</a> Esiya kuqinisela kuye isandla sam, Nengalo yam imkhaliphise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:22">89:22</a> Utshaba aluyi kumqubula; Nonyana wobugqwetha akayi kumcinezela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:23">89:23</a> Ndiya kubaqoba phambi kwakhe ababandezeli bakhe,  Ndibaxabele abamthiyayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:24">89:24</a> Inyaniso yam nenceba yam inaye; Luya kuphakama uphondo lwakhe egameni lam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:25">89:25</a> Ndiya kusisa elwandle isandla sakhe, EMilanjeni esokunene sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:26">89:26</a> Yena ukundibiza wothi, UnguBawo, UnguThixo wam, neliwa lokundisindisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:27">89:27</a> Kananjalo mna ndiya kumenza owamazibulo, Osenyangweni kookumkani behlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:28">89:28</a> Ndiya kumgcinela inceba yam ngonaphakade, Umnqophiso wam unyanise kuye;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:29">89:29</a> Ndiyimise ngonaphakade imbewu yakhe, Netrone yakhe ibe njengemihla yamazulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:30">89:30</a> Ukuba bathe oonyana bakhe bawulahla umyalelo wam, Abahamba ngamasiko am;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:31">89:31</a> Ukuba bathe bayihlambela imimiselo yam, Abayigcina imithetho yam:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:32">89:32</a> Ndoluvelela ukreqo lwabo ngentonga, Nobugwenxa babo ngemivumbo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:33">89:33</a> Ke yona inceba yam andiyi kuyaphula kuye, Ndingaxoki ekuthembekeni kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:34">89:34</a> Andiyi kuwuhlambela umnqophiso wam, Ndiyijike into ephume emlonyeni wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:35">89:35</a> Ndibufunge kwakanye ubungcwele bam, ndathi, Inene, andiyi kumxokisa uDavide;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:36">89:36</a> Imbewu yakhe iya kubakho ngonaphakade, Netrone yakhe njengelanga phambi kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:37">89:37</a> Iya kuqiniseka njengenyanga ngonaphakade; Ingqina lasesibhakabhakeni lithembekile. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:38">89:38</a> Kwawena umhlambile, umcekisile, Umphuphumele ngomsindo umthanjiswa wakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:39">89:39</a> Uthe nethe ngumnqophiso womkhonzi wakho; Usidyobhile emhlabeni isithsaba sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:40">89:40</a> Uzityhobozile zonke iintango zakhe, Uzenze inxuwa iinqaba zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:41">89:41</a> Bayamphanga bonke abadlula ngendlela, Waba yingcikivo kubamelwane bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:42">89:42</a> Usiphakamisile isandla sokunene sabambandezelayo,  Uzivuyisile zonke iintshaba zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:43">89:43</a> Wabuyisa nokubuyisa uhlangothi lwekrele lakhe, Akwammisa emfazweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:44">89:44</a> Umsusile enkazimlweni yakhe, Uyikhahlele emhlabeni itrone yakhe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:45">89:45</a> Uyinqumle imihla yobutsha bakhe, Wamthi wambu ngokudana.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:46">89:46</a> Kunini na, Yehova, uhleli uzisithelisile, Busitsha njengomlilo ubushushu bakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:47">89:47</a> Khumbula ukunqamka kwam, into okuyiyo! Ubadaleleni na,  baba yinto engento bonke oonyana babantu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:48">89:48</a> Yiyiphi na indoda ehleliyo, engayi kukubona ukufa,  Enokuwusindisa umphefumlo wayo esandleni selabafileyo?  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:49">89:49</a> Ziphi na iinceba zakho zangaphambili, Nkosi yam,  Owamfungela zona uDavide ngokuthembeka kwakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:50">89:50</a> Khumbula, Nkosi yam, ukungcikiveka kwabakhonzi bakho;  Ndithwele esifubeni sam zonke izizwe ezininzi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:51">89:51</a> Ezingcikivayo, ziziintshaba zakho, Yehova; Ezingcikiva amanyathela omthanjiswa wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:52">89:52</a> Makabongwe uYehova ngonaphakade. Amen, amen.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:1">90:1</a> Umthandazo kaMoses, umfo wakwaThixo. Nkosi yam, ulikhaya wena kuthi, Isizukulwana ngesizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:2">90:2</a> Kungekazalwa zintaba, Ungekavelisi mhlaba, nazwe limiweyo,  Kususela kwaphakade kude kuse ephakadeni, wena unguThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:3">90:3</a> Umbuyisela umntu eluthulini, Uthi, Buyani, nyana babantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:4">90:4</a> Ngokuba iwaka leminyaka emehlweni akho Linjengemini yezolo,  xa idluleyo, Linjengomlindo wasebusuku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:5">90:5</a> Uyabakhukulisa, balale; Ngengomso babuya bahlume njengotyani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:6">90:6</a> Ngomso butyatyamba, bubuye buhlume; Ngokuhlwa buyasikwa bome.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:7">90:7</a> Ngokuba siyaphela ngumsindo wakho, Sikhwankqiswe bubushushu bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:8">90:8</a> Ububeke ubugwenxa bethu phambi kwakho, Nesibufihlileyo ububeka ekukhanyiseleni kobuso bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:9">90:9</a> Ngokuba yonke imihla yethu isangene ngokuphuphuma komsindo wakho, Siyiphelisile iminyaka yethu njengentsebezo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:10">90:10</a> Imihla yeminyaka yethu iseminyakeni engamashumi asixhenxe;  Ukuba ithe yaba mininzi kakhulu, iba yiminyaka emashumi asibhozo, Libe ke iqhayiya layo likukwaphuka nokungabi nto yanto, Ngokuba ithe phe yakhawuleza, saphaphazela semka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:11">90:11</a> Ngubani na owaziyo amandla omsindo wakho, Nokuphuphuma kwawo, ngoko ufanele ukoyikwa ngako?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:12">90:12</a> Sazise kanye ukuyibala imihla yethu, Ukuze sizuze intliziyo elumkileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:13">90:13</a> Buya, Yehova, kunini na? Uzohlwaye ngenxa yabakhonzi bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:14">90:14</a> Sihluthise kwakusasa ngenceba yakho, Simemelele, sivuye yonke imihla yethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:15">90:15</a> Sivuyise ngangemihla owasicinezela ngayo. Ngangeminyaka esabona ububi ngayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:16">90:16</a> Mayibonakale kubakhonzi bakho imisebenzi yakho,  Nobungangamela bakho koonyana babo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:17">90:17</a> Ubumnandi bukaYehova mabube phezu kwethu. Zimasa isenzo sezandla zethu phezu kwethu, Isenzo sezandla zethu usizimase sona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:1">91:1</a> Ohleli esitheni lOsenyangweni, Azilalise emthunzini kaSomandla,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:2">91:2</a> Uthi kuYehova, Hlathi lam, Mboniselo yam, Thixo wam,  endikholose ngaye!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:3">91:3</a> Ngokuba ngokwakhe uya kukuhlangula emgibeni womthiyeli,  Endyikityeni yokufa eyeyelisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:4">91:4</a> Wokugubungela ngeentsiba zakhe, Uzimele phantsi kwamaphiko akhe. Likhaka, yingweletshetshe inyaniso yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:5">91:5</a> Akuyi koyikiswa zizothuso ebusuku, Nalutolo lubaleka emini;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:6">91:6</a> Nandyikitya yakufa ihamba esithokothokweni, Nasifo sibhubhisayo, sibhuqa emini enkulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:7">91:7</a> Kungawa iwaka ecaleni kwakho, Isigidi ngasekunene kwakho,  Kodwa kungasondeli nto kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:8">91:8</a> Wokhangela ngamehlo akho odwa, Ukubonele ukubuyekezwa kwabangendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:9">91:9</a> Ngokuba nguwe, Yehova, ihlathi lam. Umenze Osenyangweni ikhaya lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:10">91:10</a> Akuyi kuqubisana bubi nawe. Kungafiki sibetho ententeni yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:11">91:11</a> Ngokuba izithunywa zakhe uziwisele umthetho ngawe, Ukuba zikugcine ezindleleni zakho zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:12">91:12</a> Zokuthwala wena ngezandla zozibini, Hleze ubetheke ngonyawo lwakho etyeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:13">91:13</a> Wonyathela phezu kwengonyama nephimpi, Uyinyashe ingonyama entsha nenamba ngeenyawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:14">91:14</a> Ngokuba enamathele kum, ndomsiza; Ndimse engxondeni,  ngokuba elazi igama lam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:15">91:15</a> Wondibiza, ndiphendule, Ndoba naye embandezelweni;  Ndomhlangula, ndimzukise;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:16">91:16</a> Ndimanelise ngemihla emide, Ndimbonise ukusindisa kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:1">92:1</a> Umhobe; ingoma, ngemini yesabatha. Kulungile ukubulela kuYehova, Nokulibethela uhadi igama lakho, Wena usenyangweni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:2">92:2</a> Ukuyixela kwakusasa inceba yakho, Nokunyanisa kwakho ebusuku,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:3">92:3</a> Ngoweentambo ezilishumi nangomrhubhe, Ngokulubetha uhadi ngofefe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:4">92:4</a> Ngokuba uyandivuyisa, Yehova, ngomsebenzi wakho, Ngezenzo zezandla zakho ndinokumemelela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:5">92:5</a> Azizikhulu izenzo zakho, Yehova! Zinzulu kakhulu iingcinga zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:6">92:6</a> Isityhakala asinakwazi; Isinyabi asikuqondi oko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:7">92:7</a> Ekudubuleni kongendawo njengomfuno, Ekutyatyambeni kwabasebenzi bonke bobutshinga, Kukuze batshabalale ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:8">92:8</a> Ke wena, Yehova, ungophezulu ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:9">92:9</a> Ngokuba uyabona, iintshaba zakho, Yehova, Ngokuba uyabona,  iintshaba zakho ziva kutshabalala; Baya kuchithwa-chithwa bonke abasebenzi bobutshinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:10">92:10</a> Uyaluphakamisa uphondo lwam njengolwenqu; Ndigalelwe ioli entsha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:11">92:11</a> Iliso lam liyababonela abandilalelayo, Indlebe yam iyabeva abasukela phezulu kum benobubi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:12">92:12</a> Amalungisa aya kudubula njengesundu, Aya kukhula njengomsedare weLebhanon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:13">92:13</a> Etyelwe nje endlwini kaYehova, Aya kutyatyamba ezintendelezweni zoThixo wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:14">92:14</a> Aya kuhluma eselenezimvi, Aya kuba etyebile, eluhlaza;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:15">92:15</a> Ukuze axele ukuba uthe tye uYehova, Uliwa lam, kungekho bugqwetha kuye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:1">93:1</a> UYehova ungukumkani, uzambathise ubungangamsha; UYehova uzambathise, ubhinqe, amandla; Lizinzile ke elimiweyo,  alinakushukunyiswa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:2">93:2</a> Kususela koko, izinzile itrone yakho; Kususela kwaphakade,  ukho wena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:3">93:3</a> Imilambo iphakamisile, Yehova, Imilambo iphakamise isandi sayo, Imilambo iphakamise ingxolo yayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:4">93:4</a> Ngaphezu kwezandi zamanzi amaninzi Angangamsha, ngaphezu kwamaza alwayo olwandle, Unobungangamsha phezulu uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:5">93:5</a> Izingqiniso zakho zinyanise kunene, Ubungcwele buyifanele indlu yakho, Yehova, imihla emide.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:1">94:1</a> Thixo wempindezelo, Yehova, Thixo wempindezelo, bengezela!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:2">94:2</a> Phakama, Mgwebi wehlabathi! Babuyisele impatho yabo abanekratshi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:3">94:3</a> Kunini na abangendawo, Yehova, Kunini na abangendawo bevuyelela?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:4">94:4</a> Balephuza amagwebu, bathetha ngokusa, Bayandolosa bonke abasebenzi bobutshinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:5">94:5</a> Batyumza abantu bakho, Yehova, Bacinezela ilifa lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:6">94:6</a> Babulala umhlolokazi nowasemzini, Bancinitha inkedama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:7">94:7</a> Bathi ke, Akaboni uYehova, Akagqali uThixo kaYakobi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:8">94:8</a> Qondani, nina bazizityhakala ebantwini; Nina zinyabi, niya kuqiqa nini na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:9">94:9</a> Omilisele indlebe, akayi kuva na? Obumbe iliso, akayi kukhangela na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:10">94:10</a> Umthethisi weentlanga akayi kohlwaya na, Ulofundisa abantu ukwazi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:11">94:11</a> UYehova ngumazi weengcinga zabantu, Ukuba zingumphunga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:12">94:12</a> Hayi, uyolo lwendoda oyithethisayo, Yehova, Oyifundisayo ngomyalelo wakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:13">94:13</a> Ukuba uyizolise eziminini zobubi, Ade ambelwe isihogo ongendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:14">94:14</a> Ngokuba uYehova akabalahli abantu bakhe, Akalishiyi ilifa lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:15">94:15</a> Ngokuba isiko liya kubuyela ebulungiseni, Balilandele bonke abantliziyo zithe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:16">94:16</a> Ngubani na oya kusukela phezulu kubo abanobubi, ngenxa yam? Ngubani na oya kumelana nabasebenzi bobutshinga, ngenxa yam?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:17">94:17</a> Koko uYehova abe luncedo lwam, Umphefumlo wam unge uhle msinya, waya apho kuthiwa cwaka khona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:18">94:18</a> Ukuba ndithi, Lwatyibilika unyawo lwam, Isuka inceba yakho, Yehova, indixhase.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:19">94:19</a> Ebuninzini beengcinga-ngcinga zam ngaphakathi kwam,  Iintuthuzelo zakho ziyawuyolisa umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:20">94:20</a> Ingaqhelana nawe na itrone yolweyeliselo, Ebumba ububi ngommiselo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:21">94:21</a> Bahlanganyela umphefumlo welungisa, Baligwebe igazi elimsulwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:22">94:22</a> Kanti ke uYehova uyingxonde kum, UThixo wam liliwa endizimela ngalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:23">94:23</a> Ububuyisela phezu kwabo ubutshinga babo, Uba bhangisa ngobubi babo; Uya kubabhangisa uYehova, uThixo wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:1">95:1</a> Yizani simemelele kuYehova, Sidume kwiliwa lokusindiswa kwethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:2">95:2</a> Masize phambi kobuso bakhe sinombulelo, Masidume kuye ngeengoma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:3">95:3</a> Ngokuba uThixo omkhulu nguYehova, NguKumkani omkhulu ngaphezu koothixo bonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:4">95:4</a> Uzisesandleni sakhe iingontsingontsi zehlabathi, Neencopho zeentaba zezakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:5">95:5</a> Ulolwakhe ulwandle, nguyena walwenzayo; Nomhlaba owomileyo zawubumba izandla zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:6">95:6</a> Yizani, masiqubude, siguqe, Sithobe phambi koYehova umenzi wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:7">95:7</a> Ngokuba nguThixo wethu yena, Thina ke singabantu bokwaluswa nguye, nezimvu zesandla sakhe. Namhla, ukuba ninokuliva izwi lakhe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:8">95:8</a> Musani ukuyenza lukhuni intliziyo yenu, njengaseMeribha,  Njengemini yaseMasa entlango;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:9">95:9</a> Oko bandilingayo ooyihlo. Bandicikida, bewubona umsebenzi wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:10">95:10</a> Iminyaka yaba ngamashumi amane ndikruqukile sesi sizukulwana, Ndathi, Ngabantu abantliziyo zindwendwayo, Abazazi iindlela zam bona;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:11">95:11</a> Endada ndafunga ndinomsindo, ukuthi, Inene, abasayi kungena ekuphumleni kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:1">96:1</a> Vumani kuYehova ingoma entsha, Vumani kuYehova, nonke hlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:2">96:2</a> Vumani kuYehova, bongani igama lakhe, Shumayelani iimini ngeemini iindaba ezilungileyo zosindiso lwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:3">96:3</a> Balisani ezintlangeni uzuko lwakhe, Balisani ezizweni zonke imisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:4">96:4</a> Ngokuba mkhulu uYehova, engowokudunyiswa kunene; Uyoyikeka yena ngaphezu koothixo bonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:5">96:5</a> Ngokuba bonke oothixo bezizwe abanto zanto; UYehova yena wenza amazulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:6">96:6</a> Yindili nobungangamela phambi kwakhe, Ngamandla nokuhomba engcweleni yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:7">96:7</a> Mnikeni uYehova, nina mizalwane yezizwe, Mnikeni uYehova uzuko namandla;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:8">96:8</a> Mnikeni uYehova uzuko lwegama lakhe; Thwalani umnikelo,  nize ezintendelezweni zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:9">96:9</a> Mnquleni uYehova, nivethe ezingcwele, Thuthumelani phambi kwakhe, nonke hlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:10">96:10</a> Yithini ezintlangeni, UYehova ngukumkani, Liya kuzinza ngoko elimiweyo, lingashukumi, Uya kugweba phakathi kwezizwe ngokuthe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:11">96:11</a> Liya kuvuya izulu, Ligcobe ihlabathi; Luya kugquma ulwandle, nenzaliseko yalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:12">96:12</a> Liya kudlamka ilizwe, nento yonke ekulo, Ize imemelele yonke imithi yehlathi</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:13">96:13</a> Phambi koYehova, ngokuba esiza, Ngokuba esiza kugweba ihlabathi. Uya kuligweba elimiweyo ngobulungisa, Nezizwe ngokunyanisa kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:1">97:1</a> UYehova ngukumkani; liyagcoba ihlabathi, Ziyavuya iziqithi ezininzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:2">97:2</a> Ngamafu nesithokothoko ngeenxa zonke kuye, Bubulungisa nokusesikweni ummiso wetrone yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:3">97:3</a> Kuhamba umlilo phambi kwakhe; Ulenya ababandezeli bakhe ngeenxa zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:4">97:4</a> Ikhanyisa elimiweyo imibane yakhe; Uyabona umhlaba,  uzibhija-bhije.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:5">97:5</a> Iintaba zinyibilika njengomthwebeba phambi koYehova, Phambi kweNkosi yehlabathi lonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:6">97:6</a> Izulu lixela ubulungisa bakhe, Zilubone uzuko lwakhe zonke izizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:7">97:7</a> Badanile bonke abakhonza umfanekiso oqingqiweyo, Abaqhayisa ngeento ezingento; Bayamnqula bonke oothixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:8">97:8</a> Iyeva, iyavuya iZiyon, Ziyagcoba iintombi zakwaYuda, Ngenxa yemigwebo yakho, Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:9">97:9</a> Ngokuba nguwe, Yehova, Osenyangweni phezu kwehlabathi lonke; Unyukile kunene ngaphezu koothixo bonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:10">97:10</a> Bathandi bakaYehova, kuthiyeni okubi. Umgcini wemiphefumlo yabenceba bakhe Uya kubahlangula esandleni sabangendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:11">97:11</a> Ukukhanya likuhlwayelelwe ilungisa, Novuyo baluhlwayelelwe abantliziyo zithe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:12">97:12</a> Vuyani ngoYehova, malungisa, Nibulele isikhumbuzo sakhe esingcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:1">98:1</a> Umhobe. Vumani kuYehova ingoma entsha, Ngokuba wenze imisebenzi ebalulekileyo; Simzuzele uloyiso isandla sakhe sokunene, nengalo yakhe engcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:2">98:2</a> Ulwazisile uYehova usindiso lwakhe, Ubutyhilile emehlweni eentlanga ubulungisa bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:3">98:3</a> Ukhumbule inceba yakhe nokunyanisa kwakhe kwindlu kaSirayeli; Zilubonile zonke iziphelo zehlabathi usindiso loThixo wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:4">98:4</a> Dumani kuYehova, nonke hlabathi, Gqobhokelani ekumemeleleni, nibethe uhadi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:5">98:5</a> Mbetheleni uhadi uYehova, Uhadi nelizwi lengoma;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:6">98:6</a> Ngamaxilongo nezwi lesigodlo Dumani phambi koKumkani uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:7">98:7</a> Malugqume ulwandle nenzaliseko yalo, Elimiweyo nabemi balo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:8">98:8</a> Imilambo mayibethe izandla, Zimemelele kunye iintaba</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:9">98:9</a> Phambi koYehova, ngokuba esiza kugweba ihlabathi. Uya kuligweba elimiweyo ngobulungisa, Izizwe ngokuthe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:1">99:1</a> UYehova nguKumkani, ziyagungqa izizwe; Ulohlala ekerubhini,  liyashukuma ihlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:2">99:2</a> UYehova mkhulu eZiyon; Uphakamile ngaphezu kwezizwe zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:3">99:3</a> Baya kulibulela igama lakho elikhulu eloyikekayo; Ngokuba ungcwele yena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:4">99:4</a> Amandla okumkani athanda okusesikweni; Uwazimasile wena ngokuthe tye; Wenze okusesikweni nobulungisa kwaYakobi wena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:5">99:5</a> Mphakamiseni uYehova, uThixo wethu, Niqubude esitulweni seenyawo zakhe; Ngokuba ungcwele yena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:6">99:6</a> OoMoses noAron phakathi kwababingeleli bakhe, NoSamuweli phakathi kwabalinqulayo igama lakhe, Baye bebiza kuYehova,  wabaphendula yena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:7">99:7</a> Wathetha kubo esemqulwini welifu; Bazigcina izingqino zakhe, Nommiselo awabanika wona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:8">99:8</a> Yehova, Thixo wethu, wabaphendula wena, Waba nguThixo oxolelayo kubo, Ongoziphindezelayo iintlondi zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:9">99:9</a> Mphakamiseni uYehova, uThixo wethu, Niqubude entabeni yakhe engcwele; Ngokuba ungcwele uYehova uThixo wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:1">100:1</a> Umhobe wombingelelo wokubulela. Dumani kuYehova, nonke hlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:2">100:2</a> Mkhonzeni uYehova nivuya; Yizani phambi kwakhe nimemelela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:3">100:3</a> Yazini ukuba uYehova nguThixo yena; Wasenza yena,  asisithi; Singabantu bakhe nezimvu ezaluswa nguye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:4">100:4</a> Ngenani emasangweni akhe nibulela, Ezintendelezweni zakhe nidumisa; Bulelani kuye, bongani igama lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:5">100:5</a> Ngokuba uYehova ulungile, Inceba yakhe ingunaphakade,  Ukunyaniseka kwakhe kukwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:1">101:1</a> EkaDavide. Umhobe. Ndiya kuvuma ngenceba nangomgwebo;  Ndiya kukubethela uhadi, Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:2">101:2</a> Ndiya kuqiqa indlela yengqibelelo; Uya kuza nini na kum?  Ndiya kuhamba ngengqibelelo yentliziyo yam Phakathi kwendlu yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:3">101:3</a> Andiyi kubeka phambi kwamehlo am Nto inobutshijolo.  Ukwenza ngokunxaxha ndikuthiyile, Akuyi kunamathela kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:4">101:4</a> Intliziyo ejibilizayo iya kukhwelela kude kum; Into embi andiyi kuyazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:5">101:5</a> Omhlebayo ummelwane wakhe ngasese, Lowo ndiya kumbhangisa.  Omehlo aqwayingileyo, ontliziyo igungubeleyo, Lowo andinakumthwala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:6">101:6</a> Amehlo am akwabanyanisayo ezweni, Ukuba bandiphahle;  Ohamba ngendlela yengqibelelo, Lowo makandilungiselele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:7">101:7</a> Akayi kuhlala phakathi kwendlu yam Owenza inkohliso;  Othetha ubuxoki akayi kuqina Phambi kwamehlo am.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:8">101:8</a> Imiso ngemiso, ndiya kubabhangisa Bonke abangendawo belizwe, Ukuze ndibanqumle emzini kaYehova Bonke abasebenzi bobutshinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:1">102:1</a> Umthandazo wolusizana xa atyhafileyo, ephalaza iinkalazo zakhe phambi koYehova. Yehova, wuve umthandazo wam, Kufike kuwe ukuzibika kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:2">102:2</a> Musa ukubusithelisa ubuso bakho kum ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam, Ndithobele indlebe yakho; Ngemini endidanduluka ngayo khawuleza undiphendule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:3">102:3</a> Ngokuba iyaphela imihla yam njengomsi; Amathambo am avutha njengeziko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:4">102:4</a> Ibethwe yoma njengomfuno intliziyo yam, Ngokuba ndilibele nokudla ukudla kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:5">102:5</a> Ngenxa yezwi lokugcuma kwam Amathambo am atshele enyameni yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:6">102:6</a> Ndifana nengcwangube yentlango, Ndinjengesikhova sasemanxoweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:7">102:7</a> Andilali; Ndinjengentaka eyodwa phezu kwendlu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:8">102:8</a> Imini yonke ziyandingcikiva iintshaba zam, Abandigezelayo bathuka ngam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:9">102:9</a> Ngokuba ndidle uthuthu njengesonka, Into endiyiselayo ndiyiphithikeze nezililo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:10">102:10</a> Ngenxa yokubhabhama kwakho noburhalarhume bakho; Ngokuba undifunqule wandilahla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:11">102:11</a> Imihla yam injengokoluka kwamathunzi; Mna ndomile njengomfuno.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:12">102:12</a> Ke wena, Yehova, uhleli ngonaphakade, Inkumbuzo yakho ikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:13">102:13</a> Uya kusuk ume, uyiphathe iZiyon ngemfesane; Ngokuba lixesha lokuyibabala eli, ngokuba lifikile ixesha elimisiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:14">102:14</a> Ngokuba abakhonzi bakho bakholiswe ngamatye ayo, Uthuli lwayo banofefe ngalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:15">102:15</a> Ziya kuloyika iintlanga igama likaYehova, Nookumkani bonke behlabathi ubuqaqawuli bakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:16">102:16</a> Ngokuba eyakhile iZiyon uYehova, Wabonakala ebuqaqawulini bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:17">102:17</a> Uwubhekile umthandazo wabachushuluzayo, Akawudela umthandazo wabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:18">102:18</a> Oko kuya kubhalelwa isizukulwana esizayo, Abantu abaza kudalwa badumise uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:19">102:19</a> Ngokuba uqondele, esendaweni yakhe ephezulu engcwele;  Wondela ehlabathini esemazulwini uYehova,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:20">102:20</a> Ukuba akuve ukugcuma kwabakhonkxiweyo, Abakhulule oonyana bokufa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:21">102:21</a> Bancokole eZiyon ngegama likaYehova, Ngendumiso yakhe eYerusalem;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:22">102:22</a> Ekubuthelaneni kwezizwe ndawonye, Nezikumkani, ukuba zikhonze uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:23">102:23</a> Uwathobile endleleni amandla am, Uyinqamle imihla yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:24">102:24</a> Ndithi, Thixo wam, musa ukundisusa phakathi kwemihla yam.  Ikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana iminyaka yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:25">102:25</a> Waliseka kudala ihlabathi; Lisisenzo sezandla zakho izulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:26">102:26</a> Ezo zinto ziya kudaka, wena ke ume; Zona zonke ziya konakala njengengubo, Wozigugisa njengesambatho, ziguge;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:27">102:27</a> Ke wena uhleli unguwe, Iminyaka yakho ayinakuphela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:28">102:28</a> Oonyana babakhonzi bakho baya kuhlala, Imbewu yabo izimaseke phambi kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:1">103:1</a> EkaDavide. Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam, Ilibonge igama lakhe elingcwele into yonke engaphakathi kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:2">103:2</a> Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam, Ungayilibali yonke impatho yakhe entle:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:3">103:3</a> Uloxolela bonke ubugwenxa bakho; Ulophilisa zonke izifo zakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:4">103:4</a> Ulokhulula ubomi bakho esihogweni, Akuthi jize ngenceba nemfesane;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:5">103:5</a> Lo uwuzalisayo umlomo wakho ngento elungileyo, Buhlaziyeke ubutsha bakho njengobokhozi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:6">103:6</a> NguYehova umenzi wemisebenzi yobulungisa, Nezigwebo ngenxa yabacudisiweyo bonke;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:7">103:7</a> Umazisi weendlela zakhe kuMoses, Wezenzo zakhe ezincamisayo koonyana bakaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:8">103:8</a> Unemfesane enobabalo uYehova, Uzeka kade umsindo, mkhulu ngenceba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:9">103:9</a> Akaphiki kuphele, Akawugcini umsindo ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:10">103:10</a> Akenzi kuthi ngokwezono zethu, Akasiphathi ngokobugwenxa bethu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:11">103:11</a> Ngokuba injengokuphakama kwezulu phezu komhlaba, Ukuba namandla, inceba yakhe kwabamoyikayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:12">103:12</a> Kunjengokuba kude kwempumalanga entshonalanga,  Ukulukhwelelisa kwakhe kuthi ukreqo lwethu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:13">103:13</a> Kunjengokusikwa yimfesane koyise kubantwana, Ukusikwa yimfesane kukaYehova kwabamoyikayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:14">103:14</a> Ngokuba uyakwazi yena ukubunjwa kwethu, Ekhumbula ukuba siluthuli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:15">103:15</a> Hayi, umntu! Injengotyani imihla yakhe; Njengentyantyambo yasendle, kunjalo ukutyatyamba kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:16">103:16</a> Xa uthe umoya wadlula kuyo, ayibikho, Ingabi sazana nayo indawo yayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:17">103:17</a> Ke yona inceba kaYehova ikwabamoyikayo, kususela kwaphakade kude kuse ephakadeni, Nobulungisa bakhe bukoonyana boonyana;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:18">103:18</a> Kwabawugcinileyo umnqophiso wakhe, Kwabazikhumbulayo iziyalezo zakhe ukuba bazenze.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:19">103:19</a> UYehova uyizinzisile emazulwini itrone yakhe, Ubukumkani bakhe bulawula into yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:20">103:20</a> Mbongeni uYehova, nina zithunywa zakhe, Magorha omeleleyo, alenzayo ilizwi lakhe, Ephulaphula isandi selizwi lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:21">103:21</a> Mbongeni uYehova, nonke mikhosi yakhe, Balungiseleli bakhe, benzi bokuthanda kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:22">103:22</a> Mbongeni uYehova, nonke zenzo zakhe, Ezindaweni zonke zobukumkani bakhe. Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:1">104:1</a> Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam. Yehova, Thixo wam, umkhulu kakhulu; Wambethe indili nobungangamela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:2">104:2</a> Ulothi wambu ukukhanya njengengubo. Ulolaneka izulu njengelengalenga lentente;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:3">104:3</a> Ulohlanganisa emanzini imiqadi yamagumbi akhe aphezulu;  Ulowenza amafu inqwelo yakhe, Ulohamba ngamaphiko omoya;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:4">104:4</a> Ulowenza izithunywa zakhe imimoya, Abalungiseleli bakhe umlilo olenyayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:5">104:5</a> Waliseka ihlabathi phezu kwemimiso yalo, Ukuba lingashukunyiswa naphakade kanaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:6">104:6</a> Waligubungela ngamanzi anzongonzongo njengesambatho, Ema amanzi phezu kweentaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:7">104:7</a> Ekukhalimeni kwakho asaba, Ezwini lendudumo yakho abaleka buphuthuphuthu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:8">104:8</a> Kwenyuka iintaba, kwehla izihlambo, Aya kuloo ndawo ubuwasekele yona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:9">104:9</a> Wamisa umda ukuba angegqithi, Angabuye awugubungele umhlaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:10">104:10</a> Ulothuma imithombo iye ezihlanjeni; Ihamba phakathi kweentaba;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:11">104:11</a> Iseza zonke iinyamakazi zasendle; Amaesile asendle aqabula inxano lawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:12">104:12</a> Kuhlala phezu kwayo iintaka zezulu, Zitsholoza phakathi kwamasebe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:13">104:13</a> Uloseza iintaba kumagumbi akhe aphezulu; Uyahlutha umhlaba ziziqhamo zezenzo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:14">104:14</a> Ulontshulisela iinkomo utyani, Nomfuno wokunceda umntu;  Ukuze kuphume isonka emhlabeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:15">104:15</a> Iwayini iyivuyise intliziyo yomntu; Bukhazimle ubuso ngeoli, Isonka siyixhase intliziyo yomntu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:16">104:16</a> Iyahlutha imithi kaYehova, Imisedare yaseLebhanon awayityalayo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:17">104:17</a> Apho zakhela khona iintaka; Ingwamza, isemisipresini indlu yayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:18">104:18</a> Iintaba zona ezo ziphakamileyo zezamagogo, Amawa azimela iimbila.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:19">104:19</a> Inyanga wayenzela amaxesha ayo, Ilanga liyakwazi ukutshona kwalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:20">104:20</a> Wenza ubumnyama wena, kube sebusuku, Ashukume ngabo onke amarhamncwa ehlathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:21">104:21</a> Iingonyama ezintsha zigqumela ukuqwenga, Zifuna ukudla kwazo kuThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:22">104:22</a> Lakuthi chapha ilanga, ziyahlanganisana, Zibuthume ezikhundleni zazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:23">104:23</a> Uyaphuma umntu aye emsebenzini wakhe Nasenkonzweni yakhe,  ahlwise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:24">104:24</a> Hayi, ukuba zininzi izenzo zakho, Yehova! Zonke ziphela uzenze ngobululumko; Uzele umhlaba zizidalwa zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:25">104:25</a> Nalo ulwandle lulukhulu, lubanzi ngeenxa zombini; Kulapho kuzinambuzane zingenakubalwa, Ezincinane kwanezikhulu izinto eziphilileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:26">104:26</a> Kulapho kuhamba iinqanawa; Nango umnenga owawubumbela ukudlala kulo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:27">104:27</a> Zonke ezo nto ziphela zikhangele kuwe, Ukuba uzinike ukudla kwazo ngexesha elililo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:28">104:28</a> Uyazinika, ziyachola; Uyasivula isandla sakho, ziyahlutha kokulungileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:29">104:29</a> Uyabusithelisa ubuso bakho, ziyakhwankqiswa;  Uyawuhlanganisa umoya wazo, ziphume umphefumlo, Zibuyele eluthulini lwazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:30">104:30</a> Uthuma umoya wakho, ziyadalwa, Ubuhlaziye ubuso bomhlaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:31">104:31</a> Ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova mabube ngunaphakade; UYehova makavuye ngezenzo zakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:32">104:32</a> Ulobheka emhlabeni, uzamazame; Uchukumisa iintaba,  ziqhume.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:33">104:33</a> Ndiya kuvuma kuYehova lo gama ndidla ubomi, Ndiya kumbethela uhadi uThixo wam ekubeni ndingokhoyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:34">104:34</a> Makube nencasa kuye ukucamngca kwam; Mna ndiya kuvuya ngoYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:35">104:35</a> Mabagqitywe ehlabathini aboni, Bangabi sabakho abangendawo. Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam, Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:1">105:1</a> Bulelani kuYehova, nqulani igama lakhe; Yazisani ezizweni izenzo zakhe ezincamisileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:2">105:2</a> Vumani kuye, mbetheleni uhadi; Xoxani ngemisebenzi yakhe yonke ebalulekileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:3">105:3</a> Qhayisani ngegama lakhe elingcwele; Mayivuye intliziyo yabamquqelayo uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:4">105:4</a> Ngxamelani uYehova namandla akhe; Funani ubuso bakhe ngamaxesha onke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:5">105:5</a> Khumbulani imisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo awayenzayo,  Izimanga zakhe, nezigwebo zomlomo wakhe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:6">105:6</a> Mbewu ka-Abraham, yomkhonzi wakhe, Nyana bakaYakobi,  banyulwa bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:7">105:7</a> NguYehova uThixo wethu yena; Zisehlabathini lonke izigwebo zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:8">105:8</a> Uwukhumbula ngonaphakade umnqophiso wakhe, Ilizwi awalimisela iwaka lezizukulwana;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:9">105:9</a> Awanqophisana ngalo noAbraham, Awalifungela uIsake;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:10">105:10</a> Awalimisayo ukuba libe ngummiselo kuYakobi, Libe ngumnqophiso ongunaphakade kuSirayeli;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:11">105:11</a> Esithi, Ndikunika ilizwe lakwaKanan, Libe licandelo lelifa lenu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:12">105:12</a> Besengamadoda ambalwa, Bebancinane, bengabaphambukeli kulo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:13">105:13</a> Babehamba besuka kolunye uhlanga, baye kolunye uhlanga,  Besuka kobunye ubukumkani, baye kwabanye abantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:14">105:14</a> Akavumelanga mntu ukuba abacudise, Wohlwaya ookumkani ngenxa yabo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:15">105:15</a> Esithi, Musani ukubachukumisa abathanjiswa bam, Musani ukubaphatha kakubi abaprofeti bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:16">105:16</a> Wabiza indlala, yeza phezu kwelizwe, Wawaphula wonke umsimelelo osisonka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:17">105:17</a> Wathuma indoda phambi kwabo; Kwathengiswa ngoYosefu, waba likhoboka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:18">105:18</a> Bazicinezela iinyawo zakhe ngamakhamandela, Wafika umphefumlo wakhe esinyithini;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:19">105:19</a> Kwada kwalixesha lokufika kwelizwi lakhe, Intetho kaYehova yamnyibilikisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:20">105:20</a> Ukumkani wathuma, wamkhulula, Umlawuli wezizwe wamvulela;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:21">105:21</a> Wamenza inkosi yendlu yakhe, Umlawuli wemfuyo yakhe yonke,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:22">105:22</a> Ukuba abakhonkxe abathetheli bakhe ngokuzithandela kwakhe, Amadoda akhe amakhulu awafundise ubulumko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:23">105:23</a> Waza uSirayeli waya eYiputa, UYakobi waphambukela ezweni lakwaHam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:24">105:24</a> Wabaqhamisa kakhulu abantu bakhe, Wabomeleza ngaphezu kwababandezeli babo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:25">105:25</a> Wazijika iintliziyo zabo, ukuba babathiye abantu bakhe,  Babaqhathanisele abakhonzi bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:26">105:26</a> Wathuma uMoses, umkhonzi wakhe, NoAron awamnyulayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:27">105:27</a> Bazenza kubo iindawo zemiqondiso yakhe, Nezimanga zakhe ezweni lakwaHam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:28">105:28</a> Wathumela ubumnyama, kwaba mnyama; Ababa nakuwaphikisa amazwi akhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:29">105:29</a> Wawaguqula amanzi abo, aba ligazi, Wazibulala iintlanzi zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:30">105:30</a> Ilizwe labo lanyakazela amasele Ezingontsini zookumkani babo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:31">105:31</a> Wathetha, zafika izibawu, Iingcongconi, emideni yabo yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:32">105:32</a> Wabanika isichotho, saba yimvula; Umlilo walenya ezweni labo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:33">105:33</a> Wayibetha imidiliya yabo nemikhiwane yabo, Wayishwaqa imithi yemida yabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:34">105:34</a> Wathetha, kwafika iinkumbi ezandayo, Nezikhothululayo,  into engenakubalwa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:35">105:35</a> Zayidla imifuno yonke ezweni labo, Zazidla iziqhamo zomhlaba wabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:36">105:36</a> Waza wababulala bonke abamazibulo ezweni labo, Intlahlela yamandla abo onke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:37">105:37</a> Wabakhupha ke abakhe benesilivere negolide, Akwabakho ukhubekayo ezizweni zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:38">105:38</a> Lavuya iYiputa ekuphumeni kwabo, Ngokuba lifikelwe kukunkwantyisa kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:39">105:39</a> Waneka ilifu lokubasitha, Nomlilo wokukhanyisa ebusuku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:40">105:40</a> Babiza, wazisa izagwityi, Wabahluthisa nangesonka sasezulwini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:41">105:41</a> Wavula iliwa, abaleka amanzi, Ahamba engumlambo emqwebedwini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:42">105:42</a> Ngokuba wakhumbula ilizwi lakhe elingcwele, Wakhumbula uAbraham umkhonzi wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:43">105:43</a> Wabakhupha abantu bakhe benemihlali, Abanyulwa bakhe bememelela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:44">105:44</a> Wabanika amazwe eentlanga, Bayihlutha inzuzo yokwaphuka kwezizwe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:45">105:45</a> Ukuze bayigcine imimiselo yakhe, Bayibambe imiyalelo yakhe. Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:1">106:1</a> Haleluya! Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile, Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:2">106:2</a> Ngubani na onokuzixela izenzo zobugorha bukaYehova,  Onokuyivakalisa yonke indumiso yakhe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:3">106:3</a> Hayi, uyolo lwabaligcinayo isiko, Lwabenza ubulungisa ngamaxesha onke!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:4">106:4</a> Ndikhumbule, Yehova, ekwenzeni kwakho isisa kubantu bakho;  Ndiyelele ngosindiso lwakho,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:5">106:5</a> Ukuze ndibone inyhweba yabanyulwa bakho, Ndivuye ekuvuyeni kohlanga lwakho, Ndiqhayise kunye nelifa lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:6">106:6</a> Sonile, thina noobawo; Senze ubugwenxa, senze okungendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:7">106:7</a> Oobawo abayiqiqanga eYiputa imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo; Ababukhumbulanga ubuninzi beenceba zakho;  Baphika elwandle, eLwandle oluBomvu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:8">106:8</a> Wabasindisa ngenxa yegama lakhe, Ukuze abazise ubugorha bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:9">106:9</a> Walukhalimela uLwandle oluBomvu, loma, Wabahambisa emanzini anzongonzongo kwanga kusentlango.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:10">106:10</a> Wabasindisa esandleni sobathiyayo, Wabakhulula esandleni sotshaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:11">106:11</a> Amanzi abagubungela ababandezeli babo, Akwasala namnye kubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:12">106:12</a> Bakholwa ke ngamazwi akhe, Bayivuma indumiso yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:13">106:13</a> Kanti bahle bazilibala izenzo zakhe, Abalilinda icebo lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:14">106:14</a> Bakhanukile entlango, Bamlinga uThixo enkangala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:15">106:15</a> Wabanika abakubizayo; Wathumela ukungcumbeka emphefumlweni wabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:16">106:16</a> Bamenzela umona uMoses eminqubeni, NoAron ongcwele kaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:17">106:17</a> Wavuleka umhlaba, wamginya uDatan, Waliselela ibandla lika-Abhiram;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:18">106:18</a> Umlilo walitshisa ibandla labo, Amalangatye abalenya abangendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:19">106:19</a> Benza ithole eHorebhe, Baqubuda emfanekisweni otyhidiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:20">106:20</a> Balwananisa uzuko lwabo Ngento emilise okwenkomo edla utyani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:21">106:21</a> Bamlibala uThixo, umsindisi wabo, Owenza imisebenzi emikhulu eYiputa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:22">106:22</a> Imisebenzi ebalulekileyo ezweni lakwaHam, Imisebenzi eyoyikekayo eLwandle oluBomvu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:23">106:23</a> Wathi uya kubatshabalalisa, Koko wesukayo uMoses,  umnyulwa wakhe, Wema ethubeni phambi kwakhe, Ebuyisa ubushushu bakhe, ukuba angatshabalalisi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:24">106:24</a> Balicekisa ilizwe elinqwenelekayo, Abakholwa lilizwi lakhe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:25">106:25</a> Bakrokra ezintenteni zabo, Abaliphulaphula izwi likaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:26">106:26</a> Wabaphakamisela isandla sakhe, Wafungela ukuba abawise entlango;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:27">106:27</a> Ayiwise imbewu yabo phakathi kweentlanga, Abachithachithe emazweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:28">106:28</a> Bazibandakanya noBhahali-pehore, Badla imibingelelo yabafileyo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:29">106:29</a> Bamqumbisa ngeentlondi zabo; Sagaleleka phakathi kwabo isibetho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:30">106:30</a> Wesuka wema uPinehasi, walamla; Sathintelwa isibetho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:31">106:31</a> Oko kwabalelwa kuye ekuthini bubulungisa Izizukulwana ngezizukulwana kude kuse ephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:32">106:32</a> Bamqumbisa emanzini aseMeribha, Kwehla ububi kuMoses ngenxa yabo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:33">106:33</a> Ngokuba bawuphikisa umoya wakhe, Waphololoza ke ngomlomo wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:34">106:34</a> Abazitshabalalisa izizwe, Awayethethe ngazo kubo uYehova;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:35">106:35</a> Baxubana neentlanga ezo, Bafunda izenzo zazo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:36">106:36</a> Bakhonza izithixo zazo, Yaba sisirhintyelo kubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:37">106:37</a> Babingelela ngoonyana babo nangeentombi zabo kwiidemon;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:38">106:38</a> Baphalaza igazi elimsulwa, Igazi loonyana babo neleentombi zabo, Ababingelela ngabo kwizithixo zakwaKanan;  Lahlanjelwa ilizwe ngamagazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:39">106:39</a> Baba ziinqambi ngezenzo zabo, Bahenyuza ngeentlondi zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:40">106:40</a> Wavutha ke umsindo kaYehova kubantu bakhe, Laba lisikizi kuye ilifa lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:41">106:41</a> Wabanikela ezandleni zeentlanga, Balawulwa ngababathiyileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:42">106:42</a> Zabaxina iintshaba zabo, Bathotyelwa phantsi kwezandla zazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:43">106:43</a> Zibe zininzi izihlandlo ebahlangula; Ke bona bamphikisa ngamaqhinga abo, Bonakala bubugwenxa babo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:44">106:44</a> Noko ke wakunonelela ukubandezelwa kwabo, Akuva ukuhlahlamba kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:45">106:45</a> Wawukhumbula ngenxa yabo umnqophiso wakhe, Wazohlwaya ngenxa yobuninzi beenceba zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:46">106:46</a> Wabafumanisa imfesane Phambi kwabo bonke abaye bebathimbile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:47">106:47</a> Sisindise, Yehova, Thixo wethu, Sibuthe ezintlangeni,  Ukuze sibulele kwigama lakho elingcwele, Sizingce ngendumiso yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:48">106:48</a> Makabongwe uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli, Kususela kwaphakade kude kuse ephakadeni. Mabathi bonke abantu, Amen.  Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:1">107:1</a> Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile, Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:2">107:2</a> Mabatsho abakhululwa bakaYehova, Awabakhululayo esandleni sombandezeli;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:3">107:3</a> Wababutha emazweni, Empumalanga nasentshonalanga, Entla naselwandle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:4">107:4</a> Badinga entlango, endleleni esenkanga, la, Abafumana mzi wakuhlala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:5">107:5</a> Belambile, benxaniwe, Watyhafa phakathi kwabo umphefumlo wabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:6">107:6</a> Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni yabo, Wabahlangula ekucuthekeni kwabo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:7">107:7</a> Wabanyathelisa endleleni ethe tye, Ukuba baye kumzi wokuhlala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:8">107:8</a> Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe, Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:9">107:9</a> Kuba ewuhluthisile umphefumlo otshobayo, Wawuzalisa ngokulungileyo umphefumlo olambileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:10">107:10</a> Behleli emnyameni nasethunzini lokufa, Bekhonkxwe yimbandezelo nasisinyithi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:11">107:11</a> Ngokuba bephikise amazwi kaThixo, Belitshitshisa icebo lOsenyangweni:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:12">107:12</a> Wayithoba intliziyo yabo ngokubasebenzisa kanzima;  Bakhubeka, akwabakho mncedi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:13">107:13</a> Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni yabo; Wabasindisa ekucuthekeni kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:14">107:14</a> Wabakhupha emnyameni nasethunzini lokufa, Waziqhawula iimbophelelo zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:15">107:15</a> Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe, Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:16">107:16</a> Kuba ezaphule iingcango zobhedu, Wayixakaxa imivalo yesinyithi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:17">107:17</a> Abamathileyo, ngenxa yendlela yokukreqa kwabo, Nangenxa yobugwenxa babo, bacinezelwa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:18">107:18</a> Konke ukudla kwaba lisikizi kumphefumlo wabo, Bafika emasangweni okufa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:19">107:19</a> Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni yabo, Wabasindisa ekucuthekeni kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:20">107:20</a> Wathumela ilizwi lakhe, wabaphilisa, Wabasiza ezihogweni zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:21">107:21</a> Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe, Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:22">107:22</a> Mababingelele imibingelelo yombulelo, Bancokole ngezenzo zakhe bememelela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:23">107:23</a> Abaya elwandle ngeenqanawa, Benze ishishini emanzini amaninzi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:24">107:24</a> Bazibona bona izenzo zikaYehova, Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo enzulwini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:25">107:25</a> Watsho, wavusa umoya ovuthuzayo, Waphakamisa amaza ayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:26">107:26</a> Banyuka basinga ezulwini, behla basinga emanzini enzonzobila; Umphefumlo wabo uthe amandla bububi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:27">107:27</a> Bathendeleka, bahexa njengenxila, Butshone bonke ubulumko babo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:28">107:28</a> Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni yabo Wabakhupha ekucuthekeni kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:29">107:29</a> Ukumisile ukuvuthuza, kwathi cwaka, Amaza ayo azola;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:30">107:30</a> Bavuya ke, kuba edambile; Wabafikisa echwebeni abalilangazelelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:31">107:31</a> Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe, Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:32">107:32</a> Mabamphakamise ebandleni labantu, Bamdumise embuthweni yamadoda amakhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:33">107:33</a> Uyenze imilambo yaba yintlango, Namathende amanzi aba ngumhlaba onxaniweyo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:34">107:34</a> Ilizwe elineziqhamo laba leletyuwa, Ngenxa yezinto ezimbi zabemi balo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:35">107:35</a> Uyenze intlango yaba lidike elinamanzi, Ilizwe elingumqwebedu laba ngamathende amanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:36">107:36</a> Wabahlalisa khona abalambileyo, Bamisa umzi wokuhlala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:37">107:37</a> Bahlwayela amasimi, batyala izidiliya, Bavelisa iziqhamo,  baba nongeniselo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:38">107:38</a> Wabasikelela, banda kunene, Iinkomo zabo akazinciphisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:39">107:39</a> Bancipha, basibekeka Ngokukhanyangwa bububi nesingqala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:40">107:40</a> Uwagalele ngendelo amanene, Wawadingisa enyanyeni,  kungekho ndlela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:41">107:41</a> Walisa engxondeni ihlwempu, kude nengcinezelo, Walenzela imizalwana yanjengomhlambi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:42">107:42</a> Baya kubona abathe tye, bavuye, Bonke ubugqwetha buvale umlomo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:43">107:43</a> Lowo ulumkileyo makazigcine ezi ndawo, Azigqale iinceba zikaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:1">108:1</a> Ingoma. Umhobe kaDavide. Izimasekile intliziyo yam,  Thixo, Ndiya kuvuma, ndibethe uhadi, Kwanozuko lwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:2">108:2</a> Vukani, mrhubhe nohadi; Ndiya kusiphangela isifingo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:3">108:3</a> Ndiya kubulela kuwe phakathi kwezizwe, Yehova,  Ndikubethele uhadi phakathi kwezizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:4">108:4</a> Ngokuba inkulu ngaphezu kwezulu inceba yakho, Yada yesa esibhakabhakeni inyaniso yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:5">108:5</a> Ziphakamise ngaphezu kwezulu, Thixo, Bube phezu kwehlabathi lonke ubuqaqawuli bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:6">108:6</a> Ukuze zihlangulwe iintanda zakho, Sindisa ngesandla sakho sokunene, undiphendule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:7">108:7</a> UThixo uthethe engcwele; mandivuyelele, Ndimabe uShekem,  ndiyilinganisele intili yaseSukoti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:8">108:8</a> Ngowam uGiliyadi, ngowam uManase, UEfrayim sisigcina-ntloko sam, UYuda yintonga yam yommiselo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:9">108:9</a> UMowabhi sisitya sam sokuhlambela, Ndiyiphosa kuEdom imbadada yam; Ndiduma ngelamaFilisti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:10">108:10</a> Ngubani na owondisa emzini onqatyisiweyo, Ngubani na owondikhaphela kwaEdom?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:11">108:11</a> Asinguwe na, Thixo, lo usihlambileyo? Akwaphuma, Thixo,  nemikhosi yethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:12">108:12</a> Sincede kumbandezeli wethu; Alunto yanto usindiso lomntu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:13">108:13</a> NgoThixo siya kweyisa, Abagqushe yena ababandezeli bethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:1">109:1</a> Kumongameli; ekaDavide. Umhobe. Thixo wendumiso yam,  musa ukuthi tu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:2">109:2</a> Ngokuba bandakhamisele umlomo ongendawo, nomlomo onenkohliso; Bathetha ngam ngolwimi lobuxoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:3">109:3</a> Bandijikele ngeentetho zentiyo; Balwa nam ngelize.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:4">109:4</a> Ekubeni mna ndibathanda, bona bayandichasa, Ndibe mna ndithandaza.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:5">109:5</a> Endaweni yobulungisa bandibuyekeza ngobubi; Ekubeni mna ndibathanda, bona bayandithiya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:6">109:6</a> Misa ongendawo, abe ngumveleli wakhe, Eme uSathana ngasekunene kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:7">109:7</a> Ekuthethweni kwetyala makaphume engongendawo, Nomthandazo wakhe ube sisono.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:8">109:8</a> Imihla yakhe mayibe mbalwa, Mabuthatyathwe ngomnye ubuveleli bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:9">109:9</a> Oonyana bakhe mababe ziinkedama, Nomkakhe abe ngumhlolokazi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:10">109:10</a> Babhadule bebhadula oonyana bakhe, becela, Bengqiba,  bekude namanxuwa akowabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:11">109:11</a> Umboleki-mali makakushwankathele konke anako, Abasemzini baphange ukuxelenga kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:12">109:12</a> Makungabikho wolulela nceba kuye, Kungabikho uzibabalayo iinkedama zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:13">109:13</a> Izivela-mva zakhe mazibe zezokunqunyulwa, Igama lazo licinywe esizukulwaneni esizayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:14">109:14</a> Mabukhunjulwe nguYehova ubugwenxa booyise, Singacinywa isono sonina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:15">109:15</a> Masibe phambi koYehova ngamaxesha onke, Akunqumle ehlabathini ukukhunjulwa kwabo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:16">109:16</a> Ngenxa enokuba engakukhumbulanga ukwenza inceba,  Etshutshise indoda elusizana, Elihlwempu, enentliziyo eyothukileyo, ukuba ayibulale.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:17">109:17</a> Ewe, wathanda ukuqalekisa, kwamfikela; Akakufuna ukusikelela, kwakhwelela kude kuye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:18">109:18</a> Wambatha ukuqalekisa kwanga yingubo yakhe, Kwangena embilinini wakhe njengamanzi, Nanjengeoli emathanjeni akhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:19">109:19</a> Makube njengengubo kuye, azithe wambu ngayo, Kube luqhwemesha, alunxibe amaxesha onke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:20">109:20</a> Nguwo lowo umvuzo wabandichasayo, ophuma kuYehova,  Wabathetha okubi ngomphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:21">109:21</a> Ke wena Yehova, Nkosi, ndenzele ngenxa yegama lakho;  Ngokokuba ilungile inceba yakho; ndihlangule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:22">109:22</a> Ngokuba ndilusizana, ndilihlwempu, Intliziyo yam ihlatyiwe phakathi kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:23">109:23</a> Ndinjengethunzi xa lolukayo, ndiyemka; Ndiphetshethwa njengenkumbi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:24">109:24</a> Amadolo am ayagexa kukuzila ukudla, Nenyama yam ibhityile, tu ukutyeba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:25">109:25</a> Ndithe ndasisingcikivo kubo; Bendibona, bahlunguzela intloko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:26">109:26</a> Ndincede, Yehova, Thixo wam, Ndisindise ngokwenceba yakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:27">109:27</a> Bazi ukuba sisandla sakho eso, Ukuba kukwenza kwakho,  Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:28">109:28</a> Bayaqalekisa aba, uyasikelela wena; Besukile bema, baya kudana; uya kubuya yena umkhonzi wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:29">109:29</a> Abandichasayo baya kwambatha ihlazo, Bazithi wambu ukudana njengengubo yokwaleka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:30">109:30</a> Ndiya kubulela kakhulu kuYehova ngomlomo wam, Ndimdumise phakathi kwabaninzi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:31">109:31</a> Kuba emi ekunene kolihlwempu, Ukuba amsindise kwabawugwebayo umphefumlo wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:1">110:1</a> EkaDavide. Umhobe. Utsho uYehova eNkosini yam ukuthi,  Hlala ngasekunene kwam, Ndide iintshaba zakho ndizenze Isitulo seenyawo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:2">110:2</a> Intonga yamandla akho uya kuyithumela uYehova, ivela eZiyon, esithi, Yiba nobukhosi phakathi kweentshaba zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:3">110:3</a> Abantu bakho baya kuzinikela ngeentliziyo, ngemini yakho yokuphuma umkhosi; Bebethe ezingcwele, ekuphumeni kwesifingo,  Uza kuwe umbethe womlisela wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:4">110:4</a> Ufungile uYehova, akayi kuzohlwaya; uthe, Ungumbingeleli ngonaphakade wena Ngokohlobo lukaMelkitsedeke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:5">110:5</a> INkosi ngasekunene kwakho Iya kuphalusa ookumkani ngemini yomsindo wayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:6">110:6</a> Iya kugweba phakathi kweentlanga, kuzale zizidumbu;  Iphaluse intloko ezweni elibanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:7">110:7</a> Endleleni iya kusela emlanjaneni; Ngenxa yoko iya kuphakamisa intloko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:1">111:1</a> Haleluya! Ndiya kubulela kuYehova ngentliziyo yonke,  Elucweyweni lwabathe tye nasebandleni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:2">111:2</a> Zikhulu izenzo zikaYehova, Zezokungxokwa iintsingiselo zazo zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:3">111:3</a> Unendili nobungangamela umsebenzi wakhe, Ubulungisa bakhe bumi ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:4">111:4</a> Uyenzele ukuze ikhunjulwe imisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo;  Unobabalo nemfesane uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:5">111:5</a> Ubaphe ukudla abamoyikayo; Uwukhumbule ngonaphakade umnqophiso wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:6">111:6</a> Ubabonise abantu bakhe amandla ezenzo zakhe, Ebanika ilifa leentlanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:7">111:7</a> Izenzo zezandla zakhe ziyinyaniso nesiko; Zithembekile zonke iziyalezo zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:8">111:8</a> Zizimasekile nanini nangonaphakade; Zenziwe ngenyaniso,  zithe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:9">111:9</a> Ubathumele abantu bakhe inkululeko; Uwumisele ngonaphakade umnqophiso wakhe; Lingcwele, liyoyikeka, igama lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:10">111:10</a> Ingqalo yobulumko kukoyika uYehova, Banengqiqo elungileyo bonke abenza ngako; Indumiso yakhe ihlala imi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:1">112:1</a> Haleluya! Hayi, uyolo lomntu omoyikayo uYehova,  Oyinoneleleyo kunene imithetho yakhe!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:2">112:2</a> Iya kuba nobugorha ehlabathini imbewu yakhe; Isizukulwana sabathe tye sisikelelwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:3">112:3</a> Bubuncwane nobutyebi endlwini yakhe; Ubulungisa bakhe buhlala bumi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:4">112:4</a> Baphunyelwa kukukhanya ebumnyameni abathe tye, Benobabalo,  nemfesane, nobulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:5">112:5</a> Unoyolo umntu obabalayo, aboleke; Uya kuyimisa intetho yakhe ematyaleni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:6">112:6</a> Ngokuba akayi kushukunyiswa naphakade; Uya kuba lilungisa elikhunjulwa ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:7">112:7</a> Akoyikiswa ziindaba ezimbi; Iqinisekile intliziyo yakhe,  ikholose ngoYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:8">112:8</a> Izimasekile intliziyo yakhe, akoyiki; Uya kuda ababonele ababandezeli bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:9">112:9</a> Uyahlakaza, upha amahlwempu; Ubulungisa bakhe buhlala bumi, Uphondo lwakhe luphakamile, lunozuko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:10">112:10</a> Ongendawo yena uya kukubona, aqumbe, Atshixize amazinyo,  anyibilike; Umnqweno wongendawo uyadaka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:1">113:1</a> Haleluya! Dumisani, bakhonzi bakaYehova, Dumisani igama likaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:2">113:2</a> Malibongwe igama likaYehova, Kususela ngokunje, kude kuse ephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:3">113:3</a> Kwasekuphumeni kwelanga kuse ekutshoneni kwalo,  Malidunyiswe igama likaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:4">113:4</a> Uphakamile ngaphezu kweentlanga zonke uYehova,  Bungaphezulu kwamazulu ubuqaqawuli bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:5">113:5</a> Ngubani na onjengoYehova, uThixo wethu? Ulohlala phezulu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:6">113:6</a> Uloqondela phantsi; Ezulwini nasemhlabeni?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:7">113:7</a> Ulomvusa eluthulini osweleyo, Ulomphakamisa ezaleni olihlwempu,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:8">113:8</a> Ukuba amhlalise namanene, Amanene abantu bakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:9">113:9</a> Ulohlalisa endlwini umfazi ongazaliyo, Abe ngunobantwana ovuyayo. Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:1">114:1</a> Ekuphumeni kukaSirayeli eYiputa, Kwendlu kaYakobi ebantwini abantetho ingaziwayo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:2">114:2</a> UYuda waba yingcwele yakhe, USirayeli waba sisikumkani sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:3">114:3</a> Ulwandle lwabona, lwasaba, IYordan yabuya umva.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:4">114:4</a> Iintaba zadloba njengeenkunzi zeegusha; Iinduli,  njengamatakane omhlambi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:5">114:5</a> Ubunani na, lulwandlendini, ukuba usabe? Wena Yordan,  ukuba ubuye umva?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:6">114:6</a> Nina zintaba, ukuba nidlobe njengeenkunzi zeegusha? Nina zinduli, njengamatakane omhlambi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:7">114:7</a> Wena hlabathi, zibhijabhije ebusweni beNkosi, Ebusweni boThixo kaYakobi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:8">114:8</a> Uloguqula iliwa libe lidike lamanzi, Iqhwitha libe yimithombo yamanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:1">115:1</a> Ungazukisi thina, Yehova, ungazukisi thina; Zukisa igama lakho, Ngenxa yenceba yakho, ngenxa yenyaniso yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:2">115:2</a> Yini na ukuba zithi iintlanga, Uphi na kaloku uThixo wabo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:3">115:3</a> UThixo wethu ke usemazulwini, Konke akuthandileyo uyakwenza.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:4">115:4</a> Izithixo zazo yisilivere negolide, Zizenzo zezandla zabantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:5">115:5</a> Zinomlomo nje, azithethi; Zinamehlo nje aziboni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:6">115:6</a> Zineendlebe nje, aziva; Zineempumlo nje, azisezeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:7">115:7</a> Izandla zazo aziphathi, Iinyawo zazo azihambi; Azidumzeli ngomqala wazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:8">115:8</a> Boba njengazo abenzi bazo, Bonke abasukuba bekholose ngazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:9">115:9</a> Wena Sirayeli, kholosa ngoYehova; Uncedo lwabo nengweletshetshe yabo nguye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:10">115:10</a> Nani bendlu ka-Aron, kholosani ngoYehova; Uncedo lwabo nengweletshetshe yabo nguye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:11">115:11</a> Nina boyiki bakaYehova, kholosani ngoYehova; Uncedo lwabo nengweletshetshe yabo nguye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:12">115:12</a> UYehova usikhumbule, wosisikelela; Woyisikelela indlu kaSirayeli, Woyisikelela indlu ka-Aron;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:13">115:13</a> Wobasikelela aboyiki bakaYehova, Abancinane kwanabakhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:14">115:14</a> UYehova wonandisa nina ngakumbi nangakumbi, Abandise oonyana benu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:15">115:15</a> Nisikelelekile kuYehova, UMenzi wamazulu nowehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:16">115:16</a> Amazulu ngamazulu kaYehova, Ihlabathi ulinike oonyana babantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:17">115:17</a> Asingabafileyo abamdumisayo uYehova, Asingabo bonke abehlayo baye kwelokuzola.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:18">115:18</a> Thina ke siya kumbonga uYehova, Kususela koku kude kuse ephakadeni. Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:1">116:1</a> Ndiyamthanda, ngokuba uYehova eliva Ilizwi lam,  ukutarhuzisa kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:2">116:2</a> Ngokuba endithobele indlebe yakhe, Ndiya kumnqula ngemihla yam yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:3">116:3</a> Izintya zokufa zandijikela, Iingxingongo zelabafileyo zandifumana, Ndafunyanwa ziimbandezelo nesingqa la.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:4">116:4</a> Ndanqula ke igama likaYehova, ndathi, Yehova, ndiya kukhunga, siza umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:5">116:5</a> UYehova unobabalo, ulilungisa, UThixo wethu unemfesane.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:6">116:6</a> Ngumgcini wabazizidenge uYehova; Ndandiswele,  wandisindisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:7">116:7</a> Buyela ekuphumleni kwakho, mphefumlo wam, Ngokuba uYehova ukuphatha kakuhle;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:8">116:8</a> Ngokuba ewuhlangule umphefumlo wam ekufeni, Iliso lam ezinyembezini, Unyawo lwam ekungqulekeni.</p>
