 <p><a name="an_116:9">116:9</a> Ndiya kuhamba-hamba phambi koYehova Emazweni abaphilileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:10">116:10</a> Ndiyakholwa, xa ndithethayo; Mna ndicinezelekile kunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:11">116:11</a> Ndathi mna ekuphakuzeleni kwam, Bonke abantu ngamaxoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:12">116:12</a> Ndingambuyisela ngantoni na uYehova Konke ukundiphatha kwakhe kakuhle?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:13">116:13</a> Ndophakamisa indebe yosindiso, Ndinqule igama likaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:14">116:14</a> Ewe, ndozizalisa izibhambathiso zam kuYehova, Phambi kwabantu bakhe bonke kalokunje.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:15">116:15</a> Kunqabile emehlweni kaYehova Ukufa kwakhakhe benceba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:16">116:16</a> Okunene, Yehova, ndingumkhonzi wakho, Ndingumkhonzi wakho, unyana womkhonzazana wakho; Uzicombulule iimbophelelo zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:17">116:17</a> Ndiya kubingelela kuwe umbingelelo wombulelo, Ndinqule igama likaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:18">116:18</a> Ewe, ndiya kuzizalisa izibhambathiso zam kuYehova, Phambi kwabantu bakhe bonke,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:19">116:19</a> Ezintendelezweni zendlu kaYehova, Esazulwini sakho,  Yerusalem. Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:1">117:1</a> Mdumiseni uYehova, nonke zintlanga, Mncomeni, nonke zizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:2">117:2</a> Ngokuba inamandla kuthi inceba yakhe, Inyaniso kaYehova ingunaphakade. Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:1">118:1</a> Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile, Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:2">118:2</a> Makathi uSirayeli, Ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:3">118:3</a> Mayithi indlu ka-Aron, Ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:4">118:4</a> Mabathi abamoyikayo uYehova, Ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:5">118:5</a> Ndabiza uYehova ndisengxingongweni; Wandiphendula uYehova,  wandibeka endaweni ebanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:6">118:6</a> UYehova ungakum, andoyiki; Angandenza ntoni na umntu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:7">118:7</a> UYehova ungakum ngokundinceda; Ndiya kubona mna kwabandithiyayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:8">118:8</a> Kulungile ukuzimela ngoYehova, Ngaphezu kokukholosa ngomntu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:9">118:9</a> Kulungile ukuzimela ngoYehova Ngaphezu kokukholosa ngamanene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:10">118:10</a> Zingafanelana zonke iintlanga zindirhawule: Egameni likaYehova inene ndozinqumla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:11">118:11</a> Zingafanelana zindirhawule zandirhawula: Egameni likaYehova inene ndozinqumla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:12">118:12</a> Zingafanelana zindirhawule njengeenyosi: Zocinywa njengomlilo weentsasa; Egameni likaYehova inene ndozinqumla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:13">118:13</a> Undityhale ngamandla wena ukuba ndiwe; Kodwa uYehova wandinceda.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:14">118:14</a> Iqhayiya lam nengoma yam nguYehova, Waba lusindiso kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:15">118:15</a> Izwi lokumemelela nelosindiso lisezintenteni zamalungisa,  lisithi, Isandla sokunene sikaYehova siyeyisa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:16">118:16</a> Isandla sokunene sikaYehova siphakamile; Isandla sokunene sikaYehova siyeyisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:17">118:17</a> Andiyi kufa, ndiya kudla ubomi, Ndibalise ngezenzo zikaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:18">118:18</a> UYehova undithethise kakhulu, Ke akandinikela ekufeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:19">118:19</a> Ndivuleleni amasango obulungisa; Ndiya kungena ngawo,  ndiya kubulela kuYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:20">118:20</a> Nali isango likaYehova, Amalungisa angena ngalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:21">118:21</a> Ndiyabulela kuwe kuba undiphendule, Waba lusindiso kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:22">118:22</a> Ilitye abalilahlayo abakhi Laba yintloko yembombo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:23">118:23</a> Kuvele kuYehova oku, Kungumsebenzi obalulekileyo emehlweni ethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:24">118:24</a> Le yimini ayenzileyo uYehova, Masigcobe sivuye ngayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:25">118:25</a> Yehova, camagu, khawusindise, Yehova, camagu,  khawuhlangule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:26">118:26</a> Makabongwe lo uzayo esegameni likaYehova, Siyanisikelela nina basendlwini kaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:27">118:27</a> UYehova nguThixo, usikhanyisela; Bophelelani umbingelelo womthendeleko ngeentambo, Kude kuye ezimpondweni zesibingelelo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:28">118:28</a> UnguThixo wam, ndiya kubulela kuwe; UnguThixo wam, ndiya kukuphakamisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:29">118:29</a> Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile, Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:1">119:1</a> Hayi, uyolo lwabandlela igqibeleleyo, Bona bahambayo ngomyalelo kaYehova!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:2">119:2</a> Hayi, uyolo lwababambe izingqiniso zakhe, Abamquqelayo ngentliziyo epheleleyo!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:3">119:3</a> Abasebenzi nokusebenza bugqwetha, Bayahamba ngeendlela zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:4">119:4</a> Uzimisile iziyalezo zakho, Ukuba zigcinwe kunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:5">119:5</a> Azaba iindlela zam bezibhekiselwe Ukugcina imimiselo yakho!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:6">119:6</a> Bendingayi kudana ke Ekubhekeni kwam kwimithetho yakho yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:7">119:7</a> Ndiya kubulela kuwe ngentliziyo ethe tye, Ekuzifundeni kwam izigwebo zobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:8">119:8</a> Ndiya kuyigcina imimiselo yakho, Musa ukundishiya kuphele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:9">119:9</a> Umfana uya kuwuqaqambisa ngantoni na umendo wakhe?  Ngokuzigcina ngokwelizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:10">119:10</a> Ndiya kuquqela kuwe ngentliziyo yam yonke; Musa ukundilahlekanisa nemithetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:11">119:11</a> Ndiyibeke intetho yakho entliziyweni yam, Ukuze ndingoni kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:12">119:12</a> Ungowokubongwa, Yehova; Ndifundise imimiselo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:13">119:13</a> Ndiyawabalisa ngemilebe yomlomo wam Onke amasiko omlomo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:14">119:14</a> Ndinemihlali endleleni yezingqiniso zakho, Ngathi kusebuncwaneni bonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:15">119:15</a> Ndiya kucamngca ngeziyalezo zakho, Ndibheke kumendo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:16">119:16</a> Ndiyaziyolisa ngemimiselo yakho; Andiyi kulilibala ilizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:17">119:17</a> Mphathe kakuhle umkhonzi wakho, ndidle ubomi, Ndigcine ilizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:18">119:18</a> Vula amehlo am, ukuba ndiyibone Imisebenzi ebalulekileyo yasemyalelweni wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:19">119:19</a> Ndingumphambukeli ehlabathini, Musa ukuyisithelisa kum imithetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:20">119:20</a> Umphefumlo wam ucumkile ngokulangazelela Amasiko akho ngamaxesha onke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:21">119:21</a> Ubakhalimele abakhukhumali, Abaqalekiswa abo,  balahlekeneyo nemithetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:22">119:22</a> Shenxisa imke kum ingcikivo nendelo, Ngokuba ndizibambile izingqiniso zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:23">119:23</a> Nangona abathetheli behlala bathethe ngam, Umkhonzi wakho yena ucamngca ngemimiselo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:24">119:24</a> Izingqiniso zakho ziziyoliso zam noko, Zingamaphakathi am.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:25">119:25</a> Umphefumlo wam unamathele eluthulini: Ndiphilise ngokwelizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:26">119:26</a> Ndizicacisile iindlela zam, wandiphendula; Ndifundise imimisela yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:27">119:27</a> Ndiqondise iindlela zeziyalezo zakho, Ndicamngce ngemisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:28">119:28</a> Umphefumlo wam uvuza iinyembezi sisingqala, Ndimise ngokwelizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:29">119:29</a> Indlela yobuxoki yisuse kum; Ndibabale umyalelo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:30">119:30</a> Ndiyinyule indlela yokuthembeka; Amasiko akho ndijolise kuwo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:31">119:31</a> Ndinamathele ezingqinisweni zakho; Musa ukundidanisa,  Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:32">119:32</a> Ndigidima ngendlela yemithetho yakho, Ngokuba uyenze banzi intliziyo yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:33">119:33</a> Ndiyalele, Yehova, indlela yemimiselo yakho, Ndiyibambe kuphele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:34">119:34</a> Ndiqondise, ndibambe umyalelo wakho, Ndiwugcine ngentliziyo yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:35">119:35</a> Ndinyathelise endleleni yemithetho yakho, Ngokuba ndiyithandile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:36">119:36</a> Intliziyo yam yithobele ezingqinisweni zakho,  Ungayithobeli ekubaweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:37">119:37</a> Dlulisa amehlo am angakhangeli inkohlakalo, Ndiphilise ngeendlela zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:38">119:38</a> Zalisa kumkhonzi wakho intetho yakho, Eyokuba bakoyike.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:39">119:39</a> Yidlulise ingcikivo yam endinxunguphala yiyo, Ngokuba amasiko akho alungile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:40">119:40</a> Nanku ndilangazelela iziyalezo zakho, Ndiphilise ngobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:41">119:41</a> Mazize kum iinceba zakho, Yehova, Nosindiso lwakho ngokwentetho yakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:42">119:42</a> Ndimphendule ngelizwi ondingcikivayo, Ngokuba ndikholose ngelizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:43">119:43</a> Musa ukuda ulihluthe emlonyeni wam ilizwi lenyaniso,  Ngokuba ndilindele izigwebo zakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:44">119:44</a> Ndowugcina umyalelo wakho ngamaxesha onke, Ngonaphakade kanaphakade;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:45">119:45</a> Ndihamba-hambe endaweni ebanzi, Ngokuba ndifuna iziyalezo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:46">119:46</a> Ndothetha ngezingqiniso zakho phambi kokumkani, Ndingabi nakudana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:47">119:47</a> Ndoziyolisa ngemithetho yakho Endiyithandayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:48">119:48</a> Ndiziphakamise izandla zam emithethweni yakho endiyithandayo, Ndicamngce ngemimiselo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:49">119:49</a> Khumbula ilizwi lakho kumkhonzi wakho, Ngenxa enokuba undithembise lona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:50">119:50</a> Yiyo le intuthuzelo yam ekucinezelekeni kwam, Yokuba intetho yakho indiphilisile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:51">119:51</a> Abakhukhumali bada bandigxeka kakhulu; Kanti andithi gu bucala emyalelweni wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:52">119:52</a> Ndawakhumbula amasiko akho kususela kwanaphakade, Yehova,  Ndathuthuzeleka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:53">119:53</a> Ndingenwe ngumsindo oshushu, Ndisenziwa ngabangendawo abalahla umyalelo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:54">119:54</a> Iziingoma kum imimiselo yakho, Endlwini yokuphambukela kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:55">119:55</a> Ndilikhumbule ebusuku igama lakho, Yehova, Ndawugcina umyalelo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:56">119:56</a> Ndinikwe oku, Ukuba ndibambe iziyalezo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:57">119:57</a> Isabelo sam, Yehova, ndithi, Sesokuba ndigcine amazwi akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:58">119:58</a> Ndiya kubongoza ngentliziyo yonke, Ndibabale ngokwentetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:59">119:59</a> Ndazicingela iindlela zam, Ndazibuyisela iinyawo zam ezingqinisweni zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:60">119:60</a> Ndikhawulezile andazila-zila Ukugcina imithetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:61">119:61</a> Izintya zabangendawo zindithandele, Andiwulibele umyalelo wakhe noko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:62">119:62</a> Ndivuka phakathi kobusuku, ndibulele kuwe, Ngenxa yezigwebo zobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:63">119:63</a> Ndilidlelane labo bonke abakoyikayo, Nelabazigcinayo iziyalezo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:64">119:64</a> Inceba yakho, Yehova, izalise ihlabathi; Ndifundise imimiselo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:65">119:65</a> Umenzele okulungileyo umkhonzi wakho, Yehova, ngokwelizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:66">119:66</a> Ndifundise, ndibe nemvo nokwazi okulungileyo, Ngokuba ndikholwa yimithetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:67">119:67</a> Ndingekacinezelwa, ndaye ndilahleka; Kungoku ndiyigcinile intetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:68">119:68</a> Ulungile wena, ulungisa; Ndifundise imimiselo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:69">119:69</a> Abakhukhumali bathungele ubuxoki ngam; Mna ndizibamba ngentliziyo yonke iziyalezo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:70">119:70</a> Ithe fithi kukutyeba intliziyo yabo; Ke mna ndiziyolisa ngomyalelo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:71">119:71</a> Kundilungele okokuba ndacinezelwayo, Ukuze ndiyifunde imimiselo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:72">119:72</a> Ulungile kum umyalelo womlomo wakho, Ngaphezu kwamawaka egolide nesilivere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:73">119:73</a> Izandla zakho zindenzile, zandilungisa; Ndiqondise,  ndifunde imithetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:74">119:74</a> Abakoyikayo bondibona, bavuye, Ngokuba ndilindele elizwini lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:75">119:75</a> Ndiyazi, Yehova, ukuba zinobulungisa izigwebo zakho;  Undicinezele, phofu uthembekile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:76">119:76</a> Ngamana inceba yakho yaba yeyokundithuthuzela,  Njengokwentetho yakho kumkhonzi wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:77">119:77</a> Mazize kum iimfesane zakho, ndiphile, Ngokuba umyalelo wakho undiyolisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:78">119:78</a> Mabadane abakhukhumali, ngokuba bendigobele phantsi ngobuxoki, Mna ndicamngca ngeziyalezo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:79">119:79</a> Mabandibuyele abakoyikayo, Nabazaziyo izingqiniso zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:80">119:80</a> Mayigqibelele intliziyo yam emimiselweni yakho, Ukuze ndingadani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:81">119:81</a> Umphefumlo wam uyaphela kukululangazelela usindiso lwakho, Ndilindele elizwini lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:82">119:82</a> Amehlo am ayaphela kukulangazelela intetho yakho,  Ndisithi, Uya kundithuthuzela nini na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:83">119:83</a> Noko ndithe ndaba njengentsuba emsini; Andiyilibali imimiselo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:84">119:84</a> Zingaphi na iintsuku zomkhonzi wakho? Uya kuda ubagwebe nini na abandisukelayo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:85">119:85</a> Abakhukhumali bandimbele izihogo, Abangenamyalelo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:86">119:86</a> Yonke imithetho yakho ithembekile: Bandisukela ngobuxoki;  ndincede.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:87">119:87</a> Baphantse ukundigqibela emhlabeni, Ke mna andizilahli iziyalezo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:88">119:88</a> Ndiphilise ngokwenceba yakho, Ndizigcine izingqiniso zomlomo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:89">119:89</a> Lingunaphakade, Yehova, Limi emazulwini ilizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:90">119:90</a> Ukuthembeka kwakho kukwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana;  Ulizinzisile ihlabathi, lema.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:91">119:91</a> Ezo zinto zimele izigwebo zakho nanamhla, Ngokuba iinto zonke zingabakhonzi bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:92">119:92</a> Koko umyalelo wakho wandiyolisayo, Ndinge ndaphelayo ekucinezelekeni kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:93">119:93</a> Andiyi kuzilibala naphakade iziyalezo zakho, Ngokuba undiphilisile ngazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:94">119:94</a> Ndingowakho mna, ndisindise, Kuba ndicamanga ngeziyalezo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:95">119:95</a> Abangendawo bandilindile ukuze banditshabalalise; Mna ndigqale izingqiniso zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:96">119:96</a> Yonke inzaliseko ndiyibonile apho iphela khona; Ke wona umthetho wakho ngumphangalala omkhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:97">119:97</a> Hayi, ukuwuthanda kwam umyalelo wakho! Imini le yonke ndiyacamngca ngawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:98">119:98</a> Indifundisa ubulumko ngaphezu kweentshaba zam imithetho yakho, Ngokuba yeyam ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:99">119:99</a> Ndinokuqiqa ngaphezu kwabafundisi bam bonke, Ngokuba ngezingqiniso zakho ndiyacamngca.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:100">119:100</a> Ndinokuqonda ngaphezu kwamadoda amakhulu, Ngokuba ndizibamba iziyalezo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:101">119:101</a> Ndizinqandile iinyawo zam kwiindlela zonke ezimbi, Ukuze ndiligcine ilizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:102">119:102</a> Andisuki emasikweni akho, Ngokuba undiyalile wena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:103">119:103</a> Hayi, ukuba mnandi kwentetho yakho ekhuhlangubeni lam!  Igqithe nobusi emlonyeni wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:104">119:104</a> Ngeziyalezo zakho ndinokuqonda, Ngenxa yoko ndiwuthiyile wonke umendo wobuxoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:105">119:105</a> Lisisibane seenyawo zam ilizwi lakho, Likukukhanya emendweni wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:106">119:106</a> Ndikufungele, ndikumisile, Ukuzigcina izigwebo zobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:107">119:107</a> Ndide ndacinezeleka kakhulu; Yehova, ndiphilise ngokwelizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:108">119:108</a> Ngamana wakholeka kuwe, Yehova, umbingelelo wesisa womlomo wam; Ndifundise amasiko akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:109">119:109</a> Umphefumlo wam uhlala usesandleni sam, Ndingawulibali umyalelo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:110">119:110</a> Abangendawo bandenzele umgibe, Andiphambukanga eziyalezweni zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:111">119:111</a> Ndizidle ilifa izingqiniso zakho ngonaphakade, Ngokuba ziyimihlali yentliziyo yam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:112">119:112</a> Intliziyo yam ndiyithobele ekwenzeni imimiselo yakho Ngonaphakade, kuphele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:113">119:113</a> Abambaxa ndiyabathiya, Wona umyalelo wakho ndiyawuthanda.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:114">119:114</a> Isithe lam nengweletshetshe yam nguwe, Ndilindele elizwini lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:115">119:115</a> Sukani kum, nina benzi beento ezimbi, Ndibambe imithetho yoThixo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:116">119:116</a> Ndizimase ngokwelizwi lakho, ndiphile, Ungandidanisi ekulindeni kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:117">119:117</a> Ndixhase ndisinde, Ndihlale ndibheke emimiselweni yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:118">119:118</a> Ubacukucezile bonke abalahlekana nemimiselo yakho,  Ngokuba inkohliso yabo ibubuxoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:119">119:119</a> Wena ususa bonke abangendawo behlabathi njengentlenga,  Ngoko ndiyazithanda izingqiniso zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:120">119:120</a> Inyama yam isuka ihambe kukunkwantyiswa nguwe, Ndizoyike izigwebo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:121">119:121</a> Ndenza ngesiko nangobulungisa, Ungandinikeli kwabandicudisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:122">119:122</a> Mmele umkhonzi wakho, kulunge; Mabangandicudisi abakhukhumali.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:123">119:123</a> Amehlo am ayaphela kukululangazelela usindiso lwakho,  Nentetho yobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:124">119:124</a> Umkhonzi wakho menzele ngokwenceba yakho Undifundise imimiselo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:125">119:125</a> Ndingumkhonzi wakho, ndiqondise, Ndizazi izingqiniso zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:126">119:126</a> Lilixa lokuba uYehova enze, Kuba bawaphule umyalelo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:127">119:127</a> Ngenxa yoko ndiyithanda imithetho yakho Ngaphezu kwegolide, nakwengcwengiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:128">119:128</a> Ngenxa yoko ndithi, Zonke iziyalezo zakho zithe tye ngezinto zonke; Wonke umendo wobuxoki ndiwuthiyile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:129">119:129</a> Ziyimisebenzi ebalulekileyo izingqiniso zakho, Ngenxa yoko uzibambile umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:130">119:130</a> Ukutyhila kwamazwi akho kuyakhanyisa, Kuqondisa abazizidenge.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:131">119:131</a> Ndakhamisa umlomo wam, ndakhefuza, Ngokuba ndiyilangazelela imithetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:132">119:132</a> Ndibheke, undibabale, Ngokwesiko lakho kubathandi begama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:133">119:133</a> Qinisa ukunyathela kwam ngentetho yakho, Mabungabi nagunya kum ubutshinga, nabuphi na.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:134">119:134</a> Ndikhulule ekucudiseni komntu, Ndizigcine iziyalezo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:135">119:135</a> Khanyisa ubuso bakho kumkhonzi wakho, Undifundise imimiselo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:136">119:136</a> Ahla imijelo yamanzi amehlo am, Ngenxa yokuba bengawugcini umyalelo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:137">119:137</a> Ulilungisa wena, Yehova, Zithe tye izigwebo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:138">119:138</a> Uzimisile izingqiniso zakho, zanobulungisa, Zaba nokuthembeka kakhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:139">119:139</a> Ikhwele lam lindibhangisile, Ngokuba abandibandezelayo bewalibele amazwi akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:140">119:140</a> Ilizwi lakho linyibilikisiwe njengegolide kunene,  Umkhonzi wakho uyalithanda.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:141">119:141</a> Ndimncinane, ndideliwe, Noko andizilibali iziyalezo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:142">119:142</a> Ubulungisa bakho bubulungisa obungunaphakade, Umyalelo wakho uyinyaniso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:143">119:143</a> Imbandezelo nengcutheko indifumene, Imithetho yakho iyandiyolisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:144">119:144</a> Zinobulungisa ngonaphakade izingqiniso zakho,  Ndiqondise, ndiphile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:145">119:145</a> Ndikhala ngentliziyo yonke, ndiphendule; Yehova,  imimiselo yakho ndiya kuyibamba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:146">119:146</a> Ndikhala kuwe, ndisindise, Ndigcine izingqiniso zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:147">119:147</a> Ndakuphangela ukusa, ndazibika, Ndalindela emazwini akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:148">119:148</a> Amehlo am aphengela imilindo yasebusuku, Ukuze ndicamngce ngentetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:149">119:149</a> Live ilizwi lam ngokwenceba yakho, Yehova, ndiphilise ngokwamasiko akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:150">119:150</a> Bayasondela abaphuthuma amanyala, Banyawuka emyalelweni wakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:151">119:151</a> Usondele wena, Yehova, Yonke imithetho yakho iyinyaniso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:152">119:152</a> Kudala ndisazi ngokwezingqiniso zakho, Ukuba uzisekile ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:153">119:153</a> Khangela ukucinezeleka kwam, undihlangule, Ngokuba ndingawulibali umyalelo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:154">119:154</a> Bambana nobambene nam, undikhulule, Ndiphilise ngokwelizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:155">119:155</a> Lunyawukile kwabangendawo usindiso, Ngokuba abayifuni imimiselo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:156">119:156</a> Iimfesane zakho zininzi, Yehova; Ndiphilise ngokwamasiko akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:157">119:157</a> Baninzi abandisukelayo nabandibandezelayo; Andithi gu bucala ezingqinisweni zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:158">119:158</a> Ndababona abatshinizi, ndakruquka, Abo bangayigciniyo intetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:159">119:159</a> Bona ukuthanda kwam iziyalezo zakho, Yehova, ndiphilise ngokwenceba yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:160">119:160</a> Isimbuku selizwi lakho siyinyaniso iphela,  Zingunaphakade zonke izigwebo zobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:161">119:161</a> Abathetheli bandisukela ngelize, Intliziyo yam iyankwantyiswa ngamazwi akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:162">119:162</a> Ndinemihlali ngentetho yakho, Njengofumene ixhoba elininzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:163">119:163</a> Ndikuthiyile ukuxoka, lisikizi kum; Ndiyawuthanda umyalelo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:164">119:164</a> Ndikudumisa kasixhenxe ngemini, Ngenxa yezigwebo zobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:165">119:165</a> Banoxolo olukhulu abawuthandayo umyalelo wakho; Akukho sikhubekiso kubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:166">119:166</a> Ndikhangela usindiso lwakho, Yehova; Ndenza imithetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:167">119:167</a> Umphefumlo wam uyazigcina izingqiniso zakho, Ndizithanda kunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:168">119:168</a> Ndiyazigcina iziyalezo zakho nezingqiniso zakho, Ngokuba zonke iindlela zam ziphambi kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:169">119:169</a> Makusondele phambi kwakho ukuhlahlamba kwam; Yehova,  ndiqondise ngokwelizwi lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:170">119:170</a> Masifike isikhungo sam phambi kwakho; Ndihlangule ngokwentetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:171">119:171</a> Umlomo wam mawumpompoze indumiso, Kuba undifundisile imimiselo yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:172">119:172</a> Ulwimi lwam luya kuyiphendula intetho yakho, Ngokuba yonke imithetho yakho inobulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:173">119:173</a> Isandla sakho masibe sesokundinceda, Ngokuba ndizinyulele iziyalezo zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:174">119:174</a> Ndilangazelela usindiso lwakho, Yehova; Umyalelo wakho uyandiyolisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:175">119:175</a> Mawuphile umphefumlo wam, ukudumise, Andincede amasiko akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:176">119:176</a> Ndiya ndimka njengemvu elahlekileyo; mfune umkhonzi wakho, Ngokuba andiyilibali imithetho yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:1">120:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. Engxingongweni yam ndakhala kuYehova,  Wandiphendula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:2">120:2</a> Ndathi, Wuhlangule, Yehova, umphefumlo wam emlonyeni oxokayo, Elulwimini olunenkohliso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:3">120:3</a> Makakunike ntoni na, akongeze ntoni na, Lulwimindini lunenkohliso?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:4">120:4</a> Iintolo zegorha ezitsolo, Kunye namalahle avuthayo onwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:5">120:5</a> Athi ke mna! Kuba ndingumphambukeli kwaMesheki, Ndihleli ngasezintenteni zakwaKedare.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:6">120:6</a> Umphefumlo wam kade uhleli Nabaluthiyileyo uxolo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:7">120:7</a> Mna ndingowoxolo; Ke ndithi ndakuthetha, bona babe yimfazwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:1">121:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. Ndiwaphakamisele ezintabeni na amehlo am? Luya kuvela phi na uncedo lwam?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:2">121:2</a> Uncedo lwam luvela kuYehova, UMenzi wezulu nehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:3">121:3</a> Akayi kukha alunikele unyawo lwakho ekutyibilikeni; Akayi kukha ozele umgcini wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:4">121:4</a> Uyabona, akozeli, akalali, UMgcini kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:5">121:5</a> NguYehova umgcini wakho, NguYehova umthunzi wakho ekunene kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:6">121:6</a> Emini ilanga aliyi kukwenzakalisa, Nenyanga ebusuku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:7">121:7</a> UYehova uya kukugcina ebubini bonke, Uya kuwugcina umphefumlo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:8">121:8</a> UYehova uya kukugcina ukuphuma kwakho nokungena kwakho,  Kususela ngoku kude kuse ephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:1">122:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. KaDavide. Ndavuya bakuthi kum, Masiye endlwini kaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:2">122:2</a> Iinyawo zethu zifike zema Emasangweni akho, Yerusalem;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:3">122:3</a> Yerusalem, wena wakhiweyo Ngokomzi ohlangeneyo wamnye;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:4">122:4</a> Apho zinyuka ziye khona izizwe, Izizwe zikaYehova;  Ibubungqina ke loo nto kwaSirayeli, Ukuba kubulelwe kwigama likaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:5">122:5</a> Kuba khona apho kumiswe iitrone zokugweba, Iitrone zendlu kaDavide.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:6">122:6</a> Celelani iYerusalem uxolo; Mababe nokuchulumacha abakuthandayo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:7">122:7</a> Malube luxolo eludongeni lwakho olurhaqileyo,  Nokuchulumacha ezingxandeni zakho ezinde.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:8">122:8</a> Ngenxa yabazalwana bam nowethu, Makhe ndithethe uxolo ngawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:9">122:9</a> Ngenxa yendlu kaYehova, uThixo wethu, Ndiya kufuna okukulungeleyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:1">123:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. Ulohlala emazulwini, Ndiwaphakamisela kuwe amehlo am.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:2">123:2</a> Uyabona, njengokuba amehlo abakhonzi Emi kwisandla seenkosi zabo; Njengokuba amehlo omkhonzazana Emi kwisandla senkosikazi yakhe: Ngokunjalo amehlo ethu akuYehova, uThixo wethu, Ade asibabale.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:3">123:3</a> Sibabale, Yehova, sibabale, Ngokuba sanele kakhulu kukudelwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:4">123:4</a> Umphefumlo wethu wanele kakhulu Kukugculela kwabangakhathalele bani, Nokudela kwabanekratshi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:1">124:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. KaDavide. Koko uYehova ebengakuthi,  Makatsho uSirayeli,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:2">124:2</a> Koko uYehova ebengakuthi Ekusukeleni kwabantu phezulu kuthi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:3">124:3</a> Bange beba basiginya sihleli, Ekuvutheni komsindo wabo kuthi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:4">124:4</a> Ange esintywilisele amanzi, Wadlula phezu komphefumlo wethu umsinga;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:5">124:5</a> Ange edlule phezu komphefumlo wethu Amanzi akhukumeleyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:6">124:6</a> Ungowokubongwa uYehova, Ongasinikelanga emazinyweni abo,  ukuba siqwengwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:7">124:7</a> Umphefumlo wethu usindile, njengentaka emgibeni wababambisi; Umgibe uqhawukile, sasinda ke thina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:8">124:8</a> Uncedo lwethu lusegameni likaYehova, UMenzi wezulu nehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:1">125:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. Abo bakholosa ngoYehova banjengentaba yaseZiyon: Ayishukumi, ihleli ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:2">125:2</a> IYerusalem ijikelezwe ziintaba; Ke uYehova ubajikelezile naye abantu bakhe, Kususela ngoku kude kuse ephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:3">125:3</a> Ngokuba ayiyi kuhlala intonga yokungendawo elifeni lamalungisa, Ukuze amalungisa angazisi ebugqwetheni izandla zawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:4">125:4</a> Yehova, yenza okulungileyo kwabalungileyo, Kwabathe tye ezintliziyweni zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:5">125:5</a> Ke bona abathi gu bucala ngeendlela zabo ezimagoso-goso,  UYehova makabemkise, kunye nabasebenzi bobutshinga. Malube luxolo kuSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:1">126:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. Ekubabuyiseni kukaYehova ababuyayo baseZiyon, Saba njengabaphuphayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:2">126:2</a> Waza wazala kukuhleka umlomo wethu, Lwazala kukumemelela ulwimi lwethu. Baza bathi phakathi kweentlanga, UYehova ubenzele izinto ezinkulu aba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:3">126:3</a> UYehova usenzele izinto ezinkulu, Saba ngabavuyayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:4">126:4</a> Buyisa, Yehova, abathinjiweyo bakuthi, Njengemilambo yamanzi yelasezantsi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:5">126:5</a> Abahlwayelayo beneenyembezi Baya kuvuna benokumemelela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:6">126:6</a> Ohamba ahambe elila, Ephethe intlwayelelo, Uyabuya eze ememelela, Ethwele izithungu zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:1">127:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. KaSolomon. Ukuba akayakhi uYehova indlu, Bafumana besaphuka yiyo abakhi bayo. Ukuba umzi akawugcini uYehova, Ufumana ephaphama owugcinayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:2">127:2</a> Nifumana nivuka kusasa, Nihlale nisebenza kude kube sebusuku, Nikudla ukudla kokubulaleka; Uyipha intanda yakhe,  ilele ubuthongo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:3">127:3</a> Uyabona, ilifa likaYehova ngoonyana, Umvuzo sisiqhamo sesizalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:4">127:4</a> Njengeentolo esandleni segorha, Banjalo oonyana bobutsha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:5">127:5</a> Hayi, uyolo lomfo ozalise umphongolo wakhe ngabo! Abayi kudana, Xa bathetha neentshaba esangweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:1">128:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. Hayi, uyolo lwabantu bonke abamoyikayo uYehova, Abahamba ngeendlela zakhe!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:2">128:2</a> Ukuxelenga kwezandla zakho inene uya kukudla, Uya kuba noyolo wena, kulunge kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:3">128:3</a> Umkakho woba njengomdiliya oqhamayo Endlwini yakho ngaphakathi; Oonyana bakho babe njengezithole zomnquma Ngeenxa zonke esithebeni sakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:4">128:4</a> Yabona, unjalo ukusikelelwa umfo Omoyikayo uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:5">128:5</a> Makakusikelele uYehova eZiyon. Uyibone iYerusalem inenyhweba Yonke imihla yobomi bakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:6">128:6</a> Ubone abantwana babantwana bakho. Malube luxolo kuSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:1">129:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. Kukaninzi bendibandezela kwasebuncinaneni bam, Makatsho uSirayeli;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:2">129:2</a> Kukaninzi bendibandezela kwasebuncinaneni bam: Ababanga nakundithini noko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:3">129:3</a> Abalimi balima emhlana kum, Bayolula indima yabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:4">129:4</a> UYehova ulilungisa, Uzinqumle izintya zabangendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:5">129:5</a> Mabadane babuye umva Bonke abayithiyayo iZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:6">129:6</a> Mababe njengengca ephuma phezu kwezindlu, Eyomayo ingekahlumi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:7">129:7</a> Engekasizalisi nesandla sakhe umvuni, Engekalizalisi nesondo lengubo yakhe umbophi wezithungu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:8">129:8</a> Bengekathi nabadlulayo, Intsikelelo kaYehova mayibe kuni;  Siyanisikelela egameni likaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:1">130:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. Ezinzulwini ndinqula wena, Yehova,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:2">130:2</a> Nkosi, yiva ilizwi lam. Iindlebe zakho mazilibazele Ilizwi lokutarhuzisa kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:3">130:3</a> Ukuba uthe wabunqala ubugwenxa, Yehova, Ngubani na ongaba nokuma, Nkosi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:4">130:4</a> Ngokuba kunawe ukuxolela, Ukuze woyikwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:5">130:5</a> Ndithembele kuYehova, uthembile umphefumlo wam; Ndilinde ilizwi lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:6">130:6</a> Umphefumlo wam ulindele eNkosini Ngaphezu kwabalinde ukusa, Ewe, abalinde ukusa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:7">130:7</a> Lindela kuYehova, Sirayeli, Ngokuba inceba ikuYehova;  Ikuye inkululeko eninzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:8">130:8</a> Yena ke wowakhulula amaSirayeli Ebugwenxeni bawo bonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:1">131:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko; kaDavide. Yehova, intliziyo yam ayiphakamile, amehlo am akaqwayingile; Andihambi ezintweni ezinkulu, Eziyimisebenzi ebalulekileyo kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:2">131:2</a> Inene, ndiwuzolise ndawuthozamisa umphefumlo wam;  Unjengomntwana olunyulweyo, ehleli kunina; Unjengomntwana olunyulweyo umphefumlo wam kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:3">131:3</a> Wena Sirayeli, lindela kuYehova Kususela ngoku kude kuse ephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:1">132:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. Yehova, mkhumbulele uDavide Ukucinezeleka kwakhe konke;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:2">132:2</a> Yena wamfungelayo uYehova, Wabhambathisa kwimbalasane enguThixo kaYakobi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:3">132:3</a> Esithi, Andiyi kungena ententeni eyindlu yam, Andiyi kunyuka ndiye esililini, emandlalweni wam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:4">132:4</a> Andiyi kuwanika amehlo am ubuthongo, Neenkophe zam ukozela:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:5">132:5</a> Ndide ndimfumanele indawo uYehova, Ndiyifumanele umnquba imbalasane kaYakobi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:6">132:6</a> Khangela, sawuva e-Efrata, Sawufumana ezintilini zaseKiriyati-yeharim.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:7">132:7</a> Masingene emnqubeni wakhe, Siqubude esihlalweni seenyawo zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:8">132:8</a> Khawusuk ume, Yehova, uze ekuphumleni kwakho, Wena netyeya yamandla akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:9">132:9</a> Ababingeleli bakho mabambathe ubulungisa, Bamemelele abakho benceba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:10">132:10</a> Ngenxa kaDavide umkhonzi wakho, Musa ukubutyhala ubuso bomthanjiswa wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:11">132:11</a> UYehova wamfungela uDavide; Inyaniso, akayi kubuya kuloo nto, Esithi, Esiqhameni sezibilini zakho Ndimisa oya kuba setroneni yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:12">132:12</a> Ukuba bathe oonyana bakho bawugcina umnqophiso wam,  Nesingqiniso sam endibafundisayo: Oonyana babo bothi nabo bahlale Etroneni yakho nanini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:13">132:13</a> Ngokuba uYehova uyinyule iZiyon, Uyinqwenele ukuba ibe likhaya lakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:14">132:14</a> Esithi, Nantsi indawo yam yokuphumla kwam nanini; Ndiya kuhlala apha, ngokuba oko ndikunqwenele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:15">132:15</a> Umphako wayo ndiya kuwusikelela kunene; Amahlwempu ayo ndiya kuwahluthisa ngesonka,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:16">132:16</a> Ndibambathise ngosindiso ababingeleli bayo, Abenceba bayo bamemelele bememelela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:17">132:17</a> Apho ndiya kumhlumisela uphondo uDavide, Ndiya kumlungisela isibane umthanjiswa wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:18">132:18</a> Iintshaba zakhe ndiya kuzambathisa udano; Ke phezu kwakhe yena siya kutyatyamba isithsaba sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:1">133:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko; kaDavide. Yabonani, ukuba kuhle, ukuba mnandi, Ukuthi abazalwana bahlale bemxhelo mnye!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:2">133:2</a> Kunjengeoli elungileyo entloko, Isihla ezindevini,  Ezindevini zika-Aron, Isihla iye emqukumbelweni weengubo zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:3">133:3</a> Kunjengombethe waseHermon, Ohla phezu kweentaba zaseZiyon;  Ngokuba uYehova wayimisela khona apho intsikelelo, Ubomi, kude kuse ephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:1">134:1</a> Ingoma yezinyuko. Yabonani, mbongeni uYehova, nonke bakhonzi bakaYehova, Nimiyo endlwini kaYehova ebusuku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:2">134:2</a> Phakamiselani engcweleni izandla zenu, Nimbonge uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:3">134:3</a> Makakusikelele eZiyon uYehova, UMenzi wezulu nehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:1">135:1</a> Haleluya. Dumisani igama likaYehova; Dumisani, nina bakhonzi bakaYehova,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:2">135:2</a> Nimiyo endlwini kaYehova, Ezintendelezweni zendlu yoThixo wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:3">135:3</a> Dumisani uYehova, ngokuba elungile uYehova; Libetheleni uhadi igama lakhe, ngokuba kumnandi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:4">135:4</a> Ngokuba uYehova unyule uYakobi ukuba abe ngowakhe, Wanyula uSirayeli ukuba abe yinqobo kuye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:5">135:5</a> Ngokuba ndiyazi mna ukuba mkhulu uYehova, INkosi yethu ingaphezu koothixo bonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:6">135:6</a> Konke akuthandileyo uYehova uya kwenza, Ezulwini nasemhlabeni, Ezilwandle nasemanzini onke enzonzobila.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:7">135:7</a> Ulonyusa amafu eziphelweni zehlabathi, Imvula wayenzela imibane; Ulorhola umoya koovimba bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:8">135:8</a> Owawabulalayo amazibulo aseYiputa, Ethabathele ebantwini wesa ezinkomeni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:9">135:9</a> Wathumela imiqondiso nezimanga Phakathi kwakho, Yiputa,  KuFaro nakubakhonzi bakhe bonke;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:10">135:10</a> Owabulala iintlanga ezinkulu, Wabulala ookumkani abanamandla;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:11">135:11</a> OoSihon, ukumkani wama-Amori, No-Ogi, ukumkani waseBhashan, Nezikumkani zonke zakwaKanan;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:12">135:12</a> Walinikela ilizwe labo lalilifa, Lalilifa kumaSirayeli,  abantu bakhe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:13">135:13</a> Yehova, igama lakho lingunaphakade, Inkumbuzo yakho,  Yehova, ikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:14">135:14</a> Ngokuba uYehova uya kugweba phakathi kwabantu bakhe,  Azohlwaye ngenxa yabakhonzi bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:15">135:15</a> Izithixo zeentlanga yisilivere negolide, Umsebenzi wezandla zabantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:16">135:16</a> Zinomlomo nje, azithethi; Zinamehlo nje, aziboni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:17">135:17</a> Zineendlebe nje, aziva; Akukho nento engumoya emlonyeni wazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:18">135:18</a> Baya kuba njengazo abenzi bazo, Bonke abasukuba bekholose ngazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:19">135:19</a> Nina ndlu kaSirayeli, bongani uYehova; Nani ndlu ka-Aron,  bongani uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:20">135:20</a> Nina ndlu kaLevi, bongani uYehova; Nani boyika uYehova,  bongani uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:21">135:21</a> Ngowokubongwa uYehova eZiyon, Ulohlala eYerusalem.  Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:1">136:1</a> Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:2">136:2</a> Bulelani kuThixo woothixo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:3">136:3</a> Bulelani kuNkosi kankosi: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:4">136:4</a> KuloMenzi wemisebenzi ebalulekileyo emikhulu yedwa:  Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:5">136:5</a> KuloMenzi wezulu ngengqondo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:6">136:6</a> KuloMtwabululi wehlabathi phezu kwamanzi: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:7">136:7</a> KuloMenzi wezikhanyiso ezikhulu: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:8">136:8</a> Ilanga lilawule emini: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:9">136:9</a> Inyanga neenkwenkwezi zilawule ebusuku: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:10">136:10</a> Kulowabulala amaYiputa kumazibulo awo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:11">136:11</a> Wawakhupha amaSirayeli phakathi kwawo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:12">136:12</a> Ngesandla esithe nkqi, nangengalo eyolukileyo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:13">136:13</a> KuloMgabuli woLwandle oluBomvu, lwagabuka: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:14">136:14</a> Wawaweza amaSirayeli esazulwini salo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:15">136:15</a> Wamvuthululela uFaro nempi yakhe eLwandle oluBomvu:  Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:16">136:16</a> Kulohambisa abantu bakhe entlango: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:17">136:17</a> Kulowaxabela ookumkani abakhulu: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:18">136:18</a> Wabulala ookumkani abaziingangamsha: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:19">136:19</a> USihon, ukumkani wama-Amori: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:20">136:20</a> No-Ogi, ukumkani waseBhashan: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:21">136:21</a> Walinikela ilizwe labo laba lilifa: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:22">136:22</a> Laba lilifa kuSirayeli umkhonzi wakhe: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:23">136:23</a> Owasikhumbulayo ebuphantsini bethu: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:24">136:24</a> Wasihlangula kwabasibandezelayo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:25">136:25</a> Ulonika into yonke ephilileyo ukudla: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:26">136:26</a> Bulelani kuThixo wamazulu: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:1">137:1</a> NgaseMilanjeni yaseBhabheli Sahlala phantsi khona, salila,  Sakuyikhumbula iZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:2">137:2</a> Emingculubeni phakathi kwayo Sazixhoma khona iihadi zethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:3">137:3</a> Ngokuba khona apho abathimbi bethu basibiza Izango zengoma; Abathuthumbisi bethu basibiza uvuyo, Besithi,  Sivumeleni ingoma yaseZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:4">137:4</a> Singathini na ukuvuma ingoma kaYehova Emhlabeni wolunye uhlanga?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:5">137:5</a> Ukuba ndithe ndakulibala, Yerusalem, Masinyele isandla sam sokunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:6">137:6</a> Ulwimi lwam malunamathele ekhuhlangubeni lam, Ukuba andithanga ndikukhumbule; Ukuba andithanga ndiyinyuse iYerusalem Ngaphezu kwemivuyo yam yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:7">137:7</a> Bakhumbule, Yehova, oonyana bakaEdom, Umhla weYerusalem,  Abo bathi, Yidilizeni, yidilizeni Kuse elusekweni lwayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:8">137:8</a> Ntombi inguBhabheli, wena unyashiweyo; Hayi, uyolo lwalowo ukubuyekezayo ukuphatha kwakho Osiphethe ngako!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:9">137:9</a> Hayi, uyolo lwalowo ubabambayo abahlekeze abantwana bakho Engxondorheni!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:1">138:1</a> EkaDavide. Ndiya kubulela kuwe ngentliziyo yam yonke;  Phambi koothixo ndiya kukubethela uhadi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:2">138:2</a> Ndiya kuqubuda ndibhekise etempileni yakho engcwele,  Ndibulele kwigama lakho, ngenxa yenceba yakho, nangenxa yenyaniso yakho; Kuba ulikhulisile ilizwi lakho ngaphezu kwegama lakho lonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:3">138:3</a> Ngomhla wokubiza kwam wandiphendula, Wandikhaliphisa,  yangamandla emphefumlweni wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:4">138:4</a> Baya kubulela kuwe, Yehova, bonke ookumkani behlabathi,  Bakuweva amazwi omlomo wakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:5">138:5</a> Bavume ngeendlela zikaYehova, Ukuba lukhulu uzuko lukaYehova:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:6">138:6</a> Ngokuba noko uYehova aphakamileyo, uyambona othobekileyo;  Ke yena oziphakamisayo umazi nakude.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:7">138:7</a> Ukuba ndithe ndahamba-hamba phakathi kweembandezelo,  uyandiphilisa; Wosolulela emsindweni weentshaba zam isandla sakho, Sindisindise isandla sakho sokunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:8">138:8</a> UYehova uya kundifezela. Yehova, inceba yakho ingunaphakade, Izenzo zezandla zakho musa ukuziyekela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:1">139:1</a> Kumongameli; ekaDavide. Umhobe. Yehova, undigocagocile,  wandazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:2">139:2</a> Wena uyakwazi ukuhlala kwam nokusuka kwam; Uyaziqonda izicamango zam nakude.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:3">139:3</a> Ukuhamba kwam nokulala kwam, uyakwela; Uqhelene neendlela zam zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:4">139:4</a> Ngokuba akukho lizwi elulwimini lwam Ongalaziyo ke,  Yehova, kanye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:5">139:5</a> Ngasemva nangaphambili undingqingile, Wasibeka phezu kwam isandla sakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:6">139:6</a> Kubalulekile kum oko kwazi, Kuphezulu, kundinqabele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:7">139:7</a> Ndingahambela phi na ukumka emoyeni wakho? Ndingabalekela phi na ukumka ebusweni bakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:8">139:8</a> Ukuba ndithe ndenyuka ndaya emazulwini, ulapho wena; Ukuba ndithe ndazandlalela kwelabafileyo, nanko ukho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:9">139:9</a> Ukuba ndithe ndaphakamisa amaphiko esifingo, Ndaya ndahlala ekupheleni kolwandle,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:10">139:10</a> Besingandikhaphayo kwanalapho isandla sakho, Sindibambe isandla sakho sokunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:11">139:11</a> Ukuba ndithe, Mabundisongele ubumnyama bona bodwa,  Nokukhanya kube bubusuku ngeenxa zonke kum:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:12">139:12</a> Kwanobumnyama obo abungebi bubumnyama kuwe; Ubusuku bungaba mhlophe njengemini, Ubumnyama bungaba njengokukhanya</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:13">139:13</a> Ngokuba wena wazibumba izintso zam, Wandibiyela esizalweni sikama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:14">139:14</a> Ndiyabulela kuwe ngenxa enokuba ndenziwe ngokoyikekayo,  ngokubalulekileyo; Zibalulekile izenzo zakho, Umphefumlo wam uyazi kakuhle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:15">139:15</a> Ayengagushekile kuwe amathambo am, Mna ndenzelwayo entsithelweni, Ndalukwa ndayimfakamfele ezinzulwini zomhlaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:16">139:16</a> Amehlo akho andibona ndiseyimbumba, Zazibhalwe encwadini yakho iimini zonke ziphela; Ziyiliwe ngenxa engaphambili,  Kungekabikho ke nanye kuzo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:17">139:17</a> Kum ke zinjani na ukunqaba izicamango zakho, Thixo!  Asingangani isimbuku sazo!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:18">139:18</a> Zingathi, ndizibalile, zibe ninzi ngaphezu kwentlabathi;  Ndakuvuka ndoba ndisenawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:19">139:19</a> Ngamana wambulala ongendawo, Thixo! Nina madoda amagazi,  sukani kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:20">139:20</a> Abo bakukhankanyela amayelenqe, Balibizela inkohlakalo igama lakho abazondi bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:21">139:21</a> Andinakubathiya na abakuthiyayo, Yehova, Ndikruquke ngabasukela phezulu kuwe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:22">139:22</a> Ndibathiya ngentiyo ephelelisileyo, Kum mna baziintshaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:23">139:23</a> Ndigocagoce, Thixo, uyazi intliziyo yam; Ndicikide, uzazi iingcinga-ngcinga zam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:24">139:24</a> Ubone ukuba kukho ndlela yobubi na kum, Undikhaphele kwindlela engunaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:1">140:1</a> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Ndihlangule, Yehova,  esintwini esinobubi, Ndilondoloze emntwini ogonyamelayo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:2">140:2</a> Abacinga okubi entliziyweni. Imihla yonke baxhaya imfazwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:3">140:3</a> Balola ulwimi lwabo njengenyoka; Ubuhlungu berhamba busemlonyeni wabo (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:4">140:4</a> Ndigcine, Yehova, ezandleni zongendawo, Ndilondoloze emntwini ogonyamelayo, Abacinga ukuzikhubekisa iinyawo zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:5">140:5</a> Abanekratshi bandiqhushekele isibatha nezintya, Baneke umnatha ecaleni kwendlela, Bandithiyele ngemigibe.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:6">140:6</a> Ndithi kuYehova, UnguThixo wam; Beka indlebe, Yehova,  elizwini lesikhungo sam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:7">140:7</a> Yehova, Nkosi yam, nqaba endisindisayo, Uyigqubuthele intloko yam ngemini yeduli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:8">140:8</a> Musa ukumnika, Yehova, ongendawo iminqweno yakhe; Musa ukuwuphumelelisa umnkqangiyelo wakhe, Hleze aziphakamise.  (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:9">140:9</a> Yona intloko yabandingqingayo, Ububi bomlomo wabo mabubagubungele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:10">140:10</a> Mabathotyelwe amalahle avuthayo; Makabawise emlilweni,  emimbithini, bangabi saphuma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:11">140:11</a> Indoda enolwimi mayingazinzi ehlabathini; Indoda enokugonyamela, ububi mabuyizingele ngembembetshane.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:12">140:12</a> Ndiyazi ukuba uYehova uya kulifeza Ityala losizana,  ibango lamahlwempu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:13">140:13</a> Inene, amalungisa aya kubulela kwigama lakho; Baya kuhlala ebusweni bakho abathe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:1">141:1</a> Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, ndiyakunqula, khawuleza uze kum; Libekele indlebe izwi lam ekudandulukeni kwam kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:2">141:2</a> Umthandazo wam mawuhlale uhleli phambi kwakho usisiqhumiso, Nokuphakamisa kwam izandla kube ngumnikelo wangokuhlwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:3">141:3</a> Umlomo wam wumisele umlindi, Yehova; Misa umgcini emnyango womlomo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:4">141:4</a> Intliziyo yam musa ukuyithobela entweni embi, Ukuba isebenze intlondi yokungendawo Namadoda asebenza ubutshinga;  Mandingazidli izimnandi zawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:5">141:5</a> Malindibethe ilungisa linenceba, lindohlwaye; Ioli enjalo yentloko ayingeyali intloko yam: Ngokuba usekho nomthandazo wam ebubini bawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:6">141:6</a> Bakhahlelwa emacaleni engxondorha abagwebi bawo, Beve amazwi am ukuba amnandi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:7">141:7</a> Njengolimayo enqika umhlaba, Anjalo ukuthi saa amathambo ethu emlonyeni wengcwaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:8">141:8</a> Ngokuba akuwe, Yehova, Nkosi yam, amehlo am; Ndizimela ngawe; musa ukuwuphalaza umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:9">141:9</a> Ndigcine esangweni lomgibe wabandithiyelayo,  Nasezirhintyelweni zabasebenza ubutshinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:10">141:10</a> Mabeyele ezintanjeni zabo abangendawo, Ndide ndidlule mna okukanye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:1">142:1</a> Eyokuqiqa kaDavide; oko ebesemqolombeni. Umthandazo.  Ndikhala kuYehova ngezwi lam, Ndikhunga uYehova ngezwi lam,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:2">142:2</a> Ndiphalaza inkalazo yam phambi kwakhe, Ndixela imbandezelo yam phambi kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:3">142:3</a> Ekutyhafeni komoya phakathi kwam, Uyayazi wena ingqushu yam. Emendweni endihamba ngawo Bandiqhushekela isibatha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:4">142:4</a> Bheka ngasekunene ubone, Akukho undibukayo; Andinandawo ndingasabela kuyo, Akukho uwukhathaleleyo umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:5">142:5</a> Ndikhala kuwe, Yehova, Ndithi, Nguwe ihlathi lam, Isabelo sam ezweni labahleliyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:6">142:6</a> Kubazele indlebe ukuhlahlamba kwam, Ngokuba ndiswele kakhulu: Ndihlangule kwabandisukelayo, Ngokuba bomelele kunam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:7">142:7</a> Wukhuphe entolongweni umphefumlo wam, Ndibulele kwigama lakho. Amalungisa aya kuzithi jize ngesithsaba ngenxa yam,  Ngokuba undiphethe kakuhle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:1">143:1</a> Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, yiva umthandazo wam, kubekele indlebe ukutarhuzisa kwam; Ndiphendule ngokunyaniseka kwakho,  ngobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:2">143:2</a> Musa ukumsa ematyaleni umkhonzi wakho: Ngokuba phambi kwakho akukho namnye uhleliyo olilungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:3">143:3</a> Ngokuba utshaba luwusukele umphefumlo wam, Lubutyumzele emhlabeni ubomi bam; Lundihlalise ezindaweni ezimnyama,  njengabafe ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:4">143:4</a> Utyhafile phakathi kwam umoya wam; Imangalisiwe phakathi kwam intliziyo yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:5">143:5</a> Ndikhumbula imihla yamandulo; Ndicamngca ngemisebenzi yakho yonke, Ndicamngca ngesenzo sezandla zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:6">143:6</a> Ndizolulela kuwe izandla zam, Umphefumlo wam ukungxamele njengelizwe elibharhileyo. (Phakamisani.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:7">143:7</a> Khawuleza undiphendule, Yehova; uyaphela umoya wam. Musa ukubusithelisa kum ubuso bakho, Ndifane nabahla baye emhadini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:8">143:8</a> Ndivise kwakusasa inceba yakho, Ngokuba ndikholose ngawe.  Ndazise indlela endiya kuhamba ngayo: Ngokuba ndiwuphakamisela kuwe umphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:9">143:9</a> Ndihlangule ezintshabeni zam, Yehova. Ndizimela ngawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:10">143:10</a> Ndifundise ukwenza ikholo lakho, ngokuba unguThixo wam.  UMoya wakho olungileyo makandikhaphele ezweni elisithabazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:11">143:11</a> Ngenxa yegama lakho, Yehova, ndiphilise; Wukhuphe embandezelweni umphefumlo wam ngobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:12">143:12</a> Ngenceba yakho zibhangise iintshaba zam, Ubatshabalalise bonke abawubandezelayo umphefumlo wam, Ngokuba ndingumkhonzi wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:1">144:1</a> EkaDavide. Makabongwe uYehova, uliwa lam, Ulofundisa izandla zam ukulwa, Iminwe yam imfazwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:2">144:2</a> Unceba yam, umboniselo yam, Ungxonde yam, umsindisi wam,  mna lo; Ungweletshetshe yam, undizimela ngaye; Ulonyathelela abantu bam phantsi kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:3">144:3</a> Yehova, uyintoni na umntu, le nto umaziyo? Unyana womfo,  le nto umnyamekelayo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:4">144:4</a> Umntu lo ufana nomphunga, Imihla yakhe injengethunzi elidlulayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:5">144:5</a> Yehova, thoba amazulu akho, uhle; Phatha ezintabeni,  ziqhume.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:6">144:6</a> Banekisa imibane, uziphangalalise; Thuma iintolo zakho,  uziduba-dube.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:7">144:7</a> Thuma izandla zakho, zivele phezulu; Ndirhole, ndihlangule emanzini amakhulu. Esandleni soonyana bolunye uhlanga;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:8">144:8</a> Abamlomo uthetha inkohlakalo, Abasandla sokunene sisesokunene sobuxoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:9">144:9</a> Thixo, ndokuvumela ingoma entsha, Ndikubethele umrhubhe ontambo zilishumi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:10">144:10</a> Ulonika ookumkani usindiso, Ulohlangula uDavide umkhonzi wakhe ekreleni elinobubi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:11">144:11</a> Ndirhole, ndihlangule esandleni soonyana bolunye uhlanga,  Abamlomo uthetha inkohlakalo, Abasandla sokunene sisesokunene sobuxoki;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:12">144:12</a> Baze oonyana bethu babe njengezityalo ezikhulileyo ebutsheni babo; Iintombi zethu zibe njengeembombo ezivathisiweyo ngeemfakamfele ngokokwakhiwa kwebhotwe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:13">144:13</a> Oovimba bethu bazale, bavelise iintlobo ngeentlobo;  Iigusha zethu zizale amawaka, zande ngezigidi emaphandleni ethu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:14">144:14</a> Iinkomo zethu zizale, Kungabikho kungenelwa, kungabikho kuthinjwa, Kungabikho kuhlahlamba ezitratweni zethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:15">144:15</a> Hayi, uyolo lwabantu ekunjalo kubo! Hayi, uyolo lwabantu abaThixo unguYehova!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:1">145:1</a> Eyokudumisa kaDavide. Ndiya kukuphakamisa, Thixo wam,  wena Kumkani, Ndilibonge igama lakho ngonaphakade kanaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:2">145:2</a> Imihla yonke ndiya kukubonga, Ndilidumise igama lakho ngonaphakade kanaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:3">145:3</a> Mkhulu uYehova, ngowokudunyiswa kakhulu; Ubukhulu bakhe abunakugocwagocwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:4">145:4</a> Izizukulwana ngezizukulwana, kunconywa izenzo zakho,  Kuxelwe ubugorha bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:5">145:5</a> Bunobungangamela ubuqaqawuli bendili yakho; Ngeendawo zakho ezibalulekileyo ndiya kucamngca.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:6">145:6</a> Bothetha ngamandla ezenzo zakho ezoyikekayo, Ndibalise ngobukhulu bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:7">145:7</a> Bompompoza isikhumbuzo sokulunga kwakho okukhulu,  Bamemelele ngobulungisa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:8">145:8</a> Unobabalo nemfesane uYehova, Uzeka kade umsindo, mkhulu ngenceba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:9">145:9</a> Ulungile uYehova kubo bonke, Imfesane yakhe ikuzo zonke izenzo zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:10">145:10</a> Ziyabulela kuwe, Yehova, zonke izenzo zakho, Bakubonge abakho benceba;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:11">145:11</a> Uzuko lobukumkani bakho balutsho, Bathethe ngobugorha bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:12">145:12</a> Ukuba babazise oonyana babantu ubugorha bakhe,  Ubuqaqawuli obuhle bobukumkani bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:13">145:13</a> Ubukumkani bakho bubukumkani bamaphakade onke, Nolawulo lwakho lukwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:14">145:14</a> UYehova ungumxhasi wabo bonke abawayo, Ngumphakamisi wabo bonke abagobileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:15">145:15</a> Amehlo eento zonke akhangele kuwe, Wena ke uzinika ukudla kwazo ngexesha elililo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:16">145:16</a> Uyasivula isandla sakho, Uzihluthise iinto zonke eziphilileyo ngeento ezikholekileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:17">145:17</a> Ulilungisa uYehova ngeendlela zakhe zonke, Unenceba ngezenzo zakhe zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:18">145:18</a> Usondele uYehova kubo bonke abamnqulayo, Kubo bonke abamnqulayo ngenyaniso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:19">145:19</a> Uyayenza into ekholekileyo kwabamoyikayo, Akuve ukuzibika kwabo, abasindise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:20">145:20</a> UYehova ungumgcini wabo bonke abamthandayo,  Abatshabalalise bonke abangendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:21">145:21</a> Umlomo wam mawuthethe indumiso kaYehova, Inyama yonke ilibonge igama lakhe elingcwele ngonaphakade kanaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:1">146:1</a> Haleluya! Mdumise uYehova, mphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:2">146:2</a> Ndiya kumdumisa uYehova lo gama ndidla ubomi; Ndiya kumbethela uhadi uThixo wam ekubeni ndingosekhoyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:3">146:3</a> Musani ukukholosa ngamanene, Ngonyana womntu, yena ungenalo usindiso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:4">146:4</a> Uyaphuma umoya wakhe, abuyele yena emhlabeni wakhe; Ngaloo mini ayatshitsha amabhongo akhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:5">146:5</a> Hayi, uyolo lwalowo uluncedo lunguThixo kaYakobi, Lwalowo ulinde kuYehova uThixo wakhe:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:6">146:6</a> KuMenzi wezulu nomhlaba, Nolwandle neento zonke ezikulo;  Kulogcina inyaniso ngonaphakade;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:7">146:7</a> Kogweba ityala labacudiswayo; Kopha abalambileyo ukudla;  KuYehova okhulula ababanjwa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:8">146:8</a> KuYehova ovula amehlo eemfama; KuYehova ophakamisa abagobileyo; KuYehova othanda amalungisa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:9">146:9</a> KuYehova ogcina abaphambukeli; Kulophakamisa inkedama nomhlolokazi, Ayiphethule indlela yabangendawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:10">146:10</a> UYehova ungukumkani ngonaphakade, UThixo wakho, Ziyon,  kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana. Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:1">147:1</a> Haleluya! Ngokuba kulungile ukuvuma ngoThixo wethu;  Ngokuba kumnandi, ifanelekile indumiso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:2">147:2</a> Umakhi weYerusalem nguYehova; Abagxothwa bakwaSirayeli ubabuthela khona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:3">147:3</a> Ulophilisa abaphuke intliziyo, Abophe amanxeba abo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:4">147:4</a> Ulobala inani leenkwenkwezi, Ezibiza zonke ngamagama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:5">147:5</a> Inkulu iNkosi yethu, inamandla amakhulu; Ingqondo yayo ayiphele ndawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:6">147:6</a> Ulophakamisa abalulamileyo nguYehova, Uthobela abangendawo emhlabeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:7">147:7</a> Hlabelani kuYehova eyokubulela, Mbetheleni uhadi uThixo wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:8">147:8</a> Ulosibekelisa izulu ngamafu, Ulolungisela umhlaba imvula;  Ulontshulisa utyani ezintabeni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:9">147:9</a> Ulonika inkomo ukudla, Namathole ehlungulu alilayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:10">147:10</a> Akabunanze nganto ubugorha behashe, Akakholiswa zizitho zendoda;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:11">147:11</a> UYehova ukholiswa ngabamoyikayo, Abalinde inceba yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:12">147:12</a> Mncome uYehova, Yerusalem. Mdumise uThixo wakho, Ziyon:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:13">147:13</a> Ngokuba eyomelezile imivalo yamasango akho, Ebasikelele abantwana bakho phakathi kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:14">147:14</a> Ngulomisa uxolo emideni yakho, Wakuhluthisa ngengqolowa etyebileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:15">147:15</a> Ulothumela intetho yakhe ehlabathini, Ilizwi lakhe ligidima ngokukhawuleza;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:16">147:16</a> Ulonika ikhephu njengoboya bezimvu, Ugcwayela iqabaka njengothuthu,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:17">147:17</a> Ephosa umkhenkce wakhe njengamaqhekeza; Ngubani na onokuma phambi kwengqele yakhe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:18">147:18</a> Uthumela ilizwi lakhe, ezo nto azinyibilikise; Uvuthuzisa umoya wakhe, aqukuqele amanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:19">147:19</a> Uloxelela uYakobi ilizwi lakhe, USirayeli imimiselo yakhe namasiko akhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:20">147:20</a> Akenjanga ngalo kolunye uhlanga, Namasiko aluwazi.  Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:1">148:1</a> Haleluya! Dumisani uYehova emazulwini; Mdumiseni ezindaweni eziphezulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:2">148:2</a> Mdumiseni, nonke zithunywa zakhe; Mdumiseni, nonke mikhosi yakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:3">148:3</a> Mdumiseni, wena langa, nawe nyanga; Mdumiseni, nonke zinkwenkwezi zinokukhanya;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:4">148:4</a> Mdumiseni, mazulu awo amazulu, Nani, manzi angaphezu kwezulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:5">148:5</a> Mazilidumise ezo nto igama likaYehova; Ngokuba wawisa umthetho, zadalwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:6">148:6</a> Wazimisa ngonaphakade kanaphakade, Wazimisela ummiselo ezingayi kuwugqitha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:7">148:7</a> Dumisani uYehova ehlabathini, Nina bominenga, nani nonke,  manzi enzonzobila:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:8">148:8</a> Wena mlilo, nawe sichotho; wena khephu, nawe msi; Moya uvuthuzayo, ulenzayo ilizwi lakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:9">148:9</a> Nina zintaba, nani zinduli nonke, Nina mithi eneziqhamo,  nani misedare nonke;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:10">148:10</a> Nina marhamncwa, nani zinkomo nonke, Nina zinambuzane,  nani zintaka zinamaphiko;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:11">148:11</a> Ookumkani behlabathi, nezizwe zonke, Abathetheli nabagwebi behlabathi lonke;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:12">148:12</a> Umlisela kwanomthinjana, Amadoda amakhulu kunye nabafana:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:13">148:13</a> Mabalidumise igama likaYehova, Ngokuba liyingxonde igama lakhe yena yedwa; Indili yakhe ingaphezu komhlaba nezulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:14">148:14</a> Wabaphakamisela abantu bakhe uphondo, Lwayindumiso kwabakhe benceba bonke, Koonyana bakaSirayeli, abantu abasondeleyo kuye. Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:1">149:1</a> Haleluya! Mvumeleni uYehova ingoma entsha, Indumiso yakhe ebandleni labenceba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:2">149:2</a> USirayeli makavuye ngoMenzi wakhe; Usapho lwaseZiyon malugcobe ngoKumkani walo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:3">149:3</a> Mabalidumise igama lakhe beqamba, Bembethela ingqongqo nohadi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:4">149:4</a> Ngokuba uYehova uyakholiswa ngabantu bakhe, Uyabahombisa abalulamileyo ngoloyiso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:5">149:5</a> Mabadlamke benozuko abenceba, Mabamemelele besezililini zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:6">149:6</a> Yimibongo kaThixo emqaleni wabo, Likrele elintlangothi mbini esandleni sabo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:7">149:7</a> Ukuze benze impindezelo ezintlangeni, Izohlwayo ezizweni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:8">149:8</a> Bakhonkxe ookumkani bazo ngemixokelelwane, Nabazukileyo kuzo ngamakhamandela esinyithi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:9">149:9</a> Benze kubo isiko elibhaliweyo. Luzuko olo lwabakhe benceba bonke. Haleluya!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:1">150:1</a> Haleluya! Dumisani uThixo engcweleni yakhe, Mdumiseni esibhakabhakeni samandla akhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:2">150:2</a> Mdumiseni ngenxa yobugorha bakhe, Mdumiseni ngokobuninzi bobukhulu bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:3">150:3</a> Mdumiseni ngokuvuthela isigodlo, Mdumiseni ngomrhubhe nohadi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:4">150:4</a> Mdumiseni ngengqongqo nengqungqo, Mdumiseni ngeento ezineentambo nogwali.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:5">150:5</a> Mdumiseni ngamacangci akhenkcezayo, Mdumiseni ngamacangci adumayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:6">150:6</a> Yonke into ephefumlayo mayimdumise uYehova. Haleluya!</p> 
 <p></p><hr>

 </body>
